
Chapter 1 was a trap.

[All the characters in the book are adults.]

[Feel free to ask any questions, the author will revise.]

[No cuckolding, no cuckolding, no cuckolding, this is really important.]

[Here's an explanation of a misunderstanding caused by later plot points. I swear, I'll write 4000+ words of cuckolding.]

[Except for the male lead, no one else will touch the female lead! There won't be any wardrobe malfunctions!]

[Finally, here's a mental storage space for me.]

[Thank you all for your support, godfathers. *bows*

"Who am I? Where am I? What did I do last night?"

The room was a mess.

The man's shirt was torn into rags, the woman's dress was crumpled and huddled at the foot of the bed, as if it had been brutally abused.

An indescribable, ambiguous scent lingered in the air.

Xia Feng had been awake for a while.

He stood there shirtless, holding Liu Ruyan, who was also completely naked, in his arms, staring blankly at the ceiling.

His mind was a jumbled mess, like a scrambled cassette tape, completely disoriented.

Countless thoughts raced through his head like marbles, making his temples throb.

"Hmm..."

The person in his arms stirred, letting out a soft, kitten-like nasal sound.

Liu Ruyan's smooth, silky body shifted, finding a more comfortable position in his arms, pressing tightly against his chest, before lazily opening her eyes.

Liu Ruyan (Anime Version)

Those eyes, usually carrying a hint of aloofness, were now alluring, watery, and seemed capable of stealing one's soul.

She looked at Xia Feng's somewhat dazed, handsome face and chuckled.

A slender, fair arm reached out and gently rested on his chest, fingertips tracing light circles on his firm, muscular pectoral muscles.

“Are you stunned?”

Liu Ruyan’s voice was hoarse from just waking up, yet held a hint of allure.

“What are you staring at the ceiling for so early in the morning? What, are you unhappy with my performance yesterday?”

Her words instantly snapped Xia Feng back to reality.

He lowered his head, looking at the beautiful face in his arms—a face both familiar and unfamiliar.

Familiar because it was his childhood sweetheart, Liu Ruyan.

Unfamiliar because, before yesterday, they were inseparable, like brothers, but now… what was going on?

Xia Feng’s Adam’s apple bobbed violently, his voice dry and hoarse.

“Ruyan…we…”

He wanted to ask, but didn’t know where to begin.

"Didn't we sign that...that fake marriage agreement?"

"How could we..."

As soon as these words left his mouth, Xia Feng felt utterly unsure of himself.

An agreement?

They'd already slept in the same bed, what kind of agreement was that!

The events of yesterday flashed through his mind like a movie on fast-forward.

Just yesterday morning, this Miss Liu, the famously cold and aloof female CEO of Jiangcheng, stormed into his rented apartment that cost a thousand yuan a month like a gust of wind.

Without a word, she tossed him a contract.

"Marriage Agreement."

Party A: Liu Ruyan.

Party B: —.

The content was shockingly simple and brutal: Xia Feng needed to maintain a three-year marital relationship with Liu Ruyan, a marriage of convenience, publicly appearing as a loving couple, but privately not interfering with each other.

After three years, they would amicably divorce.

As compensation, Liu Ruyan would pay Xia Feng 50,000 yuan per month for living expenses.

Xia Feng was completely stunned.

He and Liu Ruyan were childhood friends, growing up in the same compound, their relationship incredibly close.

But precisely because they were so close, there had never been any romantic feelings between them.

Their interactions were no different from those of two grown men.

They would drink and play games together, and she would often tease him about being a "straight man," saying it was no wonder he couldn't find a girlfriend.

This "good buddy" suddenly wanted to marry him?

"You're paying me to be your husband?"

Xia Feng's first reaction was, "Are you crazy? Has your family pressured you into marriage to this extent?"

Liu Ruyan's face wasn't pleasant at the time, and she said coldly, "Stop talking nonsense, just tell me if you're going to sign or not? Consider it a favor."

What could Xia Feng say?

When a friend is in trouble, you have to be there for them.

Besides, 50,000 yuan a month, no work required, just the title of "married"—where else can you find such a good deal?

So, with a flourish, he signed his name.

Then, the two of them rushed to the Civil Affairs Bureau like they were at a market, and got that blindingly red marriage certificate.

When he came out of the Civil Affairs Bureau with the marriage certificate in his hand, Xia Feng was still completely dazed.

This... he's married?

Before he could even process this fact, Liu Ruyan patted him on the shoulder and boldly suggested, "Come on, getting our marriage certificate is such a big deal, we have to celebrate with a couple of drinks!"

Xia Feng naturally agreed.

The two found a quiet bar that Liu Ruyan frequented; the environment was nice and peaceful.

Then…

Then things started to go wrong.

Xia Feng knew his own alcohol tolerance. He could drink a pound of baijiu with clients and still be able to discuss contracts clearly.

But last night, he drank those fancy cocktails with Liu Ruyan. After only three glasses, he felt dizzy, his head felt like lead, and he couldn't remember much after that.

He only vaguely remembered being helped by Liu Ruyan into a luxury hotel room.

He even thought, "This woman is really kind; she even knew to get me a room."

Then, he took a shower, feeling like a fire was burning inside him, making him parched and uncomfortable.

He thought he could just lie down and sleep it off.

But just as he was about to fall asleep, a warm, soft body pressed against him.

The touch…

The scent…

Boom!

The pent-up lust within him exploded like a bucket of gasoline being poured on it!

Rationality, self-control—all vanished in that instant.

What remained was only the most primal instinct.

When he regained consciousness, this was the situation he was in this morning.

This was definitely a trap!

Most importantly, Xia Feng had a huge question burning in his mind that he had to get off his chest.

He looked at Liu Ruyan, his eyes filled with unbearable complexity.

"Besides... Ruyan, haven't you always liked Lin Yu?"

"We're already like this, what about Lin Yu?"

This question was like a needle piercing Liu Ruyan's heart.

"What did you say?!"

Liu Ruyan, who had just been all smiles, instantly darkened upon hearing Xia Feng's words!

The hand that had been circling his chest suddenly twisted downwards!

"Ouch—"

Xia Feng gasped in pain, feeling as if she had almost pinched off one of his abs.

"You dare mention Lin Yu?!"

Liu Ruyan sat up abruptly from his embrace, the blanket slipping off, revealing a large expanse of her smooth, white skin, but she didn't care.

She glared down at Xia Feng, her eyes seeming to want to skin him alive.

"Xia Feng! You're a block of wood! No, you're a fossil! A fossil from millions of years ago!"

Liu Ruyan's chest heaved with anger as she pointed her finger at Xia Feng's nose and began to berate him.

"Don't you have any idea how I've treated you since we were kids?"

"Who's the first to bring you good food? Who's the first to stand up for you when you're bullied? Who secretly topped up your meal card when you didn't have enough money for university?"

"Haven't I made it obvious enough? Huh?!"

Xia Feng was stunned by her barrage of questions, opening his mouth but unable to utter a single word.

Liu Ruyan's anger flared even more at his oblivious, dumbfounded state.

"It's all because of you, you blockhead! I was desperate, so I came up with this terrible idea of ​​pretending to be interested in Lin Yu! I wanted to see if you'd get jealous, if you'd react at all!"

"And what happened?!"

Liu Ruyan's eyes reddened with anger.

"And you! You actually came over to congratulate us! Saying you wished us a long and happy marriage and many children!?"

"Xia Feng, do you know how I felt? I wanted to strangle you!!"

"And Lin Yu! She was so angry with you she almost laughed herself silly! She said she'd never met such a clueless man in her life!"

Boom!

Every word Liu Ruyan said was like a heavy hammer blow to Xia Feng's heart.

He was completely stunned.

Pretending to like Lin Yu… was it to provoke me?

Lin Yu… was she playing along?

His mind was a complete mess. He stared blankly at the trembling woman before him, unable to utter a single word for a long time.

What could he say?

Could he tell her, "Big sister, it's not that I'm dense, it's because your name is Liu Ruyan!"

He couldn't very well tell her that he'd kept his distance from her since childhood just because of her name, could he? The name "Empress Ruyan" had left a deep psychological scar on his mind from his past life!

That's right, Xia Feng was a transmigrator, reborn into this world with memories of his previous life.

In his previous life, he was just an ordinary office worker, going to get off work and coming home every day, exhausted like a dog, his only entertainment being lying in bed scrolling through short videos.

Back then, a ridiculous short drama called "Stop Torturing the CEO, the Empress Has Returned" was incredibly popular online, constantly being pushed to his feed by algorithms.

The female lead was named Liu Ruyan!

And the plot was extremely melodramatic and addictive.

So, in this life, when he heard that exquisitely beautiful little girl introduce herself in kindergarten, saying, "My name is Liu Ruyan," he was stunned.

From that day on, he labeled that name "Extremely Dangerous, Do Not Approach."

Although, due to various coincidences, they became best friends, and later the two met Lin Yu, the three of them growing up together, he always maintained an insurmountable barrier in his heart.

Dating the Empress Ruyan?

What a joke!

That's like an old man hanging himself—wanting to die!

What if he angered her one day? Would he end up like those cannon fodder characters in the short drama, ruined and destroyed?

So, no matter how good Liu Ruyan was to him, he forced himself to treat her as a buddy, regardless of gender.

When he heard that Liu Ruyan had "liked" Lin Yu, his first reaction wasn't jealousy, but a long sigh of relief!

Great!

This powerful figure is finally taken! He's finally safe!

That's why he went to "bless" them.

Who could have imagined…

This was all a trap!

Thinking this, Xia Feng's gaze towards Liu Ruyan changed.

Seeing Xia Feng's constantly shifting expressions, Liu Ruyan's anger subsided considerably, but her heart began to pound.

Had she… said too harshly?

Scared him? What if he really got angry?

Xia Feng composed himself, looked at Liu Ruyan, and carefully asked one last question.

“Then… the marriage agreement…”

“Fake!”

Liu Ruyan blurted out without thinking.

“Of course it’s fake! It’s just a trick to get you to register the marriage!”

She finished speaking confidently, but seeing Xia Feng’s complicated gaze, her momentum faltered.

She bit her lip, cautiously leaning closer, her large, watery eyes blinking as she looked at him, her voice becoming soft and sweet.

“Um… I… I had no choice but to do it.”

“You… you won’t blame me, will you?”

By the end, her voice was barely a whisper, her fingers nervously gripping the sheets beneath her, like a little girl awaiting judgment.

Looking at her like this, Xia Feng’s chaotic emotions instantly vanished.

Blame her?

What could he blame her for?

For being too beautiful?

Or for setting up such a scheme just to get him?

A female CEO of a multi-billion dollar conglomerate had been devoted to him since childhood, even resorting to such methods to trick him into bed and marriage.

If word got out, wouldn't everyone be incredibly envious?

Why was he being so coy?

Looking at Liu Ruyan's nervous and endearing expression, he suddenly grinned.

To Liu Ruyan's surprise, Xia Feng abruptly reached out and pulled her back into his arms, holding her tightly!

"Ah!"

Liu Ruyan exclaimed, her entire body crashing into his firm chest.

"What...what are you doing?"

"Doing!"



Chapter 2 The Great Love System


It was noon.

Xia Feng glanced at the bright sunlight outside the window, then looked down at the limp Liu Ruyan in his arms, feeling incredibly content.

Liu Ruyan was truly too lazy to move a single finger; she just clung limply to Xia Feng.

"Get up, I'll carry you to take a bath, otherwise you'll feel sticky and uncomfortable."

"Mmm...no...I don't have the strength..." Liu Ruyan whimpered, like a spoiled cat, burying her face in his chest and refusing to move.

Xia Feng chuckled.

"It's alright, I'll help you."

Without waiting for her objection, he easily lifted her up in a princess carry and strode into the bathroom.

In the bathroom, the water was running.

Xia Feng was truly considerate, carefully washing her.

Liu Ruyan kept her eyes closed the entire time, letting him do as he pleased, but her exquisite face remained flushed from head to toe.

This feeling was incredibly embarrassing!

When the two emerged from the bathroom, the hotel staff had already brought two brand-new sets of clothes, complete with everything from underwear to outerwear.

Fortunately, this hotel was a property of the Liu Group; a simple phone call was all it took to have everything prepared.

Xia Feng glanced at them. One set was casual wear for himself, and the other was a standard business suit: a black pencil skirt and a white silk blouse—clearly Liu Ruyan's style.

Xia Feng quickly dressed himself first, then dutifully began helping Liu Ruyan get dressed.

This process presented yet another unique scene.

Although Liu Ruyan had regained some strength, she was still like a puppet, letting Xia Feng help her put on the blouse, button it up, and then slip on the tight-fitting skirt.

By the time everything was finished, it was almost noon.

Liu Ruyan, standing before the mirror, had completely reverted to her aloof, icy CEO persona.

A perfectly tailored business suit accentuated her curvaceous pear-shaped figure, her long, flowing hair cascading down her back. A pair of gold-rimmed glasses adorned her stunningly beautiful face.

Cool, aloof, unapproachable.

A hint of alluring charm in her eyes added a fatal allure.

She tried to take a few steps.

"Hiss..."

Liu Ruyan frowned, her steps faltering slightly, her legs instinctively not quite touching.

Xia Feng quickly stepped forward to support her, both amused and exasperated by her defiant attempt.

"I say, Ruyan, why don't you take the day off and rest at home?"

"Look at you now, you can barely stand, how are you going to go to the company meeting?"

Hearing this, Liu Ruyan looked up and gave Xia Feng a charmingly disdainful eye roll.

"Hmph, isn't it all your fault?"

Her voice wasn't loud, carrying a hint of reproach and complaint, but mostly an undisguised sweetness.

"Like a bull, not to mention last night, and this morning... I really don't know the meaning of 'chivalry'!"

Xia Feng touched his nose and smiled sheepishly.

Well... it was indeed his fault.

He'd gotten carried away, and really hadn't been able to control himself.

"My fault, my fault."

Xia Feng quickly backed down, supporting her waist and softly saying, "Then let's not go to the company, okay?"

"No way!"

Liu Ruyan refused without hesitation.

"There's a very important board meeting this afternoon, I have to attend."

Well, the workaholic is still the same workaholic.

Xia Feng didn't try to persuade her further, and could only dutifully act as her crutch, helping her out of the hotel room.

At the entrance, the hotel manager and a row of waiters stood there respectfully, not daring to breathe.

Seeing the two of them come out, the manager quickly came forward and handed Xia Feng the black car keys.

"Mr. Xia, Ms. Liu, the car is ready."

A waiter had already driven Liu Ruyan's bright red Maserati to the hotel entrance.

Xia Feng carefully helped her into the passenger seat, considerately fastening her seatbelt before walking around to the other side and getting into the driver's seat himself.

He started the engine, shifted gears, and the bright red sports car emitted a deep roar, smoothly merging into traffic.

They drove in silence.

They arrived at the imposing skyscraper of the Liu Group.

Xia Feng parked the car and was about to get out to help her when Liu Ruyan pressed his hand down.

After resting for a while, she felt much better.

"Husband,"

she suddenly called out sweetly.

Xia Feng felt half his bones melt.

"I can go up by myself, you don't need to see me off."

Liu Ruyan unbuckled her seatbelt, turned to look at him, her eyes sparkling.

"Don't you have to go to work too? You can have this car, saves you from squeezing onto the subway."

"Remember, pick me up from get off work tonight."

Xia Feng looked at her sweet, feminine demeanor, his heart warming.

He felt like he was dreaming.

In one day, he not only went from a single guy to a married man, his best buddy became his wife, but even his car upgraded from two legs to a Maserati.

His life had been like a rocket launch!

He hesitated slightly, then tentatively said, "Okay... then... honey, I'm going to work?"

His "honey" sounded a little awkward, a little embarrassed.

But when Liu Ruyan heard it, her eyes instantly curved into two crescent moons.

Her smile was like a blooming rose, so radiant that Xia Feng was stunned.

She suddenly leaned in and planted a quick kiss on Xia Feng's cheek.

Then, before Xia Feng could react, she pushed open the car door, her high heels clicking as she gracefully and calmly walked into the company building, much to the astonishment of the passing employees.

Just before entering, she turned back and blew Xia Feng a seductive kiss.

Xia Feng sat in the car, touching his cheek and grinning foolishly for a while.

He only came to his senses when Liu Ruyan's figure disappeared at the elevator entrance.

Looking at the trident logo on the steering wheel, Xia Feng took a deep breath.

A new life had begun!

He drove his multi-million dollar Maserati towards his small game company.

While waiting at a red light, Xia Feng suddenly remembered something and silently called out in his mind.

"System, are you there?"

[Yes, what are your orders, host?]

A cold, mechanical voice rang directly in his mind.

Holy crap! It really exists!

Xia Feng's heart skipped a beat. He knew the voice he vaguely heard when he woke up this morning wasn't his imagination.

The moment he opened his eyes, this so-called system had bound itself to him.

He composed himself and continued to ask in his mind, "System, what are your functions?"

[This system is called the "Great Love System."]

[The host can earn system points by performing acts of "great love."]

[Points can be used for lotteries, with prizes including money, skills, items, attribute points, and anything else the host desires.]

[The host can try silently reciting "Open Panel" to view their own information.]

The Great Love System?

To embody the spirit of "great love"?

Xia Feng's expression became somewhat strange, but he still did as instructed.

"Open Panel."

Instantly, a blue virtual screen visible only to him appeared before his eyes.

[Host: Xia Feng]

[Age: 26]

[Height: 185cm]

[Strength: 12 (Average for adult males: 10)]

[Constitution: 13 (Average for adult males: 10)]

[Endurance: 15 (Average for adult males: 10)]

[Speed: 11 (Average for adult males: 10)]

[Skills: Basic Game Development, Basic Combat]

[Points: 10]

Looking at his attributes, which were significantly higher than those of an average person, Xia Feng nodded in satisfaction.

It seems that his years of consistent fitness training have been quite effective, especially… this endurance.

Hehe.

Ru Yan should understand this all too well.

His gaze finally settled on the 10 points.

He asked, somewhat puzzled, "System, are these 10 points a newbie bonus?"

【No.】

The system's answer remained cold.

【This system has no newbie bonuses. These 10 points are a reward for the host completing the underlying logic prescribed by the system.】

"..."

Xia Feng's lips twitched.

He understood instantly.

He recalled what had happened between him and Liu Ru Yan from last night to this morning.

So, this so-called "great love" meant this!

Xia Feng's eyes lit up instantly!

So, from now on, as long as he's more affectionate with his wife, he can earn points to draw prizes and become stronger?

Seriously?!

For the sake of points, it seems he'll have to work even harder to embody the spirit of "great love"!

He suppressed his excitement and asked the system, "System, can I draw a prize with 10 points?"

[Yes. 10 points can be used for one beginner-level prize draw. Start now?]

"Draw! Draw now!" Xia Feng thought without hesitation.

[Instruction received. Beginner prize draw roulette wheel is starting...]

Before Xia Feng's eyes appeared a colorful roulette wheel, filled with densely packed squares displaying various prizes.

The roulette wheel spun rapidly, the pointer flashing erratically.

[Start the prize draw!]

The pointer's speed gradually slowed down, finally... coming to rest on one of the gold squares.

[Ding!]

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained...]



Chapter 3 Boss Su Qingxue


[Congratulations, Host! You have received a golden reward: Skill: God-Level Massage]

What the heck?

Xia Feng sat in the driver's seat of the Maserati, staring blankly at the glittering golden words in his mind.

Massage?

God-Level Massage?

Did this system make a mistake?

This thing counts as a "golden reward"?

You might as well just give me ten million in cash!

Xia Feng was about to mentally bombard the system with complaints.

The next second!

Boom—!

A massive flow of information, like a burst dam, surged into his brain!

It gave him absolutely no chance to react!

The human body has 361 regular acupoints and thousands of extra acupoints…

The direction of every muscle, the texture of every fascia…

Pushing, grasping, pressing, rubbing, kneading, pinching, tapping, patting… thousands of massage techniques, and their corresponding effects…

In a mere second, this vast sea of ​​knowledge transformed into an innate instinct within him!

It was as if… he was born to do this!

“Beep beep!”

An impatient horn sounded behind him.

Xia Feng snapped out of his daze and realized the red light had turned green.

He quickly started the car and continued driving smoothly.

While driving, he rapidly processed the extra information in his mind.

Now, he could clearly “see” a complete model of the human body's meridians simply by closing his eyes.

He knew which acupoints to press to refresh the mind, and which meridians to knead to relax muscles and improve circulation.

Even…

The most amazing thing about this skill is that it can stimulate the body's life potential through specific massage techniques, revitalizing the body!

Simply put, it can prolong life and even, to some extent, reverse aging!

This is no massage at all!

“Goodness…”

Xia Feng's Adam's apple bobbed.

“I… misunderstood the system!”

He finally understood; none of the gold rewards were easy!

Then, Liu Ruyan's stunningly beautiful face flashed into Xia Feng's mind, along with her pitiful state that morning, weak and staggering.

A grin spread across his face, and he couldn't help but let out a strange "hehehe" laugh.

“Tonight, I'll give my wife Ruyan a good try with this god-level massage.”

Thinking about the wonderful things that might happen that night, Xia Feng felt a little lightheaded while driving.

Soon, the Maserati stopped in the parking lot downstairs at the company.

This was an impressive 30-story office building, and Xia Feng's company was on the 20th floor.

The company was called "Dream Chaser," which sounded a bit cheesy, but the atmosphere was genuinely great.

The entire company had only about twenty people, all of them Xia Feng and his partners, game fanatics recruited from various places.

This group of people wasn't driven by money or profit, but by a shared dream: to create a truly fun, game-loving domestically produced game that players would rave about!

Xia Feng parked his car and took the elevator to the company.

"Good afternoon, Brother Feng."

"Oh, Brother Feng's here."

"Brother Feng, you've finally arrived! Why are you so late today? Did something happen? Let me know if you need help."

As soon as he entered, a group of young and enthusiastic faces surrounded him, greeting him all at once.

The atmosphere in the company was very relaxed and harmonious, with no airs of superiors and subordinates; everyone seemed more like brothers striving for the same goal.

Xia Feng smiled and greeted them one by one, waving his hand.

"It's nothing, just some personal business. Go ahead and get busy."

With that, he walked through the open-plan office area and went straight to the innermost office.

His office was shared with his boss and partner.

So, as soon as he pushed open the door, he saw a beautiful and alluring figure sitting behind the boss's large desk, engrossed in processing documents.

Hearing the door open, the figure looked up.

Upon recognizing Xia Feng, a teasing smile immediately appeared on her delicate and pretty face.

"Hey, isn't this our company's head manager, Xia?"

"What's this? Getting more and more arrogant, huh? Arriving later than me, the boss? Want me to give you a raise?"

Hearing her familiar teasing, Xia Feng looked helpless.

"Hey Su Qingxue, Boss Su, didn't I call you this morning to ask for leave? I really have something urgent."

The woman in front of him was Xia Feng's college classmate, and also another founder of this "Dream Chaser" company, Su Qingxue.

Su Qingxue

Her long, black hair reached her waist, simply tied into a low ponytail, casually draped over her shoulders, giving her a gentle and refined appearance.

Her features were delicate, her large eyes seemed to speak volumes, lively and mischievous, and when she smiled, a sweet dimple appeared on her cheek.

But completely incongruous with her pure and sweet face was her ridiculously voluptuous figure!

At this moment, she was just sitting there casually.

The blue dress, clearly altered to be larger, was still stretched taut by her.

It was so voluminous that she had to rest it on the edge of her desk while seated!

The image was incredibly striking!

Her lower body featured a pair of long, shapely legs encased in black stockings.

Xia Feng's gaze was irresistibly drawn to them.

Su Qingxue seemed completely oblivious to his gaze, casually crossing her legs, shifting to a more comfortable position.

The perfect curves of her legs, encased in black stockings, reflected an alluring sheen under the light.

Instantly, she became even more captivating.

Su Qingxue crossed her arms.

She raised an eyebrow, a half-smile playing on her lips, as she looked at Xia Feng.

"Hmph, not even a decent reason, just a 'I had something to do this morning' to brush me off?"

Her voice was sweet, but her words carried a sharp edge.

"Looks like our Manager Xia has gotten too big for her britches. She doesn't respect me, her little boss, and is planning to abandon our little company and start her own business?"

That's quite a accusation.

Xia Feng was at his wit's end. Dealing with Su Qingxue head-on was absolutely useless; he had to use a softer approach.

He could only smile helplessly, walk around the desk, and go behind her.

Then, he gently placed his hands on her thin but warm shoulders, kneading them lightly.

"My fault, my fault, Boss Qingxue, please forgive me this time."

He said in a fawning tone as he kneaded.

"I promise, next time I'll give you a complete report! I really had a huge emergency that kept me up today!"

Xia Feng instinctively used the [God-Level Massage] he had just acquired.

Su Qingxue was about to retort, and had already opened her mouth.

But the instant Xia Feng began the massage!

Su Qingxue's mind went blank!

What was this feeling?

It felt like countless tiny ants were crawling inside her bones, or like she was soaking in warm water, so comfortable she wanted to moan!

Her sweet face flushed crimson, two intoxicating blushes spreading all the way to her ears.

Startled, she quickly raised her hands, covering her mouth tightly, afraid of making any more embarrassing noises.

And Xia Feng?

He saw Su Qingxue suddenly fall silent, her shoulders trembling slightly.

He assumed his flattery had worked, and the beautiful boss had finally calmed down.

Hmm, it seems this tactic worked!

So, Xia Feng put in even more effort!

His fingers precisely located several acupoints on her shoulders, stiffened from long hours of desk work.

A series of fluid movements followed.

Finally, Xia Feng felt it was enough and slowly withdrew his hands.

"How was it, Boss Qingxue? Are you calm now?"

He asked with a smile.

But when he looked down, he discovered…

Goodness, this effect… wasn't it a bit too strong?!



Chapter 4 Unexpected News


Xia Feng's heart pounded as he looked at Su Qingxue's vividly "miserable" state.

He dared not look at her again.

If he kept looking, he might end up saluting her.

Don't look at what you shouldn't look at! Don't look at what you shouldn't look at!

Xia Feng silently chanted to himself, then quickly slipped back to his seat as if fleeing.

He pretended nothing had happened, turned on his computer, and opened a work file, but his eyes kept darting out of the corner of his eye to see what was happening across the desk.

His heart was pounding.

Was this "divine massage" a little too intense?

He just wanted to calm her down, he didn't mean to make her collapse!

After a while, Su Qingxue, who was slumped over the desk, finally recovered.

The feeling that had made her weak and her scalp tingle slowly subsided, replaced by an unprecedented sense of comfort and relaxation, as if all the fatigue of the past few days had been swept away.

But immediately afterward, an overwhelming sense of shame and indignation surged within her!

She had actually… she had actually let him press her down a few times, and yet she had made that shameful sound and acted that way!

Su Qingxue slowly sat up straight, tidied her slightly disheveled clothes and hair, then raised her head, glaring fiercely at Xia Feng with eyes full of shame and anger.

The meaning in her eyes was clear: You bastard! You wait! This isn't over!

Xia Feng keenly caught this "glare attack."

What could he do?

He could only pretend to be blind.

He lowered his head even further, his fingers clattering on the keyboard, feigning innocence, as if to say, "I'm busy, I don't know anything, I didn't see anything."

An eerie silence descended upon the office.

A lingering ambiguity and awkwardness seemed to hang in the air.

This silence lasted for quite some time.

Finally, Su Qingxue couldn't hold back any longer.

She cleared her throat, trying to make her voice sound normal, but the slight tremor at the end betrayed her inner turmoil.

"Xia Feng."

"Hmm?"

Xia Feng looked up, staring at her blankly.

"What...what did you do this morning?"

Su Qingxue was genuinely curious.

She and Xia Feng had known each other since university, almost ten years of friendship, making them one of the people who understood each other best.

She knew how reliable and responsible Xia Feng was.

Since they founded this company together, Xia Feng had never been late or left early, let alone taken leave.

Today was the first time ever.

This made her feel uneasy.

Hearing Su Qingxue's question, Xia Feng didn't think too much about it. After all, their relationship was so close, there was no point in hiding it.

He scratched his head and answered casually,

"Oh, that... I got married yesterday."

He spoke so lightly, as if he were saying, "I had hot pot yesterday."

"So this morning... well, I had some things to prepare, so I had to take the day off."

Xia Feng dared not tell the truth.

He couldn't very well tell her that he'd gotten so carried away with the experience that he and his wife had been so lovey-dovey in the hotel that he hadn't gotten out of bed until late morning, could he?

If he said that aloud, he was sure Su Qingxue would grab a keyboard and slap him across the face.

"Oh, so you got married..."

Su Qingxue didn't react at first, nodding subconsciously.

But the next second, her brain finally processed what Xia Feng had just said.

Married?!

"Huh?!"

A sharp exclamation uncontrollably escaped her lips!

The sound was so loud it startled Xia Feng.

He looked at Su Qingxue with a bewildered expression.

"What's wrong? Why are you reacting so strongly? It's just a marriage."

Su Qingxue felt as if an invisible hand was gripping her heart tightly, making it difficult to breathe.

"How...how did you suddenly get married?!"

Her voice was almost incoherent.

"How come I haven't heard a single word from you?!"

"And...and didn't you always say you didn't have a girlfriend?! How...how could you suddenly be at the point of marriage?!"

A barrage of questions rained down on her like a machine gun.

Her eyes were filled with shock, confusion, accusation, panic, and bewilderment.

Xia Feng was stunned by her intense reaction.

What could he say?

Should he tell her that the truth was, he had originally signed an agreement to be a fake husband, but his cunning childhood sweetheart had tricked him, and he had unwittingly fallen for her, leading to a real marriage?

That was too far-fetched; no one would believe him!

He could only bite the bullet and fabricate a half-truth, half-lie story.

"Well... well..."

He organized his thoughts, trying to make it sound plausible.

"It's about my childhood sweetheart, Liu Ruyan, you know her."

"I always thought of her as just a buddy, but... but yesterday she suddenly confessed to me."

"And then... I thought about it carefully, and it seemed kind of okay? So... I agreed."

"And then... she just dragged me to the Civil Affairs Bureau and we got our marriage certificate..."

Xia Feng felt a little guilty at the end, and could only manage a couple of dry laughs.

"Haha, even I think this development... was a little too fast."

After he finished speaking, the office fell silent again.

Su Qingxue just stared at him, unable to say a word.

Her lips trembled slightly, and her eyes unconsciously welled up with tears.

She blinked hard, trying to force back that damned mist.

Why...

Why did this happen?

The secret she'd kept hidden in her heart for so many years, the relationship she'd carefully guarded for so long…

Just like that, suddenly, it was a death sentence?

She thought they had so much time left.

She thought that as long as she stayed by his side, supported him in his business, and stood by him until he succeeded, one day he would turn around and see her.

But now… he's married.

To another woman.

This fact, like the sharpest knife, pierced her heart, the pain almost suffocating her.

But she couldn't cry.

At least, not in front of him.

She was his best friend, his most trusted partner.

She had her pride.

After a long while, she took a deep breath and forced a smile that was more painful than tears.

"Is that so..."

Her voice was hoarse.

"Then...then I wish you...a happy and fulfilling married life."

Every word seemed to be squeezed out from between her teeth, exhausting all her strength.

She slowly sat back down, then turned back to her computer screen.

She looked as if she was about to immediately immerse herself in her work, using endless tasks to numb her senses and distract herself.

Xia Feng, seeing this, also turned around and continued working on his project.

The office was filled only with the crisp sound of keyboard clicks, but the oppressive, suffocating atmosphere lingered.

Time ticked by.

Soon, it was six o'clock in the evening, time to leave work.

Xia Feng shut down his computer, packed his things, and got up to go to Su Qingxue's side.

"Qingxue, I'm leaving now."

"Mm."

Su Qingxue didn't even look up, only uttering a single syllable through her nose.

She remained glued to the screen, clearly intending to work overtime.

Su Qingxue was a workaholic; working overtime was commonplace for her.

After greeting her and receiving her response, he was already thinking about picking up his newlywed wife.

He turned, pushed open the door, and left.

The office door closed softly.

A click.

That sound was like the last straw that broke the camel's back.

The moment she was left alone in the office,

Su Qingxue's taut shoulders finally collapsed.

She couldn't hold on any longer.

She reached out her trembling hands, covered her face, and buried her head deeply in her arms.

The tears she had suppressed all afternoon finally burst forth.

"Waaah...waaah..."

The suppressed sobs echoed in the empty office.

Liu Ruyan walked slowly into the CEO's office on the top floor.

Her face maintained the aloofness of an icy female CEO, but only she knew that every step she took felt strange.

That man was too...too much!

But the next second, the slight pain on her face vanished instantly, replaced by a silly, irrepressible, sweet smile.

What was this small price to pay?

This was the best proof that she, Liu Ruyan, had given herself completely to the man she had loved for over twenty years!

Her voice was filled with unwavering determination.

"If they think those men are so great, why don't they marry them themselves? Why are they bothering me every day!"

"Okay, as expected of the CEO Liu I know. Since you have an idea, go for it! I'll always be your strongest support.

If you really can't handle it, come find me. I can even get my dad to step in and keep things under control."

"Haha, no need to thank me, we're practically family! Alright, I won't disturb your honeymoon anymore, bye-bye, wishing you happiness and a baby soon!"

She looked at the ceiling, murmuring to herself, "Ruyan, that girl, is finally with the person she loves. Where is my...him?"

She sent a message to Lin Yu, her "good friend" who was still covering for her overseas.

"Little Fish, I've made it ashore!"

Followed by a triumphant peace sign emoji.

She knew it was probably past midnight there, and Lin Yu was likely still asleep, so she didn't expect an immediate reply.

Having done all this, Liu Ruyan finally put her phone away, satisfied.

Alright, time to get back to work.

The financial statements and project plans that usually captivated her, making her completely absorbed, seemed like gibberish to her today; she couldn't understand a single word.

Her mind kept replaying the images of her and Xia Feng that morning.

His domineering manner, his gentle manner, the way he held her…

Thinking about it, her face flushed again.

She spent more time checking her watch than reading the documents.

"It's only 3:00...time is crawling..."

Ten minutes passed.

"It's only 3:10...why aren't we off work yet..."

Another half hour passed.

"It's not even 4:00 yet...I'm going crazy..."

She felt like a lovesick teenager after a first date, anxiously awaiting her boyfriend's return, restless and anxious.

She wished she had superpowers to fast-forward time to 6:00 PM!

In this bittersweet state, Liu Ruyan finally made it to the end of the workday.

Just after six o'clock, she began frantically packing her things, organizing her files, and placing her bag in the most convenient spot, waiting for Xia Feng's call.

Another half hour passed.

Buzz—

Her phone finally vibrated!

Liu Ruyan felt her heart skip a beat, and she frantically grabbed her phone.

On the screen, a contact saved as "My Darling Husband" had sent a message.

[Wife, I'm downstairs at the company. When are you getting off work?]

Liu Ruyan couldn't suppress her smile!

She quickly typed on the screen.

[Coming down now! Wait for me!]

After sending the message, she grabbed her already packed bag and rushed out of the office like a whirlwind.

However, because the movement was so sudden, she aggravated a wound on her body that hadn't fully healed.

"Hiss—"

She gasped in pain, staggering slightly.

But this minor pain couldn't stop her from running towards her beloved.

Ignoring the discomfort, she practically jogged towards the CEO's private elevator.

Soon, the elevator reached the lobby.

Liu Ruyan immediately spotted the familiar scene outside.

Her bright red Maserati was parked quietly in a parking space not far from the company entrance.

A tall, handsome man, dressed casually, leaned lazily against the car door, one hand in his pocket, looking down at his phone, seemingly waiting for someone.

The evening glow bathed his profile, casting a golden hue on his features, making him breathtakingly handsome.

At that moment, Liu Ruyan felt the whole world light up.

Her smile was like a blooming rose, radiant beyond compare.

She strode over in her high heels, her voice brimming with undisguised joy and excitement.

Chapter 6 The Clingy Liu Ruyan


Xia Feng was leaning against the car door, idly scrolling through short videos.

The various catchy tunes and hilarious clips failed to pique his interest in the slightest.

"Honey!"

Her usually icy, beautiful face was now adorned with a radiant smile.

Xia Feng drove without looking at her, but his words were as sweet as honey.

"Hehe, me too."

The two chatted sweet nothings for a while, exchanging meaningless words.

It's my fault, all my fault."

Treatment?

Upon hearing those two words, Liu Ruyan's mind instantly went astray.

Does that mean...she needs to apply medicine?

Her husband personally...applying medicine for her?

Thinking of certain indescribable scenes, her face flushed red, like a ripe apple, but her heart was also filled with a certain anticipation.

Xia Feng told Liu Ruyan, the "injured party," to stay in the car, and he rushed upstairs.

It was an upscale, wealthy neighborhood in a prime location in Jiangcheng, filled with detached villas and extremely tight security.

The entire villa was decorated in a European style, understated yet luxurious, exquisitely refined.

Xia Feng smiled helplessly, then easily lifted her up in a princess carry and strode towards the bathroom.

Huh?

Wasn't this supposed to be treatment?

Wasn't it supposed to be applying medicine?

Tomatoes, eggs, a bunch of greens, and a piece of pork tenderloin.

Washing vegetables, chopping vegetables, beating eggs…

What high-ranking officials, what wealthy tycoons, wouldn't they all obediently line up to give him money?
