Her voice was soft, tinged with a satisfied sigh.

"Coming home from get off work every day, seeing you, eating your cooking, watching TV with you..."

"It's all your fault, you blockhead! If only you had realized it sooner, I wouldn't have had to wait so many years!"

Xia Feng gently encircled her slender waist with one hand, and affectionately stroked her long hair with the other.

"Yes, yes, it's my fault, my problem. I'm sorry to have kept you waiting."

The two of them nestled together quietly, enjoying this hard-won moment of warmth.

Neither of them paid attention to what was playing on TV.

Time quickly passed to 10:30 PM.

It was time to sleep.

They turned off the TV and went back to their room hand in hand.

He closed the door and drew the curtains.

Next, Xia Feng began his arduous struggle once again for those precious system points.

…………………………

The next morning.

Liu Ruyan didn't go to work.

It wasn't that she didn't want to go; she simply couldn't get up.

Xia Feng had thoroughly exhausted his terrifying stamina of 15 points last night.

Now, Liu Ruyan didn't even have the strength to open her eyes, let alone move; she just wanted to continue sleeping.

Xia Feng looked at Liu Ruyan, who was lying on the bed like a corpse, and found it somewhat amusing.

He leaned down and kissed her smooth forehead, then went to the kitchen to prepare enough breakfast and lunch for her for the day, placing them in a thermal container.

Before leaving, he whispered to Liu Ruyan,

"Wife, I've put the food on the table. Remember to eat on time when you wake up, no skipping meals, understand?"

After saying that, he changed his clothes and went to work, looking refreshed.

A while after Xia Feng left,

Liu Ruyan on the bed finally managed to open one eye a crack.

Her face was filled with lingering fear and relief.

She reached for her phone on the bedside table, her fingers trembling, and dialed her best friend Chen Mi's number.

The call was quickly answered.

Chen Mi's signature lazy voice, tinged with morning grumpiness, came through the phone.

"Liu Ruyan! You'd better have something really serious to tell me! Calling me this early in the morning, are you trying to kill me?!"

Liu Ruyan had no time to pay attention to Chen Mi's complaints.

She spoke weakly, directly throwing out the question that had been nagging at her all night, filling her with extreme fear.

"Mimi... I have a question for you... You know... you know, how long does it usually last when men do 'that' again?"

Chen Mi on the other end of the phone was stunned.

She had no idea!

As a lifelong single woman, all her knowledge came from the internet!

She thought for a moment and could only answer uncertainly.

"The internet says... usually around... ten minutes, right? What's wrong? Why are you asking this?"

Hearing this answer, Liu Ruyan's voice trembled with fear, filled with lingering dread.

"Then why... why last night... all night long?!"

"I feel like I'm going to die! Really!!"

Her legs trembled uncontrollably at the thought of Xia Feng's performance last night.

Chen Mi was stunned by her words.

One whole night?!

She was silent for a full five seconds before speaking in an extremely strange tone:

"No... buddy, you called first thing this morning just to brag about this?"

"I thought your house was on fire! Damn!"

"No! I wasn't bragging!"

Liu Ruyan knew her best friend had misunderstood and hurriedly explained.

Liu Ruyan said, on the verge of tears.

"It's just... it's just that I can't move at all right now, my bones feel like they're falling apart, I can't even go to the office. It's terrifying, what should I do, Mimi? If it's like this every day, I'll really die!"

Chen Mi was speechless.

What else could she do?

"When he wants to, just don't give in, okay?"

"No way!"

Liu Ruyan refused without even thinking.

"What if he thinks I'm a downer and starts to dislike me?!"

"..."

Chen Mi was completely at a loss. She could only shrug and say half-jokingly,

"Then there's nothing you can do. Unless... unless you're generous and let him find someone else to help you share the burden. But I think you definitely wouldn't accept that, right?"

Chen Mi was just saying it casually, to tease Liu Ruyan about her contradictory feelings of wanting something but not being able to have it.

However...

Upon hearing this, Liu Ruyan's eyes lit up, as if a whole new world had opened up for her!

That's it!

Just find another one!

That way, she can satisfy her husband's needs without exhausting herself!

It's a brilliant, win-win plan!

"Yes! Mimi! You're so smart! Just find another one!"

"Thank you, Mimi! I love you to death!"

With that, Liu Ruyan, as if she had solved a monumental problem, slammed the phone down.

Leaving Chen Mi, still holding the phone, completely bewildered.

"Wait...huh? She...she really intends to make him find another one?!"

Chen Mi got out of bed, walked to the window, and pulled back the curtains to look at the sun outside.

"The sun...didn't rise in the west..."

Because of Liu Ruyan's astonishingly bizarre thought process, Chen Mi was completely plunged into deep self-doubt.



Chapter 9 The haggard Su Qingxue


Xia Feng had no idea that his wife was already plotting a bizarre plan to find him another "sister" to share the workload.

He was currently driving his flashy red Maserati, in a cheerful mood, to the parking lot downstairs at the company.

He had just found a parking spot and parked the car.

"Hey, Feng-ge!"

A familiar greeting came from the side.

Two male colleagues who were usually on good terms with him happened to be passing by. When they saw Xia Feng get out of the driver's seat of the flashy Maserati, their eyes widened.

"Wow! Feng-ge, when did you... strike it rich? This car must be worth millions!"

One of the colleagues circled the car, clicking his tongue in amazement.

The other also came over and nudged Xia Feng with his elbow.

"Not bad, Feng-ge, you've been keeping it a secret! But... isn't this color a bit too much for you? It's too flashy!"

Xia Feng locked the car and waved with a smile.

"Oh, this isn't mine."

"It's my wife's. I just borrowed it for a few days."

He said it casually.

???

Three big question marks simultaneously appeared above the heads of the two colleagues.

They looked at each other, their expressions incredibly varied.

Wife?

What nonsense are you talking about, Feng?!

When did you get married?

Last week, at the company dinner, weren't you hugging a bottle and crying with us about being an unwanted single dog?

It's only been a few days?!

Less than a week!

And...you're married?!

That speed, did you take a rocket or just teleport?!

Suddenly, as if they'd realized something, they looked at each other, both seeing a hint of fear and pity in each other's eyes.

Then...what about Boss Su?

Su Qingxue's crush on Xia Feng was no secret within the company.

Her undisguised care and special treatment were obvious to anyone with eyes.

Except for Xia Feng himself, of course.

Seeing the two suddenly fall silent, their expressions turning strange, Xia Feng asked curiously,

"What's wrong with you two? Why do you look so odd?"

"N-nothing! Nothing!"

The two snapped out of their daze, quickly waving their hands, forcing smiles that looked more like grimaces.

"It's just...it's just a bit too sudden. Brother Feng, you've kept this a secret incredibly well! There wasn't a single whisper of it before!"

"Oh, that."

Xia Feng scratched his head, thought for a moment, and decided to give a reasonable explanation.

"Well... it's just... fate brought them together.

They happened to like each other a lot, and then because of some things, they naturally got married.

I think... it's pretty good."

The two men listened to his casual explanation, their expressions becoming even stranger.

Fate?

Dude, your fate came way too fast!

But they didn't dare ask any more questions, only managing a few dry "Congratulations," before the three of them silently entered the elevator.

They arrived at the office area on the twentieth floor.

The two colleagues, as soon as they were out of Xia Feng's sight, huddled together, whispering like two groundhogs who had discovered a bombshell.

"Big news! Big news! Feng-ge got married!"

"What?! Really?!"

"Really! He said it himself! He even drove his wife's Maserati today!"

"Holy crap! No wonder Boss Su was like a lost soul yesterday!"

"It's over... Boss Su's hope is completely gone now..."

Instantly, an atmosphere of gossip and sighs filled the entire office area.

Everyone felt sorry for their excellent and devoted female boss.

Only Xia Feng, the stereotypical straight man, remained completely unaware.

He walked straight to the innermost office.

As soon as he pushed open the door, he saw Su Qingxue.

She was already sitting behind her desk, working.

But Xia Feng only glanced at her before his brows furrowed deeply.

Su Qingxue looked terrible today.

Her usually radiant face was now haggard, with dark circles under her eyes and bloodless lips.

Even her usually meticulously styled, smooth hair looked disheveled and dry.

She exuded a low, menacing aura, as if to say, "I'm exhausted, don't mess with me."

But even so, her stunning beauty remained undeniable.

Instead, it possessed a fragile, heartbreaking beauty.

Xia Feng quickly walked over.

"Qingxue, what's wrong? You look terrible. Didn't you sleep last night?"

His tone was full of concern and a hint of reproach.

Su Qingxue seemed not to hear him enter, her eyes fixed on the computer screen, replying without looking up.

"It's nothing, just a little insomnia. I still have some work to do, almost finished, I'll rest after I'm done."

Her voice was hoarse, filled with exhaustion.

Hearing this, Xia Feng's brows furrowed even more.

Still working?

You're going to die from exhaustion if you keep going like this!

Without a word, he went around behind his desk, giving Su Qingxue no chance to react, and scooped her up from her office chair!

A perfect princess carry!

"Ah!"

Su Qingxue was startled by the sudden weightlessness, instinctively reaching out to tightly wrap her arms around Xia Feng's neck.

When she came to her senses, her pretty face instantly flushed red!

"Xia Feng! What are you doing! Put me down!"

She struggled, both embarrassed and angry.

Xia Feng, however, held her even tighter, his tone leaving no room for argument.

"No! You have to go to sleep right now!"

"If you don't get a proper rest today, you can forget about doing this job!"

"Unless you fire me right now!"

With that, he picked up Su Qingxue and strode towards the small cubicle in the office that served as a makeshift rest area.

How could Su Qingxue possibly fire him for something like this?

She struggled a couple of times, but found she couldn't break free from the man's strong arms, so she gave up resisting and let him hold her.

Held so possessively in her arms, feeling the warmth of his chest and his familiar scent, a sweet feeling uncontrollably welled up in Su Qingxue's heart.

It had been… a long time since he had held her like this.

But that sweetness instantly transformed into boundless bitterness.

She remembered.

This embrace no longer belonged to her.

He… was someone else's husband.

Xia Feng carried her into a small cubicle.

Inside was a small but soft bed, usually used for them to take a nap when they were tired from working overtime.

He carefully placed Su Qingxue on the bed and even gently removed her high heels.

Looking at her pale and haggard face, etched with extreme fatigue, Xia Feng felt a pang of sadness.

He knew Su Qingxue was just like that—when she worked, she worked herself to the bone.

He sighed, walked to the bedside, and gently placed his hand on her temples.

"Close your eyes, let me massage your head and help you relax."

Su Qingxue wanted to say something.

But when Xia Feng's warm, large hands began to gently massage her head,

a warm and comfortable sensation instantly spread from her scalp throughout her body.

That feeling…it was so comfortable…

It was as if all her restlessness, all her fatigue, was being soothed and dissipated little by little under his magical massage.

She could no longer resist the overwhelming wave of drowsiness.

Her eyelids grew heavier and heavier…

She soon fell asleep.

Her breathing gradually became even and long.

Xia Feng looked at her sleeping face without stopping.

He continued to use his divine massage techniques to help her regulate her blood and energy, which had become disordered due to staying up late and poor emotional state.

Under his treatment, Su Qingxue's pale complexion gradually regained its rosy hue.

Only after confirming that her problem was basically resolved and her condition had stabilized did Xia Feng gently withdraw his hand.

He covered her with a blanket, then quietly left the cubicle and returned to his workstation to continue working.

...

When Su Qingxue woke up again, she was awakened by the blinding sunlight streaming in through the window.

She opened her eyes groggily, momentarily disoriented.

She felt as if she had had a very long dream.

In the dream, something warm seemed to be comforting her.

She glanced at her phone.

It was already noon.

She had slept the entire morning?

And this sleep had been sweeter and more restful than ever before!

Upon waking, she felt not the dizziness she had felt before, but rather refreshed and full of energy!

She knew it was all Xia Feng's doing.

That man…

He's always like this…

He always appears when she needs him most, caring for her and looking after her in his domineering yet gentle way…

He's so good to her, so considerate…

But why… doesn't he understand her feelings?

Su Qingxue didn't get up.

She lay quietly on the bed, raising one hand to shield her eyes.

Her other hand was pressed tightly against her chest.

It ached faintly there because of that man.

After a long while, she let out a barely audible sigh.

"How can I let you go like this..."

"You bastard..."



Chapter 10: If you swing the hoe well, there's nothing you can't dig down...


After Xia Feng settled Su Qingxue in,

he returned to his seat and let out a long sigh of relief.

He was in for a lot of work.

The game his team had poured their hearts and souls into developing for over a year was about to enter its final internal testing phase.

This was a crucial step that would determine the company's fate; it couldn't be taken lightly.

Just as he was about to dive into his work, a thought struck him, and he opened the system panel.

[Points: 20]

Looking at the newly added 20 points, Xia Feng's expression was somewhat complicated.

This was all the result of his hard work last night!

"Sigh..."

He couldn't help but sigh inwardly.

"Looks like I got a little too carried away yesterday; I exhausted Ruyan."

He had already discovered last night that his stamina was 15, while Liu Ruyan's physical abilities were probably only at the average level, at most an 8 or 9.

This was a complete dimensional advantage.

"No, I'll have to take it easy tonight. I'll just hold her while she sleeps, let her rest and recover."

Xia Feng made up his mind.

Then, looking at the 20 points, his heart started itching again.

"System, draw a prize!"

[Instruction received, initiating beginner prize draw x2...]

The familiar and cool roulette wheel reappeared, spinning rapidly.

[Ding!]

[Congratulations, host, you have drawn 1 [Attribute Point]!]

[Ding!]

[Congratulations, host, you have drawn 3 [Attribute Points]!]

The roulette wheel disappeared.

Xia Feng stared dumbfounded at the lone 4 extra attribute points on the panel.

"..."

Silence.

Dead silence.

A few seconds later, Xia Feng roared inwardly.

"System! Did you steal my points?! Huh?!"

"Two draws, and this is what I get?! What happened to the promised gold reward?!"

[Host, please calm down. Don't slander this system's reputation out of thin air.]

The system's voice remained cold and emotionless.

[The appearance of a gold reward is an extremely low-probability event.

Yesterday, on your first draw, the system automatically triggered the "Newbie Luck" bonus, thus increasing your chances of winning.]

Xia Feng's lips twitched.

Good grief, there's a newbie protection period?

But those 20 points were earned through his and his wife Ruyan's hard work and sweat!

And those two boxes that bravely perished…

And all they got in return was a paltry 4 attribute points?

This is outrageous!

[If the host wants to obtain better items, they can accumulate points for higher-level draws.]

The chance of obtaining rare rewards in the advanced lottery is greatly increased.

"Oh?"

Xia Feng became interested. "Then how many points are needed for each intermediate and advanced lottery draw?"

[Intermediate lottery: 100 points/draw.]

[Advanced lottery: 1000 points/draw.]

[Top-tier lottery: 10000 points/draw.]

"..."

Xia Feng almost spat out blood after hearing this price.

"Are you trying to kill me?!"

[The host can also increase the number of "confidantes" to accelerate the point acquisition speed.]

???

Countless question marks instantly appeared above Xia Feng's head.

Increase the number of confidantes?

"Isn't this just letting him go out and mess around?!"

The next second, Xia Feng righteously refused in his mind.

"Impossible! Absolutely impossible!"

"I, Xia Feng, a dignified and upright man of unparalleled integrity! Even if I jumped from this twentieth floor and died outside, I would never do anything to betray my wife!"

"This matter is not to be mentioned again!"

Xia Feng stated his position resolutely.

He was too lazy to care about that unreliable system anymore.

He couldn't decide where to allocate those 4 attribute points for the time being, so he'd just leave them for now.

He closed the panel and threw himself back into his busy work.

...

Time passed quickly.

Before he knew it, it was noon, lunch break time.

Xia Feng stretched, feeling a little hungry.

He glanced towards the cubicle and noticed that Su Qingxue hadn't gotten up yet.

She'd slept all morning; hadn't she had enough rest?

A little worried, he got up and went over.

He gently pushed open the door to the cubicle.

He saw Su Qingxue still lying on the bed, in a similar position to when he left, but her movements made his heart skip a beat.

She was shielding her eyes with one hand and pressing the other tightly against her chest.

She looked as if she was in extreme discomfort.

Xia Feng's expression instantly changed.

He thought something was wrong with her.

He quickly went over and carefully helped her up from the bed, supporting her against the wall.

"Qingxue, what's wrong? Are you feeling unwell?"

His tone was full of anxiety and concern.

"I'll take you to the hospital this afternoon!"

[Divine Massage] is, after all, just massage, not [Divine Medical Skill]. If there's something seriously wrong, massage alone won't cure it; you'll need to see a professional doctor.

Hearing Xia Feng's anxious and concerned words, feeling the warmth from his arm...

Su Qingxue's heart ached even more.

But at the same time, a strange thought uncontrollably surfaced.

"As long as you swing the hoe well, there's nothing you can't dig up..."

But she immediately shook her head vigorously, banishing this dangerous thought.

No...

That won't do...

She took a deep breath, stood up from the bed, and gave Xia Feng a somewhat forced smile.

"I'm fine, just a little groggy from just waking up."

"Thank you, Xia Feng.

I feel much better now."

"That's good."

Xia Feng was still worried.

"But I think it's better to go to the hospital for a check-up this afternoon."

"No need!"

Su Qingxue's tone became firm.

"I'm fine now, just hungry and want to eat. Let's go eat, it's my treat."

Seeing her resolute attitude, Xia Feng didn't say anything more.

He could only nod and follow her out of the office.

The two went to their usual lunch spot downstairs from the company and ordered a couple of simple dishes.

While waiting for their food, Su Qingxue casually brought up Liu Ruyan.

"Xia Feng, the wife you're talking about... is Liu Ruyan, right?"

"Is that...the stunning beauty who used to come visit you all the time in college?"

Xia Feng nodded, a smile appearing on his face.

"Yes, that's her. Actually, we've known each other since kindergarten."

"And Lin Yu, you know him too, the good buddy who used to play basketball with me all the time. The three of us practically grew up together."

Xia Feng's tone carried a hint of wistfulness and emotion.

"To be honest, I never imagined that Ru Yan had liked me since childhood."

"I'm a bit oblivious, I always thought of her as just a buddy. Then for a while, I even thought she was dating that Lin Yu guy."

"Turns out, it was all a charade she put on to provoke me."

"But thankfully, we ended up together, so it's a happy ending."

He was filled with emotion.

Meanwhile, sitting opposite him, Su Qingxue listened to Xia Feng recount his past with his wife, feeling utterly disappointed in him!

She desperately wanted to travel back in time, grab herself by the neck, and ask:

Su Qingxue, Su Qingxue! Why were you so hesitant and cowardly back then?!

If you had been braver then, just go for it! Would you be experiencing all this now, enjoying Xia Feng's doting affection?!

If Liu Ruyan could do it, why can't you?!

After Xia Feng finished speaking, seeing Su Qingxue lower her head and remain silent, just poking at the rice in her bowl with her chopsticks, he assumed she was lost in thought and didn't say anything more.

Soon, the dishes arrived.

Lunch was finished in a somewhat silent atmosphere.

The two returned to the company and continued their afternoon work.

…

Time passed by.

Soon it was time to leave work.

Xia Feng thought that Liu Ruyan must have been exhausted yesterday and probably wouldn't have much of an appetite today.

He planned to go to a nearby traditional Chinese medicine shop to buy some angelica root and goji berries to make her a chicken soup to nourish her body.

Just as he finished packing and was about to leave,

Su Qingxue, who had been working silently, suddenly spoke.

"Xia Feng."

"Hmm?"

Xia Feng turned around.

Su Qingxue looked up at him, her beautiful eyes filled with complex emotions.

"In a few days... when you're free, come have a drink with me."

"...Okay?"

Xia Feng noticed that although her complexion had improved considerably, her spirits still seemed low, so he assumed she wanted to find someone to drink with to clear her head.

Without hesitation, he readily agreed.

“Sure, no problem.”

“Just set a time and place and send it to me. I’ll be there whenever you need me.”

“Okay.”

Su Qingxue nodded gently, then lowered her head again. “Then…see you tomorrow.”

“See you tomorrow.”

Xia Feng said goodbye and turned to leave the office.

As the office door closed,

Su Qingxue, who had been keeping her head down, slowly raised it.

Her eyes churned with a complex mix of emotions.

There was struggle, pain, and… resolve.

After a long silence, she murmured to herself in a voice only she could hear:

“Really…do I have to do this…?”



Chapter 11 Target: Su Qingxue


Xia Feng, humming a little tune, drove blissfully to his usual large farmers' market.

"Boss, a whole old hen, the plumpest one, please!"

"And two pounds of the freshest oysters!"

Xia Feng mentally calculated.

Ru Yan was exhausted yesterday; she needed a good boost.

Old hen soup is incredibly nourishing.

As for the oysters… hehe, I need some too.

After buying the main ingredients, he expertly turned into a nearby traditional Chinese medicine shop and picked up several herbs suitable for making soup with the old hen.

Angelica root, astragalus root, red dates, goji berries—the ingredients were all clearly defined.

Satisfied with his purchases, Xia Feng carried two large bags of his spoils and drove his flashy red Maserati towards the villa.

…

While Xia Feng was busy shopping…

In the master bedroom of the villa.

Liu Ruyan finally groggily woke up from her sleep.

She felt like she'd slept for an eternity.

No wonder, she'd barely slept a wink last night, and unlike Xia Feng, she didn't have an abnormally strong physique. The fact that she'd only woken up this late was already a testament to her good physical condition.

She groggily stretched, the smooth silk blanket sliding down her bare body.

Instantly revealing her previously covered, delicate white skin.

Her body, taut from the stretch, outlined a beautifully curvaceous figure, every inch exuding a fatal allure.

"Hiss..."

Liu Ruyan moved slightly, feeling a little sore, but it was much, much better than the feeling of almost falling apart that morning.

She slowly got out of bed and walked barefoot into the spacious bathroom.

Her reflection shone in the mirror.

Looking at the remaining evidence on her body, her pretty face flushed, and she couldn't help but lightly spit out a curse.

"That bastard... he's such a bull..."

Though she said this aloud, the sweetness and love in her eyes were impossible to hide.

...

Some time later.

Having changed into a loose, comfortable silk nightgown, Liu Ruyan leaned back against the soft headboard.

She picked up her phone.

She opened her notes app, her expression serious, as if she were working on a crucial business plan.

The title of the notes app was: [Sister Candidate List].

She was about to begin the selection process.

A woman who could share the burden and whom she could trust.

The selection criteria for this person had to be extremely strict.

First: She must be someone she knew and trusted.

Knowing her background is key to controlling her, preventing her from inviting trouble and losing both her husband and her money.

Second: She must be good-looking.

This is a hard and fast rule! How can her husband's woman be ugly? It's embarrassing to take her out! Of course, it's best if she's not too much prettier than her.

Third: She must have a good personality.

She can't be the kind of manipulative, scheming woman who's always causing trouble, otherwise, the house will be in constant chaos.

These three points are the most important.

Liu Ruyan quickly filtered through all the women connected to Xia Feng in her mind.

Work colleagues? No, too chaotic, and she doesn't know any of them.

Former classmates? Most of them are married with children, so that's not suitable either.

After much thought, one name finally surfaced clearly in her mind:

Su Qingxue.

Xia Feng's college classmate, now his partner and boss.

Liu Ruyan had a deep impression of this woman.

Back in college, every time she eagerly went to find Xia Feng, eight out of ten times she would see Su Qingxue and Xia Feng together.

They were either in the library, the study room, or eating together in the cafeteria.

Their intimacy caused her to complain to Chen Mi countless times back then.

At that time, she even considered Su Qingxue her biggest rival in love.

But later she realized it.

Xia Feng, that blockhead, truly had a purely platonic friendship with Su Qingxue; he had no romantic feelings whatsoever.

On the contrary…

The way Su Qingxue looked at Xia Feng always seemed a little off.

She noticed it when she looked in the mirror.

That look in her eyes—she knew it all too well; it was clearly the look she gave Xia Feng!

However, after graduation, although they partnered to start a game company,

over the years, they remained just friends and business partners, with no real progress.

Liu Ruyan gradually stopped paying attention to her.

But now…

Things have changed.

Liu Ruyan stroked her chin, her eyes becoming somewhat playful.

After that terrifying night…

She felt that Su Qingxue, who had long harbored ill intentions towards her husband, was someone worth developing a relationship with.

Her looks were absolutely top-tier, no less than her own.

As for her personality, she'd met her a few times and found her quite gentle and sweet; she shouldn't be the type to cause trouble.

Most importantly, she'd liked Xia Feng for so many years!

If she were given a chance, wouldn't Su Qingxue be grateful and call her "sister"? She'd have her figured out immediately.

Yes, that's her!

The more Liu Ruyan thought about it, the more feasible the plan seemed.

She'd even started brainstorming how to create an opportunity to smoothly drag Su Qingxue into the mess.

Just as Liu Ruyan's little head was filled with these random, chaotic thoughts,

the bedroom door was gently pushed open.

Xia Feng, carrying two large bags of groceries, had returned to the villa.

He put everything in the kitchen, prepared the old hen and some ingredients that needed refrigeration, then decided to go upstairs to see if Liu Ruyan was awake.

As soon as he entered, he saw Liu Ruyan wearing loose pajamas, leaning lazily against the headboard.

She was engrossed in her phone, completely absorbed in something, oblivious to his presence.

Her focused expression suggested she was working on some world-class problem.

Xia Feng smiled and tiptoed over.

He leaned close to her, his warm breath brushing against her ear.

"Wife, what are you looking at, so engrossed?"

Liu Ruyan shuddered, but instinctively turned off her phone.

She put the phone aside and smiled at Xia Feng.

"Nothing, just looking at a report my secretary sent me from the company."

As if to bolster her credibility, she abruptly changed the subject, turning the tables on him.

She glared at Xia Feng, puffing out her cheeks, and poked his chest with her finger.

"It's all your fault! You made it so I couldn't go to the office to work today! Humph!"

He looked at Liu Ruyan's pouty face and smiled.

He leaned over and kissed her pouty cheek.

"Yes, yes, yes, it's my fault, my fault."

He took her mischievous finger and asked softly,

"Then, my dear wife, can you forgive me this time?"

Liu Ruyan didn't speak.

She simply withdrew her hand and gently placed her slender, white fingers on her full, moist lips.

Then she blinked her large, watery eyes and looked at him quietly.

This wasn't just a hint; it was a direct declaration.

Xia Feng understood instantly.

He chuckled, reached out and gently pinched her delicate chin, then lowered his head and kissed her lips.

Five full minutes later, the two finally separated, panting.

Liu Ruyan's face was flushed, like she'd been drinking, her eyes glazed and watery. She leaned limply against Xia Feng's chest, breathing softly.

Looking at her alluring appearance, Xia Feng's Adam's apple bobbed. Considering Liu Ruyan's health, he restrained himself.

"Go wait outside, shall we? I've made some soup and stir-fried a couple of dishes. Dinner will be ready soon."

Hearing that Xia Feng had already started cooking dinner, Liu Ruyan immediately perked up.

She sat up straight from Xia Feng's embrace and volunteered:

"Let me help you! Teamwork makes the dream work, right?"

Hearing this, Xia Feng instantly recalled how she'd gotten herself soaked even washing dishes last night.

He couldn't resist reaching out and pinching her soft cheek.

"Forget it, my dear CEO Liu."

He teased,

"If you don't blow up the kitchen, I'll be burning incense in gratitude."

"You!"

Liu Ruyan also remembered the embarrassing incident from last night, her pretty face blushing.

Although she knew she was only making things worse, she was still unhappy to hear Xia Feng say it so bluntly.

She crossed her arms, turned her head to the side, and looked very annoyed.

"Hmph! I'm angry!"

"The kind that needs a big hug to make me feel better!"

Seeing her adorable, petulant expression, what could Xia Feng do?

He could only indulge her!

Without saying a word, Xia Feng simply swept her up in a princess carry, easily lifting her from the bed.

"Ah!"

Liu Ruyan exclaimed, naturally stretching out her arms to tightly wrap around his neck, a happy smile spreading across her face.

Xia Feng carried her to the dining room.

Then he placed the chair next to her on the dining table.

“Wait here patiently, I’ll be done soon.”

With that, he turned and went into the kitchen to continue preparing his dinner.

Watching Xia Feng’s tall figure busy in the kitchen, listening to the sounds of chopping and stir-frying, Liu Ruyan’s lips unconsciously curved into a smile.

Her heart was filled with something called happiness.

During the day, he was always so gentle, so considerate, cherishing her like a precious gem.

But at night…

Thinking of last night, Liu Ruyan's cheeks began to burn again.

Last night, he had become so forceful, so domineering, so tireless, making it impossible for her to even entertain the slightest thought of refusal.

This stark contrast captivated her, but also...terrified her.

"As expected..."

Liu Ruyan silently made up her mind.

"Finding my sister needs to be put on the agenda as soon as possible!"

"Otherwise, if this continues, forget about going to work, I'm afraid I won't even be able to get out of bed!"



Chapter 12: Encountering a Comatose Old Lady While Joining the Fun


When Liu Ruyan saw the dinner Xia Feng had meticulously prepared, her expression was a complex mix.

There was emotion, happiness, but mostly, fear.

Especially when her gaze fell on the steaming plate of garlic oysters, her eyes instantly changed!

It was the look of someone who had seen a ferocious beast!

She instinctively shrank back, looking at Xia Feng, her voice trembling.

"I...I...I really have to go to the company tomorrow, I have a lot of important things to handle, so...so..."

She didn't finish her sentence, but the meaning was clear.

Xia Feng, seeing her terrified expression, found it amusing and was about to explain what he wasn't doing that night.

But before he could speak,

Liu Ruyan gritted her teeth, as if making a momentous decision.

She leaned close to his ear and, in a voice only the two of them could hear, dropped a bombshell.

After speaking, her face was flushed, and her head was almost buried in her chest.

Xia Feng was stunned.

He blinked, looking at Liu Ruyan's bright red ears, and the explanation he had prepared was instantly swallowed back.

He suppressed a laugh, cleared his throat, and nodded with a "serious" expression.

"Well, since you've said that..."

He could only continue this wonderful misunderstanding.

Hehe.

...

The two quickly finished the sumptuous dinner.

Under Xia Feng's half-coercive, half-coaxing approach, most of the large pot of nourishing old hen soup ended up in Liu Ruyan's stomach.

This directly resulted in Liu Ruyan collapsing onto the living room sofa after the meal.

She touched her round little belly, looking completely satisfied, as if saying, "I really can't take it anymore," truly unable to move a single finger.

Xia Feng skillfully washed the dishes.

He walked to Liu Ruyan's side, scooped her up, and laid her comfortably on his lap.

Then, he stretched out his large, magical hands and began to massage her to aid digestion.

"Mmm..."

Liu Ruyan hummed happily, enjoying Xia Feng's meticulous pampering, feeling like the happiest woman in the world.

Time slowly passed.

Soon, the clock on the wall pointed to eleven o'clock.

Liu Ruyan knew what was coming.

She glanced at Xia Feng beside her and saw him looking at her with a half-smile.

She steeled herself, stood up from the sofa, and with a resolute, almost tragic expression, strode heavily towards the room.

Xia Feng found her behavior amusing and followed her into the room.

...The night...

The next morning.

Liu Ruyan woke up feeling refreshed and energized.

Great!

Finally, she could go to work!

For the first time, Liu Ruyan felt that going to work could be such a wonderful and something to look forward to!

In contrast, Xia Feng didn't get up for work today.

Because he had just received a message from Su Qingxue in the company group chat.

It was said to be the final preparation before the game testing entered a crucial phase, so everyone was given a day off to recharge.

Therefore, he had nothing to do today.

Liu Ruyan finished washing up, put on her signature office lady suit, applied delicate makeup, and donned ten-centimeter heels, exuding the powerful aura of an icy female CEO.

She walked to the bedside, leaned down, and planted a fragrant farewell kiss on Xia Feng's lips, who was still lazing in bed.

"Here, honey."

She took a black bank card from her bag and placed it in Xia Feng's hand.

"There's twenty million in this card. You can spend it as you like. The PIN is your birthday."

"If it's not enough, just ask me for more."

"You can also buy yourself a car you like. I'm using my Maserati today."

After saying that, she couldn't resist leaning down and kissing him again.

"I'm going to work now, bye-bye."

She turned and left the room with elegant, confident steps.

Xia Feng lay on the bed, watching her perfect legs, encased in black stockings, disappear through the doorway, then looked down at the heavy black card in his hand.

He couldn't help but sigh.

This gigolo is really sweet!

...

Ten o'clock in the morning.

Since he had nothing better to do, Xia Feng decided to go to the dealership to buy himself a car.

He strolled leisurely down the street.

Just then, he noticed a large crowd gathered not far ahead, chattering excitedly.

People in China love to join in the fun, and Xia Feng was no exception.

Curious, he walked over to see what was going on.

He squeezed through the crowd and saw an elderly woman with gray hair lying on the ground, her eyes closed, her face pale, already unconscious.

The surrounding crowd, layered upon layer, were all discussing the situation, but no one dared to go forward to help her up.

Everyone's face wore a mixture of hesitation and fear, a desire to help coupled with reluctance.

The reasons were obvious to everyone.

Xia Feng dictated at a glance that the elderly woman wasn't faking an accident; she was suffering a severe heart attack!

Without immediate first aid, she might truly be in danger!

He didn't have time to think. He rushed forward, ready to use his "God-Level Massage" to perform an emergency resuscitation massage.

"Hey! Young man!"

Someone nearby immediately tried to dissuade him.

"Don't be impulsive! Think it through! If this is a scam, you'll be ruined for the rest of your life!"

Xia Feng ignored the person's advice.

He understood their concerns.

But he couldn't stand by and watch her die!

Most importantly, he had the ability to do so!

He knelt down, his hands precisely pressing on several key acupoints on the elderly woman's chest, beginning to apply pressure with a special frequency and force.

Through massage, he aimed to stimulate the life force within her body!

Everyone around held their breath, watching this scene with bated breath.

A miracle happened!

Less than a minute later.

While Xia Feng was performing first aid, the elderly woman, whose face had turned blue and whose breathing was weak, suddenly coughed and then slowly opened her eyes!

Seeing this, Xia Feng breathed a sigh of relief, withdrew his hand, and gently asked the elderly woman if she felt any discomfort.

At the same time, he took out his phone and dialed 120 for emergency medical assistance.

The surrounding crowd, seeing that Xia Feng had actually revived the woman, burst into enthusiastic applause and praise!

"Young man! Well done!"

"His medical skills are amazing!"

"Incredible! Truly a virtuous act!"

After calling the ambulance, Xia Feng carefully helped the elderly woman to a shady spot by the roadside to sit down, staying with her while she waited.

Soon, accompanied by the piercing siren, the ambulance arrived at the scene.

After conducting a preliminary examination, the paramedics were full of praise for Xia Feng's emergency measures.

To ensure the elderly woman's health was not compromised, Xia Feng, still concerned, also got into the ambulance and accompanied her to the nearest hospital for a comprehensive check-up.



Chapter 13 An Unexpected Figure


Upon arriving at the hospital, Xia Feng went straight to the payment window.

He paid all the elderly woman's examination and hospitalization fees out of his own pocket.

After completing the formalities, he went to the ward and quietly stayed with the elderly woman, waiting for her family to arrive and for the final detailed test results.

The elderly woman held Xia Feng's hand, thanking him profusely and praising him repeatedly, asking his name and address, insisting that her family repay him properly.

Xia Feng simply smiled and said it wasn't necessary, it was just a small favor.

A while later, a doctor in a white coat walked in with a test report.

The doctor's eyes showed surprise and admiration when he saw Xia Feng.

"The results are in. The elderly woman did indeed suffer a sudden acute myocardial infarction."

The doctor looked at the report, then at Xia Feng, his tone full of disbelief.

"However...it's strange, the patient's myocardial damage is very minor, and all indicators are stabilizing.

It's as if that potentially fatal condition was forcefully suppressed."

The doctor adjusted his glasses and said to Xia Feng:

"Young man, your colleagues in the ambulance said you were the first to perform CPR?

Your technique is truly exceptional! Even better than our most professional doctors!

If it weren't for your proper handling, the old man would have been in real danger!"

"He's fine now, nothing serious. Just take his medication on time and rest well."

Xia Feng nodded.

Just then, the ward door was suddenly pushed open with a bang.

A figure rushed in.

It was a very young girl.

She had a braided hairstyle that draped over her left shoulder.

She wore slightly outdated black-rimmed glasses, but behind the lenses was a delicate and pretty face.

She looked very young, still carrying a hint of student-like innocence.

But her braided pigtails and simple clothing gave her an air of gentle, domestic wifely charm.

She wore a simple white T-shirt and faded sweatpants, with ordinary canvas shoes on her feet.

She wasn't tall, probably only reaching Xia Feng's chest, making her appear petite and delicate.

She rushed in and threw herself at the old woman's bedside, still panting heavily from running so fast.

"Grandma! How are you! Are you alright? What did the doctor say? You can't be hurt!"

Her voice was clearly choked with tears, her eyes red-rimmed, obviously quite frightened after receiving the phone call and rushing over.

The old woman's face lit up with a kind smile when she saw her granddaughter.

She reached out her hand, still attached to the IV drip, and gently stroked the girl's head, comforting her:

"Yingying, don't be afraid, Grandma's alright."

"Thanks to this young man, he saved me, he's Grandma's savior!"

The old woman said, pointing in Xia Feng's direction.

The girl named "Yingying" only then noticed another person standing in the ward.

A tall, handsome man.

She paused for a moment, then quickly turned around, walked briskly to Xia Feng, and, overcome with emotion, grabbed his hand.

"Thank you! Thank you so much!"

Tears welled up instantly, streaming down her cheeks.

"The doctor's explanation on the phone was unclear, it scared me to death… If something had happened to Grandma, I… I really wouldn't know what to do…"

"Thank you so much!"

Her hand was small and soft, and she could feel it trembling noticeably as she held Xia Feng's.

Xia Feng could sense the genuine gratitude and lingering fear in her words.

But he still subtly and gently pulled his hand away.

"It's nothing, just a small favor."

His voice was gentle.

"I just happen to know a little first aid."

Although the girl's hand was soft and comforting, he was, after all, a married man, and it was best to maintain a certain distance from other women.

This was a matter of principle.

Su Qingxue didn't count; she was an old classmate and a good friend.

Feeling the warm touch in her hand suddenly disappear, Zhou Yingying suddenly realized what had happened.

In her excitement, she had actually grabbed a strange man's hand!

Her face flushed red instantly, and she lowered her head shyly.

But it was precisely Xia Feng's deliberate act of keeping his distance that instantly increased her liking for this man several notches.

He had not only saved her grandmother, but he was also a virtuous and upright gentleman!

Zhou Yingying took a deep breath, calmed herself down, and looked up at Xia Feng with a grateful smile.

She then remembered that she didn't know her benefactor's name.

She politely introduced herself:

"Hello, my name is Zhou Yingying. What is your surname, brother? How should I address you?"

"My name is Xia Feng."

"Brother Xia, hello."

Zhou Yingying's tone was full of respect.

“Thank you so much today, I don’t know how to repay this kindness. How about… I treat you to a meal? And I’ll transfer the medical expenses to you.”

“We…we should exchange contact information first?”

As she spoke, she took out her phone from her somewhat worn canvas bag.

Xia Feng’s gaze inadvertently swept over it.

He noticed that Zhou Yingying’s phone was a very old Android model, the screen even had a crack, only slightly better than those basic old-fashioned phones that could only make calls and send text messages.

He instantly understood that the grandmother and granddaughter’s family probably weren’t well-off.

He waved his hand and laughed heartily:

“No need to be so polite, I already said it was nothing.”

“As for the medical expenses, forget about it. For me, that’s just a drop in the ocean, you don’t need to worry about it.”

Before Xia Feng could finish speaking, Zhou Yingying interrupted him firmly.

“No!”

Her attitude suddenly became very resolute.

“Brother Xia, I know you're a good person and don't care about this little bit of money. But we absolutely must repay it!

Let's keep things separate! Just because it's insignificant to you doesn't mean we can accept it without a second thought!”

Her eyes held an unwavering stubbornness, a testament to her pride and dignity.

Xia Feng looked at her earnest expression with a touch of helplessness.

He knew that if he insisted on refusing, it would be disrespectful.

"Alright."

He reluctantly took out his phone and scanned the green QR code.

Zhou Yingying breathed a sigh of relief and quickly scanned the code to add Xia Feng as a friend.

Having finished his business, Xia Feng felt there was nothing more for him to do.

He planned to leave, giving the grandmother and granddaughter some space to talk.

"Well... Grandma, please rest well. Miss Zhou, I'll be going now."

Seeing Xia Feng about to leave, Zhou Yingying quickly said,

"I'll see you off!"

She insisted on escorting Xia Feng to the hospital entrance before stopping.

As Xia Feng turned to leave, she added, "..."

"Brother Xia, I will definitely contact you! Please give me a chance to treat you to a meal to express my gratitude!"

Looking at her sincere eyes, Xia Feng could only nod, agreeing.

...

Leaving the hospital, Xia Feng glanced at his watch; it was already 12:30 PM.

His stomach started rumbling.

"Let's grab some food first, and then we'll buy the car this afternoon."

He was making plans in his mind.

He strolled around the city center, finally arriving at the entrance of an extremely upscale-looking Western restaurant.

This was a place he frequented when he was still the "young master of the Lin family."

However, later, for some reason, he lost his status as the young master, and naturally, he could no longer afford to dine at such places.

But now…

Heh heh, things are different now.

Eating my wife's money? Can that be called being a kept man? That's called my wife's love for me!

He walked into the restaurant.

The restaurant played soft classical music, the decor was luxurious and elegant, and the guests were all well-dressed, chatting quietly—the whole place exuded an air of "high society."

As soon as Xia Feng entered, his gaze habitually swept around the room.

Then, he froze.

At a window seat, he saw a figure that was all too familiar.

Su Qingxue.



Chapter 14: Forced Kiss


Today, Su Qingxue was a completely different person from her usual self at the company, dressed in a blue dress and with her hair in a low ponytail.

Her long, glossy black hair was casually styled into a low bun, with a few playful strands framing her face, adding a touch of allure.

She wore a long black trench coat, completely concealing her voluptuous figure.

Even so, her exaggerated curves were far beyond what a trench coat could hide; in fact, they only made them more breathtaking.

Beneath the trench coat were her long, slender legs encased in black stockings, which extended upwards, disappearing into the mysterious depths of her body.

On her feet were a pair of high, thin red high heels.

Noble, aloof, like a black rose with thorns.

And opposite her sat a well-dressed young man in a designer suit.

The man wore what he thought was a charming smile, launching into a long, rambling conversation about everything from astronomy and geography to luxury brands.

But Su Qingxue didn't even bother to glance at him.

She simply stared blankly out the window, occasionally sipping her coffee.

Xia Feng didn't intend to disturb her. He found a booth where he could clearly see what was happening but wouldn't stand out too much.

A waiter in a vest immediately approached and respectfully handed him the menu.

Xia Feng didn't even look at it, simply saying,

"One black truffle fettuccine, one medium-rare Wellington steak, please."

His voice wasn't loud, but it was clear enough in the quiet Western restaurant.

He had just finished ordering when he looked up.

He found Su Qingxue standing prettily beside his table.

She had recognized him immediately because of his order!

So, she abruptly abandoned the young man, her high heels clicking as she walked straight to Xia Feng's side.

She crossed her arms, looking down at Xia Feng with a mocking smile.

Xia Feng was startled by her sudden appearance.

"Qing...Qingxue?"

Seeing Xia Feng's bewildered expression, Su Qingxue nodded with satisfaction, her mood seemingly improving instantly.

"May I sit here?"

she asked.

But without waiting for Xia Feng's reply, she plopped down opposite him.

The young man she had so ruthlessly abandoned was already furious!

He had watched helplessly as the blind date he had just fawned over simply sat down opposite another man.

This behavior showed a complete disregard for him.

It was an utter humiliation!

A normal man would have already stormed off, refusing to endure this humiliation.

But… Su Qingxue was simply too beautiful.

So beautiful that he couldn't bear to give up so easily.

He had no choice but to brazenly stand up from his seat and walk towards Xia Feng's table.

He forced what he thought was a very magnanimous smile, intending to sit down naturally next to Su Qingxue, hoping to strike up a conversation.

But as he took a step closer,

Su Qingxue's icy, emotionless voice rang out.

"Li Lei, don't sit next to me."

The young man named Li Lei froze instantly.

He stood there awkwardly, unsure whether to move or sit, his face alternating between pale and flushed, looking extremely unpleasant.

Seeing the tense atmosphere, Xia Feng quickly stepped in to smooth things over.

He stood up from his seat and sat next to Su Qingxue, giving up his previous spot.

"Um... sir, please sit there."

His intention was to ease the tension.

But this gesture, in Li Lei's eyes, was undoubtedly a deeper, second blow!

He wanted to sit next to Su Qingxue, but she ruthlessly stopped him!

And this man simply sat down next to her, and not only did she not say anything, she even subconsciously leaned closer to him!

This preferential treatment was too obvious!

Li Lei felt a burning pain on his face, as if he had been slapped several times in public!

At this moment, the waiter approached and respectfully asked Li Lei:

"Hello, sir, would you like me to move your order from the previous table to this one?"

Li Lei had no choice but to nod, gritting his teeth.

"...Thank you."

It seemed he intended to stubbornly stay and share a table with them.

The atmosphere became extremely awkward.

Xia Feng leaned close to Su Qingxue's ear and whispered:

"Qingxue, who is this guy? What's going on?"

Su Qingxue mimicked him, whispering in Xia Feng's ear, her warm breath tickling his ear.

"His name is Li Lei. He's a blind date arranged for me by my family.

I've refused many times, but this time, because his family has some business dealings with my dad's company, I really can't refuse."

Xia Feng understood immediately.

Well, his "good buddy" was in trouble, and as his "brother," he had to help get rid of this fly!

So, he moved even closer to Su Qingxue.

Their intimate, whispering conversation only fueled Li Lei's rage!

He felt a heavy weight on his head, as if a green meadow had sprouted there!

What was the difference between this and a minotaur in front of him?!

Suppressing his anger, he forced a smile that looked more like a grimace and asked Su Qingxue:

"Qingxue, aren't you going to introduce... this friend next to you?"

Su Qingxue's face remained cold; she didn't want to acknowledge him at all.

Seeing her like this, Xia Feng knew it was his turn to step in.

He smiled slightly, looked at Li Lei, and his opening line was a bombshell!

"Oh, hello."

"My name is Xia Feng, and I'm Qingxue's boyfriend."

Upon hearing this,

both Su Qingxue and Li Lei were simultaneously stunned.

Li Lei was shocked, while Su Qingxue was utterly overjoyed!

But her reaction was incredibly quick.

After less than a second of stunned silence, an indescribable elation flashed in her eyes, and she couldn't suppress the smile on her lips!

She didn't speak, but instead showed her stance through her actions.

She reached out and grabbed Xia Feng's arm, pulling it tightly into her embrace!

Xia Feng felt his arm sink into an indescribably warm and soft cloud, accompanied by an amazing elasticity.

The feeling was wonderfully intoxicating!

"Yes."

Su Qingxue hugged Xia Feng's arm, resting her head intimately on his shoulder, asserting her ownership over Li Lei.

"He's my boyfriend."

However, Li Lei wasn't stupid.

He had clearly caught Su Qingxue's momentary surprise.

He knew this was definitely an act!

He sneered, forcing himself to remain calm, and said:

"Qingxue, stop pretending.

There's no need to resort to such childish tricks, is there?"

"I don't think you can just fool your uncle and aunt with anyone."

Seeing that Li Lei was using his parents to pressure her, Su Qingxue's eyes turned cold.

She turned her head and softly called to Xia Feng.

"Xia Feng..."

Xia Feng also turned to look at her, about to ask what was wrong.

"Wh...Ugh!"

Before he could finish his sentence, Su Qingxue leaned in and fiercely sealed his lips with her soft, sweet lips!

This made him swallow his words.

Xia Feng's eyes widened instantly!

Meanwhile, Li Lei, sitting opposite her, saw this scene.

His face turned green in an instant!

Green to the point of purple! Purple to the point of black!

Looking at the two still kissing so brazenly, he felt like his lungs were about to explode with rage!

He simply couldn't stand it any longer!

He abruptly stood up, pointing at the two of them, stammering, "You...you two..." for a long time, finally managing only a cold snort through gritted teeth, before turning and leaving without looking back!



Chapter 15 Mutual Feeding


After Li Lei stormed off, Su Qingxue didn't immediately release Xia Feng.

Instead, it was as if she wanted to unleash all the emotions that had been building up over the past few days through this kiss!

Her movements became even more intense, more proactive.

Xia Feng's mind had completely shut down, passively accepting Su Qingxue's actions.

Finally, after a long few minutes, the two slowly separated.

A shimmering silver thread appeared between them, slowly drooping under gravity, finally breaking in mid-air.

Su Qingxue gasped for breath, her already exquisite face flushed with a captivating blush, whether from lack of oxygen or shyness.

Her eyes were hazy, shimmering with tears, staring intently at Xia Feng, as if trying to absorb him completely.

Xia Feng felt his heart pounding in his throat. He stammered,

"Qing...Qingxue, this..."

Su Qingxue seemed not to hear him.

She quickly composed herself, forcibly changing the subject, and began to thank Xia Feng.

"Xia Feng, thank you...for today. You did me a huge favor."

Her voice was still trembling, but she had regained some composure.

Xia Feng's mind was still a mess, and he could only subconsciously reply,

"Ah...oh, it's nothing, a small matter."

Then, an awkward silence fell between them again.

Xia Feng was completely at a loss for words.

He couldn't understand whether Su Qingxue's kiss was because she was acting to get rid of Li Lei, or because...

He dared not think any further.

And Su Qingxue?

She had no intention of letting go of Xia Feng's arm.

She held his arm tightly, even greedily, in her soft, supple embrace.

Her head rested affectionately on his shoulder, savoring this precious moment of intimacy that belonged only to her.

Soon, the waiter brought their food.

Aromatic black truffle fettuccine and two sizzling Wellington steaks.

And the light snacks Li Lei had ordered earlier.

With such delicious food before them, a very practical problem arose.

Xia Feng's right arm was held tightly by Su Qingxue, and cutting steak required the use of both hands.

He could only awkwardly remind her:

"Um... Qingxue, it's time to eat."

Su Qingxue's eyes showed a clear reluctance upon hearing this.

But she still reluctantly released Xia Feng's arm.

Xia Feng just breathed a sigh of relief and tried to get up to sit back down at the opposite seat.

But the moment he lifted his buttocks, Su Qingxue grabbed his sleeve.

“Don’t go…just sit here.”

“But…”

“Sit here, please.”

She looked up at Xia Feng with an almost humble, pleading gaze.

That look instantly softened Xia Feng’s heart, and he couldn’t utter a single word of refusal.

He sat back down beside Su Qingxue.

The two began to eat in silence.

The atmosphere at the table was quiet, but a fierce internal struggle was raging in Su Qingxue’s mind.

Reason told her that Xia Feng was already married, and her current behavior was the very act of a mistress she despised.

She should immediately stop herself and distance herself from him.

But…

The feelings she had harbored for nearly ten years were like an erupting volcano, impossible to suppress!

Why?

Why should the person she had silently loved for so many years be so easily taken away by someone else?

She was unwilling to accept it!

In the end, emotion triumphed over reason.

She made up her mind; she would fight for herself! Even if it meant suffering a bloody end, she would accept it!

Having made up her mind, Su Qingxue put down her knife and fork.

She raised her head, her bright and burning eyes fixed on Xia Feng.

Xia Feng was a little embarrassed by her sudden gaze.

"What's wrong? Is there something on my face?"

Su Qingxue didn't answer his question.

She simply parted her lips and uttered two words.

"Feed me."

"Huh?"

Xia Feng thought he had misheard and instinctively made a questioning sound.

Su Qingxue's voice rang out again, this time much clearer.

"I said, feed me."

She gazed at Xia Feng with her large, watery eyes, her gaze filled with expectation and assertiveness.

Xia Feng felt immense pressure.

He looked at Su Qingxue, then at the steak on his plate, and finally relented.

He clumsily cut off a small piece of steak, pierced it with his fork, and hesitantly held it to her lips.

He was frantically hypnotizing himself internally.

"It's okay, it's okay... just think of it as feeding a brother! Yes! Just like when I fed that guy Lin Yu! That's it!"

Su Qingxue looked at the steak offered to her lips, opened her cherry-like mouth, and took a big bite.

She chewed, her eyes crinkling with happiness, a satisfied smile spreading across her face, her eyes crinkling like a kitten that had stolen a treat.

Looking at her adorable expression, Xia Feng felt his steak taste even better.

Then, Su Qingxue opened her mouth again.

Xia Feng had no choice but to continue feeding her.

One piece, two pieces, three pieces…

Finally, the entire expensive Wellington steak on his plate was gone, completely devoured by Su Qingxue.

Seeing that Xia Feng had finished his steak, Su Qingxue finally picked up her knife and fork, satisfied, and began cutting her own portion.

She cut a small piece, then, mimicking Xia Feng's earlier gesture, held it to his lips, explaining:

"Here, open your mouth. This is your reward for standing up for me and feeding me."

Xia Feng, helpless against her insistent gaze, had no choice but to open his mouth and eat.

Seeing that Xia Feng had also eaten what she fed him, Su Qingxue's smile widened even more.

Lunch was finished in this mutually feeding atmosphere, a mixture of ambiguity and sweetness.

After the meal, Su Qingxue naturally wrapped her arm around Xia Feng's again, taking a break.

Xia Feng instinctively tried to pull his arm away.

But Su Qingxue held on even tighter.

This only made Xia Feng's arm sink deeper, and the sensation became even clearer and more intense.

He had no choice but to give up struggling.

"Xia Feng, what are your plans for this afternoon?"

Su Qingxue suddenly spoke, her head resting comfortably on Xia Feng's shoulder, her voice soft.

The faint fragrance emanating from Su Qingxue made Xia Feng feel somewhat at ease.

Hearing her question, he didn't hide anything and answered truthfully:

"I plan to buy a car this afternoon. I used to live close to the company, so I didn't need one.

Now that I've moved to Moonlit Villa, it's quite far from the company, so I still need a car."

Su Qingxue's eyes lit up instantly!

"I'm free this afternoon! I'll go with you! Okay?"

Her tone was pleading.

She looked up at Xia Feng, her large eyes watery and pitiful.

It was as if she would cry if Xia Feng dared to say "no."

Xia Feng, seeing her like this, didn't think anything was wrong.

So, he nodded.

"Okay, let's go together then."

Upon receiving a positive reply, Su Qingxue's eyes visibly brightened with joy, and she radiated an aura of happiness.



Chapter 16 Su Qingxue's Autobiography


After a short rest at the Western restaurant, the two left.

Su Qingxue suggested taking Xia Feng to a dealership she knew well.

Xia Feng, knowing little about cars and not caring where they went, readily agreed.

"Okay, whatever you say."

The whole way, Su Qingxue held Xia Feng's arm tightly.

This made him feel both comfortable and somewhat uncomfortable.

After all, he was now a married man.

He tried several times to ask Su Qingxue to let go.

But each time he was about to speak, Su Qingxue would immediately look at him with teary, pitiful eyes, making him swallow his words.

Finally, he became a little more forceful, half-pulling, half-dragging his arm free.

But under the onslaught of Su Qingxue's tearful gaze, he gave in.

Finally, their arms were entwined, and they were holding hands.

Her fingers were tightly intertwined.

This was the last line Su Qingxue could accept.

Looking at her "I'll cry if you let go again" expression, Xia Feng had no choice but to let her have her way.

He could only silently tell himself:

It's okay…

We're brothers! Best buddies!

What's wrong with good brothers holding hands? It's normal!

Yes, that's it!

The two of them walked hand in hand to the extremely luxurious dealership Su Qingxue had recommended.

The man was handsome, the woman beautiful, and both had outstanding presence. As soon as they entered, a very capable-looking sales manager immediately greeted them with a warm smile.

"Good afternoon, gentlemen. How can I help you?"

Xia Feng didn't really have a concept of what kind of car to buy; he just wanted to buy any car that could get him around.

Su Qingxue, familiar with Xia Feng's aversion to trouble, proactively made the decision for him.

She first turned her head and softly asked Xia Feng,

"Xia Feng, what price range are you planning to buy?"

Xia Feng thought for a moment about the card Liu Ruyan had given him and casually replied,

"Around five million."

His words surprised both Su Qingxue and the sales manager beside her.

But Su Qingxue quickly understood.

She remembered that Xia Feng's wife was the renowned president of the Liu Group—Liu Ruyan.

She understood.

For someone of Liu Ruyan's wealth, five million was indeed like five hundred yuan for an ordinary person—a drop in the ocean.

Su Qingxue ultimately chose a brand-new Maybach S-Class for Xia Feng.

Understated luxury, high-end elegance, and an extremely luxurious interior.

The car's on-the-road price was approximately four million.

Xia Feng didn't even haggle over the price, nor did he bother with a test drive.

"This one will do."

He directly took out the black card Liu Ruyan had given him and handed it to the stunned sales manager.

"Swipe the card."

The whole process was smooth and efficient.

Because it was a cash-on-delivery car, all the paperwork was completed quickly.

In less than half an hour, this brand-new Maybach was ready to drive away from the dealership.

Sitting inside, enjoying the luxurious interior and comfortable seats, Xia Feng nodded in satisfaction.

He turned and smiled at Su Qingxue beside him.

"Qingxue, get in the car, I'll take you for a drive!"

"Okay."

Su Qingxue smiled, her eyes crinkling, and naturally walked to the passenger side, opened the door, and got in.

A small sense of smugness and victory filled her heart.

Hmph, Liu Ruyan!

I'm the first woman to sit in the passenger seat of Xia Feng's new car!

Just as Su Qingxue was fastening her seatbelt, she encountered a small problem.

Because her trench coat was quite thick today, coupled with her astonishing bust, the seatbelt felt a bit tight and uncomfortable no matter how she fastened it.

She simply took off her black trench coat and casually draped it over the back seat.

With the trench coat off,

her black spaghetti strap dress underneath was completely exposed to Xia Feng's eyes.

The bottomless cleavage made Xia Feng's eyes widen.

And when she pulled the seatbelt back over her chest, it accentuated her impressive figure even more.

Xia Feng felt his throat go dry.

He quickly averted his gaze, pretending to look straight ahead, focusing on starting the car.

But according to the great law of universal gravitation,

his gaze would still uncontrollably drift towards the magnificent scenery next door every now and then.

Su Qingxue naturally noticed his restless gaze.

A sly smile curved her lips.

She deliberately stretched and puffed out her chest.

This action made the already breathtaking scenery even more magnificent.

Xia Feng felt his heart pounding even faster.

Seeing Xia Feng's awkward expression of wanting to look but not daring to, Su Qingxue couldn't hold back any longer, bursting into laughter, her clear, bell-like laughter filling the entire car.

Xia Feng drove, and before he knew it, he was on a coastal highway overlooking the boundless sea.

He rolled down the window, and the salty sea breeze blew in.

Looking at the expansive and magnificent scenery outside the window, both of them gradually relaxed, enjoying this rare tranquility.

Su Qingxue suddenly spoke.

Her voice was very soft, as if afraid of disturbing something.

“Hey, Xia Feng…”

“If…the person who told you they liked you first was me.”

“Aren’t you…aren’t you already mine?”

She laid her cards on the table.

So directly, for the first time, she revealed to Xia Feng the feelings she had buried for nearly ten years.

Xia Feng’s hand gripped the steering wheel tightly.

He didn’t speak, but silently continued driving, though the car’s speed unconsciously decreased.

"The first time I saw you was during the summer before my freshman year of college, in a park."

"At that time, you were climbing a very, very tall tree, helping a little girl who was crying desperately to rescue her kitten."

"Finally, you caught the kitten, but because the kitten was wriggling in your arms, you fell from the tree, getting covered in mud."

"I was watching from a short distance away, thinking... this person is so silly."

“But…he was a good person too.”

“Later, unexpectedly, we ended up in the same class after school started.”

“Once, a boy I didn’t like confessed to me, and I rejected him.

He actually got angry and tried to…”

“You just happened to be passing by, rushed up, chased him away, and saved me.”

“That was the first time we officially met.”

She muttered something with a slight laugh as she said this.

"You didn't even know me back then! We were in the same class, and I'm a real beauty, okay?!"

"As we spent more time together, I realized I might have fallen for you."

"When I found out you had a childhood friend who often came to see you, I was so nervous and scared."

"It wasn't until you told me that you two were just like friends that I truly breathed a sigh of relief."

"Then, we graduated.

To pursue our shared dream, we founded this game company together and found many like-minded partners.

We worked in the same office every day, constantly seeing each other.

During those days, I felt like I was the closest person in the world to you."

At this point, Su Qingxue's voice choked with emotion.

Tears finally streamed down her cheeks.

"I always thought... I always thought we'd go on like this forever, until one day, things would naturally fall into place and we could be together."

"But... but in the end, you were still taken away by Liu Ruyan."

"I don't blame her..."

Her voice was filled with pain and resentment.

"I only blame myself, blame myself for being such a coward!"

"If... if I could have been earlier, if I could have been just a little braver..."

"Would the ending... have been different?"

"Qingxue..."

Listening to her suppressed pain and soft sobs, Xia Feng felt as if his heart was being violently gripped.

He didn't know what to say.

Any words of comfort seemed so pale and powerless at this moment.

He could only remain silent, listening intently.



Chapter 17 Goodbye, My First Love


A while later,

the sobbing inside the car gradually subsided.

Su Qingxue slowly composed herself.

She took out tissues from her delicate little bag and carefully wiped away the tears on her face.

Then she took out a small makeup mirror and meticulously touched up her makeup.

Soon, a beautiful woman reappeared in the mirror.

However, the slightly reddened corners of her eyes proved that she had indeed been crying.

Looking at Xia Feng, who had remained silent beside her and even slowed the car considerably, she suddenly smiled.

That smile carried a sense of relief, like the sun breaking through a storm.

"Ah~~"

She let out a long sigh, completely relaxing.

"It feels so much better after saying it out loud."

"Looks like it's time for me to let go of this failed crush and start my new life."

She turned her head and winked playfully at Xia Feng.

"Xia Feng, don't worry about what I just said."

"Starting tomorrow, we'll still be best friends, best partners! Let's keep fighting for our dreams together!"

"Go for it!"

She even clenched her fists in front of her chest, like in an anime, to encourage herself.

That forced ease, that strained bright smile, made it seem like she had truly let go of that heavy feeling.

Xia Feng remained silent.

He just watched her quietly, his heart aching as if pricked by needles.

Because he knew it was just a forced smile.

The more relaxed she appeared, the more pain she was in.

He remained silent for a long time, so long that the smile on Su Qingxue's face was about to crumble.

He spoke slowly, in a very soft voice.

"I think..."

"I must have liked you back then."

These words exploded in Su Qingxue's mind like a thunderbolt!

She froze, her feigned ease instantly freezing.

Xia Feng didn't look at her, continuing to stare at the road ahead, talking to himself.

"After all, you're a great beauty, with a wonderful personality, and you share the same hobbies and dreams as me."

"Being with someone as outstanding as you, it would be a lie to say I wasn't moved at all."

"But..."

His voice carried apology.

"I'm sorry, Qingxue."

"Now, I no longer have the right, nor the ability, to reciprocate your feelings."

Su Qingxue, who had been stiff from the words "liked you," went limp upon hearing his final, resolute words.

She maintained her smile, but it was a forced one.

"Oh, what are you saying?"

Her voice was slightly unsteady.

"It's like I'm some kind of pitiful person. It's not like I can't live without you. Don't forget, the men who chase after me could line up from the company gate to the beach!"

As she spoke, her voice grew softer and softer, until finally she fell silent.

The atmosphere in the car became oppressive again.

After a long while,

Su Qingxue finally spoke in a deeply weary voice:

"Xia Feng, take me home."

“Okay.”

Xia Feng turned the car around and, following Su Qingxue's directions, drove towards her home.

The car eventually arrived at a top-tier villa area called “Flying Snow Manor.”

Xia Feng knew Su Qingxue was also a wealthy woman.

Thinking about it, it made sense. When they started their company together, she provided most of the initial capital, while Xia Feng only contributed his technical expertise.

Being able to casually invest millions in a game company with an uncertain future meant her family background was undoubtedly extraordinary.

The car stopped in front of one of the villas.

Su Qingxue put her black trench coat back on, opened the car door, and prepared to get out.

Xia Feng also unbuckled his seatbelt and got out, intending to walk her to the door.

The two walked a few steps towards the door in silence.

Suddenly, Su Qingxue, who was walking ahead, stopped abruptly.

Then, before Xia Feng could react, she threw herself into his arms!

She hugged his neck tightly, stood on tiptoe, and kissed him again.

Xia Feng's body stiffened for a moment, but he finally reached out and gently wrapped his arms around her waist.

This kiss was a farewell filled with sorrow and reluctance.

Soon, they parted.

"Xia Feng."

Su Qingxue looked into his eyes, a hint of determination in them.

"See you at the company tomorrow."

"And... goodbye, my first love."

"...Yeah, see you at the company tomorrow."

Xia Feng's voice was a little hoarse.

Su Qingxue gave him one last, deep look, then turned abruptly and strode quickly towards the villa gate.

Finally, her figure disappeared from Xia Feng's sight.

Xia Feng stood there for a while before getting back into his car.

He didn't drive off immediately, but sat in the driver's seat, lit a cigarette, and smoked silently.

He didn't smoke, but he carried a pack of cigarettes every now and then, lighting one when his mind was in turmoil, to give himself a little relief.

His mind was in turmoil right now, like a heavy stone was lodged in his throat, making him feel suffocated.

After a long while, he finally started his car and drove away.

He planned to buy groceries, then go home to cook and wait for his wife to come home.

He planned to tell Liu Ruyan everything that had happened that day.

Meanwhile, inside the villa.

As soon as Su Qingxue entered, she leaned against the door, as if all her strength had given way.

She watched through the window as the headlights of Xia Feng's Maybach disappeared from sight before dragging her heavy steps up to the bedroom on the second floor.

She could no longer hold on, collapsing onto the soft bed, burying her face in the pillow, lost in thought.

Just then.

Buzz—

Her phone suddenly vibrated.

It was a text message from an unknown number.

She picked it up with some confusion and opened it.

The next second, her eyes widened in shock!

……………………

On the other side.

Xia Feng, who was driving back, also received a text message from Liu Ruyan.

【Honey, one of my best friends came back from abroad today and invited me to dinner tonight, so I won't be home for dinner. You'll have to take care of dinner yourself, no need to cook for me. Love you~ Mwah (づ￣ 3￣)づ】

Xia Feng looked at the message from Liu Ruyan on his phone screen, a bitter smile creeping onto his face.

His wife's text message eased the heavy, oppressive feeling in his heart considerably.

Since she wasn't coming home for dinner, he didn't need to go grocery shopping.

He drove straight back to the villa at Moonlit Manor.

He'd just cook himself a simple bowl of noodles for dinner.

Time quickly passed to 7 PM.

Night fell, and the city lights began to twinkle.

In a high-end bar in Jiangcheng called "Nightfall Dawn."

In an exquisitely decorated private room.

A stunning woman, dressed in a standard business suit and exuding a powerful aura, sat quietly on the sofa.

She wasn't drinking, nor was she on her phone; she simply held a glass of water, seemingly patiently waiting for someone.

She was Liu Ruyan.

About ten minutes later.

The door to the private room was pushed open from the outside.

A woman with an equally stunning figure, wearing a long black trench coat and exuding a noble and aloof air, walked in.

It was Su Qingxue.

Liu Ruyan saw her and a meaningful smile appeared on her face.

She swirled the water in her glass and slowly said:

"You're here."

"I've been waiting for you for a long time."



Chapter 18 Speed ​​is of the essence, sister!


Su Qingxue entered the private room, closing the door behind her and shutting out the outside noise.

"What do you want with me?"

Her tone was certain.

No need for further probing; she had confirmed the fact once more.

Even if I like him, I can't interfere anymore."

That was a relationship that lasted a full seven years.

From their first meeting when she was eighteen, to now, twenty-six.

Eight years, eight years of companionship, eight years of affection…

How could she just let go like that?

Liu Ruyan looked at her heartbroken appearance, a mysterious smile appearing on her face.

"What if… I said I wouldn't mind you joining in?"

These words struck Su Qingxue like a thunderbolt!

They left her completely stunned!

She stared blankly at Liu Ruyan, her mind a complete blank.

Was she hallucinating?

What had she just said?

Join?

Was that even Chinese?!

Or…did this woman, the president of the Liu Group, have some peculiar fetish she wasn't aware of?

Her voice suddenly lowered, and a hint of fear even appeared on her face.

Could it be that their marriage had touched upon the interests of some powerful family, and someone wanted to harm them?

"Could it be that you've been targeted? Or that you have some terminal illness and don't have long to live, so you want me to help you take care of Xia Feng?"

This plot... is great! She can totally accept it!

And she didn't mind taking care of Xia Feng at all; in fact, she was quite willing.

"I'll take care of your husband, so you have nothing to worry about."

How could this woman's thought process be so strange!

But as she listened… her face visibly flushed, from her cheeks to her ears, and then to her neck.

She… she was still a virgin!

How could Liu Ruyan say such… shameless things in front of her!

Amidst the shyness, an uncontrollable surge of curiosity arose within her.

Was he really… really that strong?
