"Haven't you liked Xia Feng for so many years?"

"Just nod now, call me 'sister,' and I'll grant your wish."

Su Qingxue blurted out almost without hesitation, without even thinking!

Her voice was clear and crisp!

What a joke!

This incredible opportunity was like a huge pie falling from the sky and landing right in her mouth!

If she were still being coy, hesitant, and unable to accept it, then she would truly be the biggest idiot in the world!

As for two people… three people…

Does it matter?

As long as she could be with Xia Feng, and rightfully possess him, nothing else mattered!

She gestured with her hand.

Hmm… although a certain part is indeed quite large.

Now that the alliance is formed, it's time to put it into action immediately.

This is too fast!

She just tearfully said goodbye to her first love, Xia Feng, this afternoon, and tonight… she's going to… you know?

"These things need to be done quickly and decisively! We need to make it a fait accompli and settle the matter!"

"With my husband's responsible nature, he'll definitely admit it!"

"Let's go! Let's go back now!"

Liu Ruyan stood up from the sofa, grabbed Su Qingxue's hand, and started to leave.

"Wait for me in the car. I'll go in and deal with him first, create a good opportunity for you, and then I'll message you."

Xia Feng, completely unaware of their shared goal, was in the villa's living room, watching a boring TV program while planning how to tell Liu Ruyan about what happened that day when she returned.



Chapter 19: I've been tricked again.

But instead of driving directly to the villa's entrance, she parked in a secluded corner not far away.

After turning off the engine, she turned to Su Qingxue, who was sitting upright in the passenger seat, her palms sweating nervously, and gave her a gentle smile.

"Qingxue, wait for my message in the car."

She took a spare set of keys from her bag and handed it to Su Qingxue.

"These are the villa keys. Keep them just in case."

"Remember, when I message you, just open the door and come in. No need to knock. You must come!"

Excitement, nervousness, shyness, and a thrill...

“Honey, I’m home!”

“Look what I brought you!”

"Why are you so late? I thought you were going to spend the night out. I was so worried."

"This wine is silky smooth on the palate, not astringent at all, and has a fruity aftertaste—it's absolutely delicious!"

He couldn't help but exclaim.

Back when he was still the eldest son of the Lin family, his family was strict and he was rarely allowed to drink.

He could only occasionally have a little when his cheapskate father took him out to social events and broaden his horizons.

But those so-called top-tier red wines were worlds apart from this!

After all… this wine was truly delicious!

As for what happened during the day, there were more important things to do now! They could talk about it later!

Inside the Maserati outside the villa.

Su Qingxue felt like she was turning into a statue waiting for her husband.

Chapter 20 Wishes Fulfilled


Just as Xia Feng was inwardly fretting about whether he possessed some kind of "innate divine body,"

Liu Ruyan was quite uninhibited.

"No... this isn't your idea again, is it?"

he also needed to carefully review the data he had copied from that hacker's server that morning.

He wanted to see who was behind this little-known company.



Chapter 24 The Mastermind: Li Lei


The data was massive and disorganized, but that wasn't a problem for Xia Feng at his current level.

His fingers tapped lightly on the keyboard, and countless streams of data flowed like docile lambs, rapidly being filtered, organized, and categorized before his eyes.

Soon, he found the order record for the attack on "Dream Chaser" company.

[Order Placement: Anonymous (IP address encrypted via multiple layers of VPN)]

[Target: "Dream Chaser" Game Company, Jiangcheng, Longguo]

[Mission Requirements: Completely destroy all data on its servers, including backups, making it unrecoverable.]

[Reward: Five million.]

Seeing this number, a cold smile curled at the corner of Xia Feng's lips.

Five million? They wanted to destroy three years' worth of hard work and dreams from dozens of people?

The amount wasn't large, but the insult was extremely strong.

He continued reading.

The data also included internal communication records from this hacking company.

"Boss, this deal is a bit strange. It's just a little-known game company, how could someone offer five million?"

"Who cares, as long as there's money to be made! I checked, that company's firewall is as flimsy as paper, even an intern could easily take it down. This is practically picking up money!"

"Haha, it really is! It's done, less than ten minutes! The money's in the account! Earning five million was too easy, like a dream!"

Xia Feng looked at these chat logs, his eyes growing even colder.

Hopefully, that five million can make up for all your subsequent losses.

He scrolled up again, trying to see where the anonymous IP address came from.

Although it had multiple layers of encryption and a proxy, in the eyes of this top-tier hacker at the limits of human potential, these tricks were nothing.

He easily peeled back the layers of disguise, tracing back to the original IP source.

Next door, Hancheng.

A private server owned by a large family surnamed Li.

“Hancheng…the Li family…”

Xia Feng's brows furrowed tightly as he began to think rapidly.

Zhu Meng was just a small company focused on game development; Su Qingxue's initial investment was only three million.

Their company kept a low profile, quietly developing and polishing their game. How could they have offended a large family in the neighboring city?

This made no sense.

Just then, a figure flashed through Xia Feng's mind: someone dressed in an expensive suit, looking respectable, but with eyes filled with arrogance and jealousy.

Surnamed Li…

And wasn't Su Qingxue's blind date from the day before yesterday named Li Lei?

Xia Feng's eyes narrowed instantly!

Could it be such a coincidence?

He immediately entered the name Li Lei and the keywords "Hancheng Li family" into a search engine.

The next second, a large amount of related information popped up.

The Li Group of Hancheng is a prominent family business in Hancheng, and Li Lei is one of the most beloved grandsons of the Li family patriarch!

All the clues connected at this moment!

Private order…timeline…surname…

It all matches perfectly!

“As expected, you good-for-nothing.”

A cold glint flashed in Xia Feng’s eyes.

Just because he lost face in front of Qingxue, he resorts to such despicable means of revenge?

What a sore loser!

Xia Feng turned his head and glanced at Su Qingxue, who was diligently working behind her desk.

She seemed to sense his gaze, looked up, and gave him a sweet smile.

The anger in Xia Feng's heart instantly dissipated, replaced by tenderness.

He returned the smile, then looked back at the computer screen.

Qingxue absolutely couldn't know about this.

With her kind nature, if she knew that he was the reason for such a disaster for the company, she would definitely feel guilty and remorseful to death.

He would take revenge himself.

But how?

Xia Feng stroked his chin, his eyes cold.

Should he simply use his hacking skills, the limits of human capability, to send the Li family's dirty laundry to the Municipal Bureau and destroy them?

For him, this wouldn't be difficult, and he had no qualms about it.

After all, they've managed to train someone like Li Lei.

But if only there were some stealthy methods…

Like casting a spell or something.

The thought alone made Xia Feng chuckle.

But with the system at his fingertips, what if it really existed?

With a thought, he opened the system panel.

【Points: 30】

This was the result of his efforts last night with Liu Ruyan and Su Qingxue.

Perfect for three draws.

He'd give it his all; what if he could actually draw a spell?

“System, draw!”

Xia Feng silently shouted in his mind.

【Received, initiating beginner draw x3】

The familiar giant roulette wheel was about to spin again.

Xia Feng looked at the flashy but impractical animation and couldn't help but mentally complain.

"System, this roulette wheel is completely useless! You still get to decide what you draw each time, don't you?

Just tell me what I got next time, stop with all this fancy stuff."

[Received. From now on, the lottery animation will be omitted, and the reward results will be announced directly to the host.]

Before Xia Feng could react, the system notifications rang out one after another.

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained 2 [Attribute Points]!]

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained 1 [Attribute Point]!]

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained 200 boxes of daily items: Ultra-thin Suit!]

"..."

Xia Feng stared at the simple, even somewhat meager, rewards and fell into a long silence.

As expected... this is the true drop rate of the beginner lottery.

It seems those three skills he acquired before were truly a maximum benefit during the newbie protection period.

"Sigh..."

Xia Feng sighed inwardly.

It seems I'll have to honestly save up points to try my luck in the intermediate lottery, which costs 100 points per draw.

Since I can't get something as simple and direct as black magic, I'll have to resort to a slightly more complicated method.

He refocused his attention on the document and began copying all of the Li family's criminal records.

This incriminating evidence could deal them a devastating blow.

Even if he couldn't destroy it outright, it would cripple the Li family.

He organized the copied document, packaged all the evidence of their and the Li family's crimes, and anonymously sent it to the Han City Police Department.

Consider it a service to the people, and a little bonus for the police officers to boost their year-end performance.

Having done all that, he focused on his work.

He was going to use his current top-notch programming skills to redesign a firewall for the company's servers that no one in the world could break through!

Impregnable, unbreakable!

Time ticked by as he focused and worked efficiently.

…

He didn't know how much time had passed.

Xia Feng, engrossed in typing code, suddenly felt a pair of soft little hands gently pinching his cheek.

He pulled his attention away from the vast world of code and turned around.

He found Su Qingxue standing prettily beside him.

And next to her, a small folding table had been unfolded, on which were several dishes in takeout containers, still steaming.

Seeing that Xia Feng's attention was finally on her, Su Qingxue released his hand with satisfaction and led him towards the small table.

"Alright, we can talk about work later, let's eat first."

Her voice was gentle and soothing.

"I had someone pack this up for me."

Looking at his considerate wife, Qingxue, Xia Feng felt a warmth in his heart and couldn't help but shake his head and chuckle.

"I used to be the one telling you this, advising you not to overwork and to get some rest."

"Now, it's your turn to tell me that."

"How the tables have turned!"

The two sat down on opposite sides of the small table.

Su Qingxue handed him a pair of chopsticks.

"Don't say so much, just eat. These are all your favorite dishes."

Looking at the delicious-looking dishes, Xia Feng was even more touched.

He picked up a piece of sweet and sour pork ribs, but instead of putting it in his own mouth, he held it to Su Qingxue's lips.

"Wife, you eat first."

Su Qingxue tucked a strand of hair behind her ear, revealing a happy smile. She opened her mouth and took a big bite.

"Thank you, husband."

She also picked up a piece of golden-brown, crispy fried potato and fed it to Xia Feng.

"Husband, you eat too."

Lunch passed by in the midst of their sweet, affectionate interactions.



Chapter 25 Buying groceries


After lunch, Su Qingxue, seeing Xia Feng eager to plunge back into the sea of ​​code, proactively cleared all the takeout boxes from the table.

"Xia Feng, you go ahead with your work, I'll take care of this."

She knew Xia Feng was definitely doing something extremely important, so she took on these trivial tasks to avoid distracting him.

Xia Feng felt a warmth in his heart at his wife's meticulous care.

He didn't stand on ceremony, nodded, and continued working on the firewall design.

...

Time flew by, and it was already six in the evening, time to leave work.

Xia Feng stretched lazily and stood up from his seat.

After an afternoon of intense work, he had finally completed the prototype of the new firewall.

Although only about 30% of the work is complete, even that 30% is enough to reliably defend against all attacks except from a handful of top-tier hackers in the world!

Xia Feng even added a little "surprise" to this firewall.

Once an attack is detected, it not only perfectly defends but also automatically launches a counterattack along the network cable!

Using his specially crafted information torrent, it instantly overwhelms the opponent's server, paralyzing them!

Xia Feng stood up, stretching his body, which had become stiff from sitting for so long, while pondering to himself.

"This won't do. I haven't had time to exercise lately."

"I feel like everything except my lower back is rusting."

He secretly resolved to find time for a proper full-body workout; he couldn't just keep working on his lower back.

Su Qingxue also finished packing her things, stood up from her office chair, and walked to Xia Feng's side.

The two smiled at each other, then naturally took hands and walked out of the office.

This scene was finally clearly seen by the employees in the company who were preparing to leave work.

Everyone's eyes widened instantly!

If no one had noticed when the two came in this morning because the atmosphere was too tense,

now they saw it clearly!

Brother Feng, holding hands with Boss Su?!

After Xia Feng and Su Qingxue disappeared from the elevator, the entire office area erupted in chaos!

"Holy crap! Did you see that?! Brother Feng and Boss Su, they're holding hands!"

"I saw it! I saw it! My god, they're... really together?"

A female colleague covered her mouth in shock.

“It’s very possible! They were close before, but they’d never been this intimate! Now they’re holding hands, there’s definitely something fishy going on!”

“But…”

Xiao Li, who had chatted with Xia Feng in the parking lot a couple of days ago, scratched his head, looking confused.

“Didn’t Brother Feng just tell us a couple of days ago that he got married? The Maybach he drove this morning was brand new.”

Everyone fell silent upon hearing this.

Yeah… Brother Feng is already married.

Then what does this mean?

…

A young male colleague who had just graduated swallowed his words back.

The atmosphere in the office became somewhat awkward for a moment.

Finally, a programmer who was usually on good terms with Xia Feng slapped his thigh and said nonchalantly:

"Who cares! Feng-ge is so awesome, so handsome, so capable! What's wrong with having one more woman?!"

These words seemed to instantly awaken everyone.

"Yeah! What's wrong with having one more?!"

"Exactly! Isn't it normal for Feng-ge to have a few more female confidantes?"

"That's right! Support Feng-ge!"

Just then, a pretty intern with a ponytail, looking quite young, stood up, her eyes sparkling with admiration and longing.

She clenched her fist, as if making a decision, and said to her friends:

"If Boss Su can do it, then we can too! Feng-ge is our hero! I've decided, I'm going to confess to Feng-ge tomorrow!"

Her friends around her also looked excited.

"Yes! Take me with you! I'm coming too!"

Xia Feng and Su Qingxue were completely unaware of what was happening upstairs in the office.

At this moment, they were strolling hand in hand through the bustling market.

An old man who often sold vegetables there greeted Xia Feng with a cheerful smile as soon as he saw him.

"Oh, Xiao Feng, you actually brought your wife to buy groceries today?"

He glanced at Su Qingxue beside Xia Feng, his eyes lighting up.

"Oh my, your wife is so beautiful! You two are a perfect match, a match made in heaven!"

The fruit vendor next door also chimed in, praising them.

"Yes, yes, Xiao Feng is so lucky!"

Hearing these heartfelt compliments, Su Qingxue felt as sweet as if she had eaten honey, her heart overflowing with joy!

Her smile never faded, and she radiated happiness.

Finally, the two of them, carrying several large bags of groceries, contentedly put them into the trunk of the Maybach.

Xia Feng looked at the almost overflowing trunk, and pinched Su Qingxue's cheek with a wry smile.

"You, you bought so much! How are the three of us going to finish it all?"

"Looks like we won't need to buy groceries for the next week."

Su Qingxue stuck out her tongue, hugged Xia Feng's arm, and snuggled against him, saying sweetly,

"I'm happy~"

Xia Feng patted her head, his eyes full of affection.

...

Xia Feng quickly drove back to the villa at Moonlit Manor.

Coincidentally, Liu Ruyan also arrived in her flashy red Maserati.

She got out of the car and saw Xia Feng and Su Qingxue carrying several large bags of groceries out of the trunk, and she was also surprised.

"Did you bring the whole market back?"

"Are we having guests today? Why did you buy so much?"

Xia Feng chuckled and recounted the amusing events that unfolded at the market that day to Liu Ruyan.

Liu Ruyan beamed after hearing it.

She walked over to Xia Feng, took his other arm, and declared,

"Then I want to go grocery shopping with you next time!"

Xia Feng glanced at Liu Ruyan on his left, then at Su Qingxue on his right, and smiled helplessly:

"Sure. But we'll have to go to a different market then."

"Otherwise, wouldn't those old folks be terrified if they saw I had a new wife?"

The three chatted and laughed, returning to the villa in a harmonious atmosphere.

Dinner time.

Liu Ruyan, a kitchen idiot who never lifted a finger, dutifully settled into the sofa with snacks, quietly watching TV and waiting for dinner.

Meanwhile, Xia Feng and Su Qingxue, the two chefs, went into the kitchen together to prepare dinner.

Soon, a sumptuous meal was served.

During dinner, Su Qingxue excitedly recounted to Liu Ruyan what had happened at the company that morning, and Xia Feng's heroic performance in turning the tide.

Liu Ruyan listened, stunned, her eyes gleaming with admiration as she looked at Xia Feng.

"Wow! Honey, you're so amazing! You even know how to hack!"

Her tone was full of admiration and pride.

Then, as if she had thought of something, her eyes lit up.

“By the way, honey, my company’s firewall system is also needing an upgrade soon.”

“How about… you design a firewall for my company?”

She looked at Xia Feng, offering a sky-high commission in a consultative tone.

“Then, we’ll settle you according to the highest market standards.”

“I’ll have the most professional team evaluate your work to see what level it can reach.”

“If your firewall is truly outstanding, the highest… I can give you a reward of thirty million.”

She said this so Xia Feng wouldn’t feel like she was taking advantage of him.

After all, even close brothers keep clear accounts.

The same applies to husband and wife.

However, Xia Feng agreed without hesitation.

“Okay, no problem.”

He looked at Liu Ruyan, his eyes gentle.

“But forget about the money. You and Qingxue are both my wives. How can I ask for money when I’m doing something for my own wives?”

“Besides, didn’t you give me a black card with twenty million before? Consider that as payment.”



Chapter 26 Cats and Dogs War


Finally, despite Xia Feng's gentle yet resolute attitude, Liu Ruyan couldn't persuade him.

The 30 million yuan firewall design order had thus become a free project for Xia Feng, done out of love.

Liu Ruyan could only helplessly give up.

"Fine, fine, whatever you say."

Although she said this, she was secretly delighted.

Her man was so considerate, so loving!

However, as she picked up her water glass to drink, her beautiful eyes unconsciously darted around, and a sly smile curved her lips.

A bold and exciting mischievous idea was brewing in her mind.

Xia Feng was focused on eating, so he didn't notice his wife's subtle change in expression.

But Su Qingxue, sitting beside him, saw it all clearly.

She was curious; what kind of wicked idea was this woman coming up with now?

…

This time, Xia Feng volunteered to clean up the dishes after the meal.

Su Qingxue wanted to help, but Liu Ruyan pulled her to the sofa in the living room.

Su Qingxue watched Xia Feng's busy figure in the kitchen, then looked at Liu Ruyan beside her, who was smiling like a little fox.

Unable to contain her curiosity any longer, she leaned closer and whispered:

"Sister, were you thinking about something at the dinner table just now?"

"Your eyes were darting around like crazy, you're definitely up to something."

"Want to know?"

Liu Ruyan smiled mysteriously and beckoned to Su Qingxue with her finger.

"Come closer, I'll tell you."

Su Qingxue immediately obediently leaned closer.

Liu Ruyan whispered her daring plan in her ear.

As Su Qingxue listened, her already fair face visibly flushed red, spreading from her cheeks to her neck.

What...what had she heard?!

This…this is too…

But…

It sounds like…

Especially Liu Ruyan's last words echoed in her mind.

“Our husband was so amazing today, saving your whole company, don’t you…want to reward him properly?”

Reward him…

Yes!

Xia Feng was a hero today!

He saved the dreams of so many people at “Chasing Dreams”!

She had to reward him properly!

Su Qingxue’s heart was instantly filled with a sense of mission!

She looked up at Liu Ruyan and nodded heavily.

“Then come with me, we need to choose carefully!”

She stood up from the sofa, gesturing for Su Qingxue to follow.

Before leaving, she called out towards the kitchen.

“Honey! I’m taking Qingxue back to her room first!”

“Just come over when you’re done!”

Xia Feng’s somewhat puzzled reply came from the kitchen.

“Okay.”

…

The two arrived at the master bedroom on the second floor.

Liu Ruyan walked to a seemingly ordinary but enormous wardrobe in the corner of the room and simply pulled open the door.

The next second, a visually stunning new world appeared before Su Qingxue's eyes!

“Wow!”

Su Qingxue couldn't help but exclaim in amazement!

The wardrobe was filled with a huge pile of expensive clothes.

This…this is practically an armory!

Su Qingxue stared in disbelief at the sight, then turned to look at Liu Ruyan beside her.

“Sister, so many…it seems you planned this all along!”

“Of course!”

Liu Ruyan proudly put her hands on her hips, her face radiating confidence, as if everything was under control.

“I, Liu Ruyan, never fight a battle I’m not sure I can win!”

“Come on, little sister, pick whatever you like!”

The two women exchanged a smile, then enthusiastically began selecting items from the wardrobe.

…

Xia Feng finished washing the dishes and tidied up the kitchen briefly before wiping his hands and heading towards the bedroom.

He was still a little puzzled.

It wasn’t even nine o’clock yet, why was he being called in so early?

He opened the bedroom door with a question in his mind.

“I’m here, what is it…”

He couldn’t utter the rest of his words.

He stood frozen in place, as if struck by lightning, speechless with astonishment.

………………

The next morning.

As the first rays of dawn streamed into the room through the curtains.

Xia Feng opened his eyes, feeling refreshed.

With a thought, Xia Feng opened the system panel.

【Host: Xia Feng】

【Age: 26】

【Height: 185cm】

【Strength: 12】

【Constitution: 15】

【Endurance: 20】

【Speed: 12】

【Points: 60】

Looking at his dramatically increased attributes, Xia Feng nodded in satisfaction.

Constitution increased by 2 points, Speed ​​by 1 point, and Endurance skyrocketed by 5 points!

Finally, around eight o'clock, he managed to bring the two back to normal.

The three of them washed up and went downstairs together.

Liu Ruyan went to the Liu Group, while Xia Feng drove Su Qingxue to Zhumeng.

...

Liu Group, CEO's office.

As soon as Liu Ruyan sat down in her executive chair, she immediately clutched her head, her face contorted in pain.

"What happened? What on earth happened?!"

She couldn't understand.

Just the night before last, they were still able to reach a balance.

But why...

Why did it suddenly turn out like that?!

The thought of this possibility filled Liu Ruyan with despair.

No!

The Women's Sorrow Alliance must expand! It's urgent!

...

Meanwhile, on the other side.

Sitting in the passenger seat of a Maybach, Su Qingxue also looked at Xia Feng, who was driving, with fear.

"Um... Husband..."

She asked cautiously.

"Have you gotten stronger lately? You seem to run over ten kilometers without getting tired."

"Sister Ruyan and I ran five kilometers and we couldn't go any further."

Hearing her question, which was filled with lingering fear, Xia Feng could only laugh awkwardly.

What could he say?

"Ahem, maybe... I'm still growing?"

Xia Feng could only make up a random excuse to brush it off.



Chapter 27 The Smug Face of a Petty Person


Xia Feng drove his understated yet luxurious Maybach, carrying Su Qingxue, smoothly towards the company building.

But as they parked and got out to enter the building, an unexpected figure blocked their way.

Li Lei.

Today, he was dressed in a well-tailored designer suit, his hair slicked back with gel, looking quite presentable.

However, the undisguised arrogance and resentment on his face made his expensive attire look like a joke.

He stood there stiffly at the building entrance, clearly waiting for them.

His gaze was fixed on Xia Feng and Su Qingxue.

Especially when he saw Su Qingxue's face, made even more alluring and beautiful by love, seemingly glowing with a delicate beauty, the jealousy and anger in his eyes almost solidified!

This woman!

This woman who should have belonged to him!

Damn it!

He first met Su Qingxue at a business meeting between companies.

At that time, she was brought there by her father, a business tycoon, to broaden her horizons and learn the ways of the business.

His own father happened to be the other party in that collaboration.

He was completely captivated by Su Qingxue's pure and sweet face and her ridiculously hot figure at first glance!

Later, he took the initiative to strike up a conversation. When he heard Su Qingxue's soft yet sweet voice, a strong possessive desire instantly surged within him!

Such a beauty was destined to be his, Li Lei's, woman!

That's why, taking advantage of the recent business dealings between the two companies, he asked his father to mention it to the other party, hoping they could help matchmake.

Su Qingxue's father also felt that his daughter was almost twenty-six and should find a partner.

Furthermore, he had a good impression of Li Lei, this "young talent," so he decided to give it a try and arranged for the two to meet alone.

Although Su Qingxue remained aloof throughout their meeting,

and was dressed very conservatively,

Li Lei didn't take it to heart at all.

Beautiful women, after all, have a bit of a temper and a bit of airs; that's normal.

The sense of accomplishment and exhilaration of melting this aloof iceberg and conquering her was the most intoxicating!

But he never expected that Xia Feng would suddenly appear out of nowhere!

Not only did he ruin his plans, but the two of them even kissed shamelessly right in front of him!

What was this?!

This was like someone shoving a green hat on his head right in front of him!

No man could accept such an utter humiliation!

He stormed off in a rage, his anger burning so intensely he felt like he was about to explode!

Upon returning home, he immediately conducted a thorough investigation into his rival.

What he found out made him so angry he nearly flipped the table!

What kind of rich young master was he? Just a poor kid who appeared out of nowhere!

How dare he steal his woman?!

With that lousy game company he co-owned with Su Qingxue?!

So, he directly used his connections, having his men commission a well-known hacking firm to place the five million yuan order.

He wanted to utterly destroy their hard work and dreams!

He wanted them to know what the consequences of offending him, Li Lei, would be!

Then their companies would go bankrupt, they'd be desperate, and wouldn't they have to obediently come begging to him?

What a pity…

Li Lei's gaze swept over Su Qingxue's voluptuous figure encased in a black business suit, a flicker of regret crossing his mind.

She'd already been used by someone else; she definitely didn't deserve the position of his wife.

But…

Being a mistress he could summon and dismiss at will was still possible.

Just thinking about Su Qingxue's fiery figure and sweet voice moaning and yielding beneath him made him feel a surge of excitement.

...

As soon as Xia Feng and Su Qingxue got out of the car, they saw Li Lei blocking their way.

Su Qingxue's face instantly turned cold.

Without thinking, she immediately reached out and tightly hugged Xia Feng's arm, pressing her soft body against it, as if asserting her dominance.

She looked up at Li Lei with icy eyes.

"Why are you here?"

Li Lei's expression grew even more arrogant at her possessive behavior.

He snorted coldly, speaking in a tone full of mockery and schadenfreude:

"Hmph, why can't I be here?"

"As for you two, I heard there was a small problem with your company's data yesterday. Were you all scrambling around like ants on a hot plate?"

"Let me tell you, it's all because of you! It's you, this ungrateful woman, who caused all this!"

Su Qingxue heard the undisguised smugness and threat in his words, and her chest heaved with anger!

"So it really was you, you bastard!"

"Why did you do this?!"

"You can eat whatever you want, but you can't say whatever you want!"

Li Lei scoffed, shrugging his shoulders with an innocent "it's none of my business" look.

"What do you mean, why did I do this? I didn't do anything."

"I just happened to hear about something interesting happening at your company, so I came to check it out out of curiosity."

He paused, his eyes growing more threatening.

"Of course, I guess there will be more 'little accidents' like yesterday."

"And it all depends on your choice, Miss Qingxue."

"You don't want to see all your hard work of the past few years being sabotaged and ultimately reduced to nothing, do you?"

He approached step by step, a confident, triumphant smile on his face.

"As long as you agree to become my woman.

I will naturally use my power to help you sort all this out!"

He had investigated.

Her father, the chairman of Su Qingqingxue's company, never interfered in her affairs whatsoever.

In fact, he didn't approve of her running a game company at all, always wanting her to return to the family business so she could inherit it in the future.

After all, she was his only precious daughter.

Therefore, Li Lei was certain that in this situation, Su Qingxue had absolutely no one to turn to for help!

He assumed that Su Qingxue would have no choice but to endure her resentment and humiliation in agreeing to his demands.

However, he was wrong.

Just as he was gloating, preparing to enjoy Su Qingxue's desperate and humiliated expression,

a figure suddenly appeared in front of him.

It was Xia Feng.

Xia Feng's face was expressionless, only his eyes were cold.

Before Li Lei could even question him about his intentions,

*Slap—!!!*

A crisp, resounding slap suddenly echoed in the empty parking lot!

Xia Feng raised his hand and delivered a powerful slap to Li Lei's face!

The force of the blow sent Li Lei flying!

He spun through the air like a tattered sack before crashing heavily to the ground, spitting out a mouthful of bloody foam mixed with several teeth!

He was completely stunned!

Lying on the ground, his head buzzing, he couldn't get up for a long time!

Xia Feng shook his slightly numb hand and let out a long breath.

"That feels better."

He didn't even glance at the still-dazed cripple on the ground, turning to Su Qingxue with a bright smile.

"I've listened to him babbling on and on for ages, now I finally feel good."



Chapter 28 Like a Dead Dog


Xia Feng walked back to Su Qingxue's side.

He looked at his wife's chest, rising and falling slightly with anger, and her pretty face flushed with rage.

He reached out and gently pinched her smooth cheek.

"Alright, alright, don't get angry over such a lowly scoundrel."

His voice was gentle.

"If you're really still angry, just tell me, and I'll go grab him, pin him to the ground, and give him a good beating to vent your anger."

"But..."

Xia Feng's tone shifted, a mischievous smile playing on his lips.

"Don't do it yourself. I'm afraid you'll be rewarding him by hitting him."

"Save your energy for rewarding me tonight."

Su Qingxue was amused by his playful remark.

She reached out and gently patted his chest, playfully scolding,

"You're so annoying! What are you saying in public!"

Xia Feng laughed heartily, taking her hand and intertwining their fingers.

Meanwhile, Li Lei, who had been lying motionless on the ground, finally recovered from the excruciating pain and dizziness.

He staggered to his feet, feeling that half of his face was completely numb, and his mouth tasted of rust.

He wiped his hand—his hand was covered in blood!

Li Lei's eyes instantly turned red, filled with resentment and madness!

He pointed at Xia Feng, who was intimately flirting with Su Qingxue, and was about to speak, about to threaten them with the most vicious words he could think of.

But just then!

"Ring ring ring—!"

A rapid, piercing cell phone ring suddenly broke the silence of the parking lot, sounding particularly abrupt.

Li Lei instinctively took out his phone, and when he saw the word "Father" on the screen, the anger in his heart was like a bucket of cold water being poured over his head, instantly extinguishing most of it.

He forcibly suppressed his anger and the excruciating pain on his face, trying to make his voice sound normal, and answered the phone.

“Hey, Dad? What's up with calling so early…”

“Where are you, you bastard? Get back here right now!!”

“Because of you, the Li family is finished!!”

Before he could finish speaking, a deafening roar he'd never heard before came from the other end of the line!

Li Lei's expression underwent a dramatic change.

His face instantly turned ashen!

“What?! How could this be! Dad, you're not kidding me!”

Hearing his father's furious roar on the other end of the line, cold sweat began to bead on his forehead, and his body trembled uncontrollably.

“No…it can't be! We did those things so discreetly, how could we have been found out?! Who?! Who's behind this?!”

His voice was filled with obvious fear.

As the voice on the other end of the line grew more urgent, Li Lei's face finally turned deathly pale!

With a “thud,” the phone slipped from his limp hand and fell to the ground, the screen shattering instantly.

He felt as if all his strength had been drained away; his legs gave way, and he almost collapsed to the ground again.

He didn't even bother to look at Xia Feng and Su Qingxue again, nor did he bother to utter a single harsh word. He simply scrambled towards his car, his face filled with anxiety and fear.

Xia Feng watched his hastily fleeing figure, a cold smile creeping across his face.

He knew the "gift package" he'd sent out last night had taken effect.

Given the severity of the evidence in that document, the Li family was already overwhelmed with their own problems. Their only option now was probably to make a drastic sacrifice, to send out a scapegoat to quell the storm.

And Li Lei, that incompetent fool, was undoubtedly the best choice.

The best outcome would likely be spending the rest of his life in prison.

At worst, he might have to pay for those lives with his own.

Of all people to mess with, he had to mess with me.

He'd really be courting death.

...

In the elevator, only Xia Feng and Su Qingxue remained.

In this enclosed and solitary space.

Su Qingxue could no longer hold back!

She whirled around, opened her arms, and wrapped them tightly around Xia Feng's neck, clinging to him!

Then she stood on tiptoe and kissed him!

Ding—!

The sound of the elevator doors opening finally snapped them out of their passionate kiss.

A glistening silver thread stretched between them, then slowly broke.

Su Qingxue's pretty face was flushed crimson. She gasped for breath, looking at Xia Feng, giving him a meaningful look.

The meaning was clear.

"I'll reward you properly later."

Then, blushing, she straightened her slightly disheveled clothes, stepped out of the elevator first, and hurried towards her office.

Xia Feng stood at the elevator entrance, took a deep breath, and calmed his somewhat excited body.

Then he stepped into the office area.

As soon as he entered, he noticed that everyone's eyes were fixed on him.

Those eyes were full of gossip, curiosity, and ambiguity.

Some of the bolder female colleagues even seemed eager to do something, but ultimately gave up due to a lack of courage.

Xia Feng was somewhat bewildered, and could only smile and greet everyone before quickly walking towards his office.

Leaving behind a group of whispering employees.

"Holy crap! Did you guys just see that? There are lipstick marks on Feng's face and lips!"

"I saw it! I saw it! Boss Su's lip color looks a bit off too! They definitely just kissed!"

A male colleague wearing glasses groaned.

"Waaaaah, my Feng-ge... Boss Su went too fast!"

"Stop crying! What are you yelling about, you grown man?!"

"Waaaah... Feng-ge has a wife now, and Boss Su too, he definitely won't go out drinking with us anymore! My happiness is gone!"

"I really want to kiss Feng-ge too... My lipstick is strawberry flavored, it's so sweet! But... I'm too scared..."

A female colleague covered her face, looking conflicted.

"Yeah, yeah, I'm too scared either.

How about... at the next company party, we try to get Feng-ge drunk, and then we all go for him?"

"Great idea! Let's do it!"

"You guys are dreaming! Feng-ge can drink like a man, last time at the party he single-handedly took down our whole department! You bunch of pushovers?"

The person who finally told the truth was surrounded and beaten up by a group of female colleagues.

...

As soon as Xia Feng entered the office, he saw Su Qingxue frantically applying lipstick with a small makeup mirror.

Xia Feng subconsciously wiped his mouth with the back of his hand.

Sure enough, a bright red mark was left on the back of his hand.

He then understood why those guys outside had looked at him like that.

He walked over to Su Qingxue, both amused and exasperated, and pinched her soft cheeks with both hands.

"You, you, it's all your fault! I'll be laughed at at the company from now on!"

"Hehehe."

Su Qingxue didn't say anything, just let him pinch her cheeks, giggling foolishly.

Her smug expression clearly showed no remorse.

Xia Feng looked at her charming appearance.



Chapter 29 A Chance Encounter with Zhou Yingying


...

Noon.

Xia Feng, feeling refreshed, made a phone call and had two meals packed and delivered.

In the office, Xia Feng leaned back on the sofa, letting Su Qingxue comfortably nestle against him.

Then he picked up the lunchbox and began feeding her bite by bite.

"It's all your fault!"

Su Qingxue opened her small mouth, ate the bite Xia Feng fed her, and then playfully punched his chest with her little fist, complaining coquettishly.

"Now I have no energy left, I even need you to feed me."

Looking at her adorable, tired yet satisfied expression, Xia Feng felt a surge of tenderness and accomplishment.

He fed her while sincerely apologizing.

"I'm sorry, honey, it's my fault. I didn't control myself."

"To punish myself, I've decided I won't touch you for the next week! Is that okay?"

"No way!"

Before Xia Feng could finish speaking, Su Qingxue refused without even thinking!

What a joke!

She looked up at him angrily.

"You're only thinking about yourself, trying to make things easy for yourself, aren't you?"

"Don't you think about what my sister and I will do if you really hold back for a week? Do you want us to die of exhaustion in bed? Humph~"

These words left Xia Feng speechless.

It seems... she's right.

He could only force a laugh and beg for forgiveness.

"Okay, okay, my fault, my fault, I won't punish you anymore, I won't punish you anymore."

"Let's eat first, and after we eat, I'll give you a massage to help you recover your strength."

"Ah~ Mmm..."

Satisfied, Su Qingxue leaned back into his arms, opening her small mouth.

Xia Feng fed Su Qingxue bite by bite, until she finished both lunches.

Then he used his [Divine Massage] to help her recover her strength so she would have the energy to continue working in the afternoon.

After tidying everything up, Xia Feng returned to building the firewall.

...

Time quickly passed to six o'clock in the evening.

The office staff gradually left.

But Su Qingxue, sitting in her boss's chair, showed no intention of getting up to go home.

Xia Feng had completed half of the firewall. He stood up, about to ask Su Qingxue to go home with him.

He was met with a captivating glare from her.

"Hmph! It's all your fault!"

Su Qingxue pointed to the huge pile of unprocessed files on the computer screen and said angrily,

"I haven't finished my work for today! The game project is at its most critical stage, and I have to handle many things personally. I have to work overtime to get it done!"

Xia Feng knew immediately that it was indeed his fault.

He could only rub his nose and chuckle awkwardly.

"You can go back now."

Su Qingxue looked at him, her voice softening again.

"I'll probably be home very late tonight, so you don't need to wait for me or cook for me."

"Okay, call me when you're done, and I'll come pick you up."

Xia Feng said tenderly.

"Okay, goodbye, husband."

Xia Feng stepped forward and kissed her on the lips before turning and leaving the company.

He drove his Maybach straight home; the groceries he bought yesterday were enough for several days.

Just then, his phone vibrated.

It was a text message from Liu Ruyan.

【Honey, I have an urgent project coming up, I have to go on a business trip to a neighboring city for two days, so I won't be home tonight.

You and Qingxue enjoy your time together~(ﾉ´▽｀)ﾉ♪】

Xia Feng looked at the message and smiled helplessly.

Well, now neither of his wives is coming home for dinner tonight.

He was too lazy to cook, so he'd just grab something to eat out.

He drove through the bustling city.

Without realizing it, he found himself on the food street near his old university.

He parked the car and walked into a noodle shop that looked a bit old, but was kept very clean.

This noodle shop was his favorite place during his university years.

The owners were a kind elderly couple who made chewy noodles with a rich, flavorful broth at reasonable prices, making it a favorite among poor students.

Xia Feng found a seat by the window, picked up the well-worn menu, and was about to order.

Suddenly, a familiar, gentle voice reached his ears.

"Hello, what would you like to eat?"

Xia Feng instinctively looked up.

The next second, he froze.

"Huh? You are... Yingying?"

"Xia... Brother Xia?!"

Standing beside his table was none other than Zhou Yingying, whom he had met just two days ago.

Today, she was wearing the shop's simple employee uniform, a simple apron tied around her waist.

Her long, black hair was still tied into a braid and draped over her left shoulder.

Perhaps because of the familiar surroundings, she seemed much more composed than when she was at the hospital.

She wasn't wearing her somewhat dated black-rimmed glasses anymore, revealing a delicate and gentle face.

Clean, pure, and possessing a certain inexplicable gentle, domestic charm.

"What a coincidence! Are you working here?"

Xia Feng asked with a smile.

"Yes, I am."

Zhou Yingying seemed very happy to see Xia Feng, a genuine smile appearing on her face.

"My family isn't well-off, so I have to work to earn my tuition and living expenses."

"Are you a student at Jiangcheng University?"

"Yes!"

Zhou Yingying nodded.

"That's such a coincidence."

A nostalgic smile appeared on Xia Feng's face.

"I used to be at Jiangcheng University too, in the Computer Science department."

Upon hearing this, Zhou Yingying's eyes instantly lit up!

"Brother Xia, are you also a student at Jiangcheng University?!"

"I'm also in the Computer Science department!"

"That's even more of a coincidence."

Xia Feng chuckled.

"So, you should call me senior."

"Xia... Senior Xia, hello!"

Zhou Yingying was a little shy, but still greeted him sweetly.

Because of this short exchange, the distance between the two instantly shortened considerably, making them seem more like friends.

Just then, a urging voice came from the kitchen.

"Yingying! Come help! We'll be getting busy soon!"

"Okay! Coming!"

Zhou Yingying quickly called out towards the kitchen.

She turned to Xia Feng, looking a little embarrassed.

"So, what would you like to eat, senior? It's on me."

Xia Feng waved his hand, smiling as he declined.

"No need, it's just a bowl of noodles, no need to pay for such a small thing."

"It's only such a small amount of money that I can afford to treat you."

Zhou Yingying playfully stuck out her tongue.

"If it's some fancy meal, I really won't have any money. Hehe."

Looking at her frank and adorable appearance, Xia Feng chuckled.

"Well... thank you so much, Junior Yingying."

"You're welcome~"

"Then I'll have a bowl of their signature beef noodle soup, and a plate of dumplings, with extra chili sauce."

"Okay, please wait a moment, senior. It'll be up soon."

Zhou Yingying jotted down notes in her notebook as she gave her instructions.

"Okay, no rush. You go ahead with your work, but be careful not to fall."

"Okay!"

Watching Zhou Yingying's retreating figure, Xia Feng couldn't help but sigh inwardly.

What a coincidence this world is!



Chapter 30: Another Golden Reward


While waiting for the item to appear, Xia Feng, having nothing better to do, opened the system panel.

Looking at the 70 points displayed, his heart began to itch again.

It wasn't that he didn't want to try the intermediate lottery, which required 100 points per draw.

But leaving these 70 points idle seemed like a waste.

How about…

another round of beginner lotteries?

What if? What if he got another golden skill? Wouldn't that be a huge win?

Once this thought popped into his head, he couldn't suppress it.

"Damn it, let's do it!"

Xia Feng mentally slapped his thigh.

"Points can be earned again, as long as I go back and train my back properly!"

With that thought, he didn't hesitate any longer and directly gave the system a command in his mind.

"System! Lottery! Draw them all!"

[Received, initiating beginner lottery x7]

The system's voice was still as cold as ever, but Xia Feng's heart was burning with excitement.

The next second, a dazzling golden light almost blinded him!

"Holy crap!"

Xia Feng's heart leaped!

"Golden light!"

"Whoosh, takeoff!"

His emotions instantly surged with excitement!

Immediately afterward, a series of system notifications, like firecrackers, rang wildly in his mind!

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained the item: 1000 pairs of various black stockings!]

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained the item: 1000 pairs of various white stockings!]

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained 4 attribute points!]

[Congratulations, host, you have obtained 2 attribute points!]

[Congratulations, Host! You have obtained 1 [Attribute Point]!]

[Congratulations, Host! You have obtained 500 boxes of Ultra-Thin Suit Sets!]

[Congratulations, Host! You have obtained a Golden Reward: Skill: Ancient Martial Arts!]

“…”

Xia Feng stared at the long list of rewards, his expression a mixture of speechlessness and ecstatic joy.

What the heck were those two thousand pairs of stockings?

System, are you running a textile factory?!

But…

Xia Feng's mind conjured up images of Liu Ruyan and Su Qingxue's long legs encased in stockings.

Hmm, these rewards… seem pretty good?

I'll have Qingxue try on all those strange styles when I get back!

As for the seven attribute points, I'll save them for later.

And those five hundred boxes of Ultra-Thin Suit Sets, the more the merrier.

After all, I'm using them up a bit too quickly.

Finally, his gaze fell on the last, glittering golden reward.

[Skill: Ancient Martial Arts]

Just by looking at the name, you know this is an absolutely divine skill that can enhance combat power!

He accepted it in his mind without hesitation.

"Accept!"

Boom—!!!

A terrifying flow of information, far larger than the previous two, poured into his brain!

At the same time, a mysterious and powerful warm current flowed through his limbs and bones, permeating every corner of his body!

Countless profound principles about fist techniques, palm techniques, body techniques, and internal energy cultivation methods seemed to be engraved into his bones, instantly becoming a bodily instinct!

At this moment, he not only fully understood the knowledge, but his body also internalized it as an instinct!

After a while, Xia Feng slowly opened his eyes.

At this moment, even his temperament had undergone a subtle change.

Although his appearance remained unchanged, his eyes held a new depth and composure.

His entire being seemed to have ascended to a new level!

Is this… the realm of a Grandmaster of Ancient Martial Arts?

Xia Feng clenched his fist, feeling the subtle control he now had over his body, utterly astonished.

"Amazing."

Just as he was silently experiencing the changes in his body,

a commotion suddenly arose not far away.

Xia Feng looked up, following the sound.

He saw Zhou Yingying standing helplessly beside a dining table, repeatedly bowing and apologizing to a bald, burly man.

The man was extremely muscular, wearing a tight black vest, his muscles bulging like blocks of iron, exuding explosive power.

On his black vest was a very noticeable dark stain, stained with some soup and food residue, clearly indicating that something had been spilled on him.

Xia Feng frowned and quickly got up to go over.

He walked to Zhou Yingying's side and asked with concern,

"What's wrong? What happened?"

When Zhou Yingying saw Xia Feng, she seemed to see her pillar of support; her eyes reddened, and her voice became flustered.

"Senior..."

She pointed to the bald, burly man, then to the mess on the ground, explaining in a tearful voice,

"I...I was carrying noodles and walking in a bit of a hurry, I didn't notice this gentleman, and then...and this happened..."

She quickly turned back to the bald, burly man and continued to apologize profusely.

"I'm sorry, I'm sorry! Sir, I'm so sorry! I didn't mean to!"

"Um...I'll pay for your table! Consider it an apology, I'm really sorry!"

Xia Feng looked at her almost crying appearance, then at the bald, burly man who had remained silent throughout.

This guy doesn't look like someone to mess with. If he's a troublemaker, Yingying will be in big trouble.

However, to his surprise,

the bald, burly man merely frowned, glanced at the mess on his clothes, then waved his hand and spoke in a deep, steady voice:

"It's alright, little girl."

His appearance was intimidating, but his voice was gentle.

"You'd better be more careful in the future. Even if you're in a hurry, watch your step when you walk. It wouldn't be good if you bumped into an elderly person or a child."

"Alright, that's fine. I'll wash my clothes when I get home."

With that, he simply turned around and returned to his seat.

Sit at his table were several other burly men dressed similarly to him, all looking equally menacing.

But they all just glanced at him and continued eating, showing no intention of causing trouble.

Xia Feng raised an eyebrow in surprise.

Zhou Yingying breathed a sigh of relief, as if granted a pardon.

Xia Feng watched the bald, burly man's retreating figure.

He noticed that the men's breathing was deep and steady, their steps firm and measured, clearly indicating they were all trained fighters.

Moreover…

He could also sense a faint, palpable aura of steely ruthlessness emanating from them, an aura possessed only by those who had spent years teetering on the edge of life and death.

Xia Feng instantly made a judgment.

These people were definitely not street thugs; they seemed more like… former soldiers.

Since they didn't seem to be causing trouble, Xia Feng didn't want to get involved.

He patted Zhou Yingying on the shoulder, offering a reassuring word.

“Alright, it's okay now. Go clean this up.”

“Okay!”

Zhou Yingying gave Xia Feng a grateful look, quickly grabbed some tools, and deftly cleaned up the mess on the floor.

Then she ran to the cashier, insisting on paying for that table of customers as an apology.

Xia Feng watched her earnest expression and returned to his seat.

Soon, his noodles and dumplings arrived.

The aroma was enticing; it was that familiar taste.

Xia Feng ate while observing the table with the bald, burly man.

They ate with the discipline of soldiers, sitting upright, silent and quietly finishing their food.

Then, the bald, burly man led the way, getting up and going to the cashier to pay.

Upon learning that Zhou Yingying had already paid, he paused for a moment, then pulled a hundred-yuan bill from his pocket, insisted on giving it to the still-busy Zhou Yingying, and turned to leave with his men.

They didn't say a word the entire time.

After Xia Feng finished eating, the noodle shop gradually emptied, and Zhou Yingying finally had a chance to sit opposite him.

As soon as she sat down, she buried her face in her arms and began to sob.

"Ugh~ I almost wasted my whole day."

"But thankfully, that guy was a good person. He didn't hold me responsible and even left me the money. That's so kind of him."

Xia Feng, seeing her adorable, relieved expression, couldn't help but tease her:

"Yeah, looks like I judged him by his appearance today."

"I thought he'd be a rough, unpleasant guy, but he's actually so understanding."

He then changed the subject, lecturing the junior schoolmate.

"You too, you need to be more careful in the future.

You were lucky this time, you met a reasonable person.

Next time, if you encounter someone unreasonable, you'll be in for it."

"And most importantly, what if you fell and hurt yourself? Hospital visits are free, aren't they?"

Zhou Yingying looked up and nodded pitifully.

"Okay, senior, I'll definitely be more careful next time."

"Also... thank you for helping me earlier, senior, I..."

"Alright, alright."

Xia Feng waved his hand, interrupting her.

"If you really want to thank me, then hurry up and get back to work, go home and rest early.

Don't tire yourself out all day."

"Okay!"

Zhou Yingying nodded emphatically.

"Yingying! Get ready to clean up!"

The proprietress's voice came from the kitchen.

"Coming right up!"

Zhou Yingying immediately stood up from her seat and stuck her tongue out at Xia Feng.

"Then, senior, I'll go back to work."

"Go ahead, be careful."

"Okay~"

Watching her revitalized figure, Xia Feng shook his head and also got up and went to the cashier.

He had no intention of actually letting a younger female student treat him to a meal.

He took out his phone, scanned the QR code to pay, and then sent Zhou Yingyin a message:

[The noodles were delicious. I'll pay this time. Treat me again next time!]

After doing all this, he turned and left the little noodle shop filled with memories.



Chapter 31 Zhou Yingying's Inferiority Complex


It was 8 PM.

The noodle shop was almost empty. Zhou Yingying and the owner were clearing away the last dishes.

Once they were completely finished, she took off her slightly greasy work clothes, changed into her own, said goodbye to the owner, and prepared to go home.

She specifically told the owner, "Auntie, you can deduct the money from my salary for the handsome guy who was sitting by the window earlier."

The owner looked at this sensible and capable young woman, simply smiled and nodded, without saying anything more.

On her way home, the evening breeze carried a slight chill, dispelling her day's fatigue.

Zhou Yingying thought she should visit her grandmother at the hospital first, so she stopped at a fruit shop to buy some of her grandmother's favorite fruits.

She picked out a few large, red apples and was about to pay when she noticed an unread text message. It was from Xia Xuechang?

"The noodles were delicious. I'll pay this time. Treat me again next time!"

Looking at that short but thoughtful message on the screen, Zhou Yingying's lips unconsciously curled into a smile.

A warm, sweet feeling welled up inside her.

This Senior Xia… he's so kind!

After paying, she carried the fruit towards the hospital.

She took out her phone and reopened the text message, reading it over and over again, a silly smile on her face that she herself didn't even realize.

Before she knew it, she had arrived at the hospital.

The thought of Xia Feng paying for her grandmother's hospital and examination fees without a second thought made her girlish heart pound uncontrollably again.

This sum of money was an astronomical figure for her.

Yet he spoke of it so casually, without even mentioning it.

She didn't know how to repay such a debt of gratitude.

With these complex yet sweet feelings, she entered her grandmother's hospital room.

"Grandma, I'm here."

The elderly woman in the hospital bed was watching TV. Upon seeing her granddaughter, a kind smile immediately spread across her face.

"Yingying, you're here."

"Didn't I tell you to go home and rest after get off work? You don't need to come here every day. Grandma can manage on her own."

Zhou Yingying placed the fruit she was carrying on the bedside table and went over to tuck her grandmother in.

"What are you saying, Grandma? You're my only family now. How could I not come to see you?"

She picked up two apples, washed them at the small sink in the hospital room, then took a small knife and sat back down on the stool beside the bed, carefully peeling the apples.

As she peeled an apple, she enthusiastically shared her day's adventures with her grandmother.

"Oh, right, Grandma, I ran into Brother Xia again at the shop today!"

"You know what? Brother Xia was actually my senior from the same university, also in the Computer Science department! But he graduated several years ago."

Once Xia Feng was mentioned, Zhou Yingying's chatterbox completely opened up, and she talked non-stop about everything related to him.

Her bright eyes seemed to sparkle, and her face brightened considerably.

"He was such a nice guy, handsome, capable, and incredibly gentle..."

The old woman watched her granddaughter with a beaming smile, listening to her endless praise of the young man named Xia Feng.

As someone with experience, how could she not understand?

This girl had fallen for him.

She waited until Zhou Yingying finished speaking before slowly and bluntly asking:

"Yingying, you've taken a liking to Xia Feng?"

"Grandma! You...you're saying that!"

Zhou Yingying blushed at her grandmother's direct words, her hands pausing, almost cutting her finger.

She lowered her head, flustered, and explained:

"I...I didn't...I just think he's a very good person, a benefactor to us..."

But as she spoke, her voice grew softer and softer, and the light on her face gradually dimmed.

Yes...

Even if she really liked him, what could she do?

"Xia Xue-chang and I are from completely different worlds."

Her voice carried a bitterness she herself hadn't even noticed.

"I'm just an ordinary girl. My family is poor, and I have to work hard to earn my tuition and living expenses. I'm just average-looking, nothing special..."

"How could someone as outstanding as him possibly be interested in me?"

As she spoke, she thought of the heavy medical bills.

She said she would repay them, but after paying tuition and basic necessities, there was practically nothing left of what she earned each month.

Repaying the money seemed like a distant dream.

The gap... was simply too vast.

Seeing her granddaughter's sudden dejection, the old woman felt a pang of heartache and helplessness.

What could she say?

It was indeed the truth.

Both grandmother and granddaughter knew their family's situation perfectly well.

Her daughter-in-law and son died in a car accident several years ago, leaving her and her granddaughter Zhou Yingying to depend on each other.

For years, they've barely managed to survive on her meager pension and Yingying's odd jobs.

Now, her mother is hospitalized due to health reasons, further exacerbating their financial situation.

Alas…it's truly been hard on Yingying.

The old woman reached out her withered hand, still attached to an IV drip, and gently stroked Zhou Yingying's head, as if offering silent comfort.

Zhou Yingying composed herself, peeled the apple, and carefully cut it into small pieces with a knife. She picked up a piece with a toothpick and fed it to her grandmother.

"Grandma, eat an apple."

"Okay."

The grandmother and granddaughter shared the two apples.

The apple's sweetness seemed to gradually soothe the bitterness in their hearts.

Could she really repay Senior Xia's favor?

Zhou Yingying wondered silently.

...

Meanwhile.

Xia Feng didn't drive his Maybach; instead, he chose to walk alone through the streets of Jiangcheng.

He hadn't enjoyed this kind of peaceful solitude in a long time.

Ever since that cunning little vixen, Liu Ruyan, tricked him, his life had completely ended his single life.

Every day was sweet and blissful, with women on both sides, carefree and happy.

He had to admit, this was the happiest and most fulfilling period of his life since leaving the Lin family.

As he walked, thinking of his two stunningly beautiful wives, a gentle smile unconsciously crept onto his lips.

Wandering around, he didn't even know how he got there; he found himself in a seemingly remote, almost deserted old town.

The buildings here were very old, with peeling paint, tangled electrical wires like spiderwebs, and a damp, decaying smell permeated the air.

"How did I get here?"

Xia Feng looked at the unfamiliar surroundings and shook his head with amusement.

"Never mind, let's go back.

Qingxue should be off work by now; I need to pick her up. I'll try my luck with the lucky draw prize tonight, hehe."

Just as he was about to turn away,

a strange sound suddenly came from a dark alley not far away.

The sound was dull, like a heavy object striking flesh, mixed with a few suppressed groans.

Xia Feng frowned.

Driven by curiosity, he tiptoed silently toward the direction the sound came from.

His control over his body was now far beyond that of ordinary people.

His movements were almost silent.

He slipped behind a large trash can and peeked into the alley.

The next second, his eyes narrowed slightly.

Deep in the alley, under the dim streetlights, a fierce battle was unfolding!

On one side were the bald, burly man he had encountered at the noodle shop earlier that day and his gang.

Their opponents were a group of thugs who looked menacing, covered in various ferocious tattoos, and armed with steel pipes, machetes, and other weapons.

Although the other side outnumbered them and were armed...

But the bald, burly man and his gang were holding their own.

Their movements were clean and efficient, their teamwork seamless, every punch and kick brimming with explosive power!

With each strike, a thug would scream and fall to the ground!

It was a one-sided massacre!

Xia Feng watched this scene unfold without any intention of intervening.

Clearly, the bald, burly man and his gang were more than capable of handling it.



Chapter 32 The Masked Man in Stockings


But two fists can't fight four hands.

Although the bald, burly man and his brothers were all formidable fighters, each capable of taking on ten men, they were simply outnumbered!

The twenty-odd armed thugs charged forward like mad dogs, wave after wave!

Gradually, all four men began to show signs of injury, and their strength began to wane.

After struggling for a few more minutes, the bald, burly man finally succumbed to the sheer number of opponents, exhausted, when a steel pipe slammed into his back.

Soon, the four men were bound tightly with rough ropes and roughly shoved in front of two men.

One of them was the arrogant-looking man in the suit, "Tiger."

The other man, wearing a similar black vest to the bald, burly man, was equally imposing, but his eyes were filled with evasiveness and fear.

"Hey, officers, you've been chasing me for so long, and in the end you still fell for me?"

The burly man, Tiger, wore a smug, arrogant smile. He pulled a cigar from his pocket, lit it, and slowly exhaled a smoke ring.

"Why did you have to do this? Wouldn't it have been better if we'd kept to ourselves and lived in peace?"

The four burly men completely ignored him, staring intently at the man in the same vest, their eyes filled with anger and disbelief.

The bald man's voice was filled with disappointment and heartache.

"Dog, why did you betray your brothers?"

The man called "Dog" gave a bitter look.

"Brother Lei, I... I didn't want to..."

His voice sounded full of helplessness.

“But…but Tiger offered way too much, I…I had no choice!”

Upon uttering these words, the other three men, except for the bald giant, spat bloody saliva onto the ground!

“Pah! Shameless bastard!”

“Dog, you’re trash! For a few stinking bucks, you’ve forgotten your identity and mission!”

“What about the oath we swore together? Did you feed it to the dogs?!”

Hearing his brothers’ angry curses, the man called Mad Dog stopped pretending to be bitter; his expression instantly twisted and became ferocious.

“Heh, honor? Mission?”

He sneered, his tone filled with disdain.

The bald, burly man, seeing his ugly face, finally felt utterly disheartened.

He slowly closed his eyes, no longer looking at him, no longer wanting to say another word.

...

Hiding in the shadows, Xia Feng finally understood the situation completely.

It turned out that during the pursuit of the criminal, a traitor had emerged in the team, and the other side had turned the tables on them.

Since that Tiger Lord was a bad guy, things were much easier.

A cold smile curled at the corner of Xia Feng's lips.

Perfect timing! I haven't even had a chance to test the effects of my newly acquired [Ancient Martial Arts] skill yet!

Today, I'll use you bunch of blind trash as my starting point!

Four points went into Strength, bringing his Strength attribute to 16.

Three points went into Speed, bringing his Speed ​​attribute to 15.

After doing all this, he felt an explosive surge of power coursing through his body!

Then, he took something out of his system space.

Capture the leader first!

A clean, swift chop to the back of his thick neck!

A few quick swishes!

The ropes binding the four burly men snapped!

He used the back of the blade.

With a swift, decisive motion!

One strike, one kill!

Each blow landed precisely on the back of the neck, the force perfectly controlled—enough to incapacitate them instantly without causing fatal damage.

In the blink of an eye, seven or eight thugs lay screaming on the ground!

"Brothers! Let's get them!"

Items won through the system lottery could be stored in the system space, but this space could only store items produced by the system; nothing else could be stored.

Chapter 33 Ranking Up

I'm all alone at home...

A lone man and woman...

Could it be...?

The thought of that possibility sent a jolt of color through her pale face, flushed from staying up all night!

Far from feeling any resistance, she felt a small surge of anticipation.

"Um... I'll lead the way."

She pulled away from Xia Feng's grasp and walked quickly ahead, like a dutiful little guide.

Soon, they arrived at Zhou Yingying's house.

Opening the door, a warm yet slightly worn atmosphere wafted out.

Xia Feng glanced at the small, but clean and tidy, little house.

There wasn't even a decent sofa in the living room, just a few old wooden chairs.

"Where's your room?"

"Huh?!"

This...this is too fast!

Too...too direct!

We haven't even...we haven't even built up any feelings yet!

"This...is it so urgent?"

Her face flushed, her voice barely a whisper.

"Well...okay...it's over there..."

She pointed a trembling finger to a closed door beside her.

Xia Feng nodded and walked over, pushing open the door.

Zhou Yingying, like a shy bride, followed him inside, her face still red.

The room wasn't large, and the furnishings were simple.

A single bed, a desk, and a wardrobe.

Her desk was piled high with various study materials and textbooks; it was clear she was a diligent student.

"Lie down on it."

What on earth was going on in this junior's head?!

"I can't be gentle."

His voice held a hint of teasing.

“Today, I’m going to teach you a lesson about the consequences of not taking care of your body.”

“Ah—!”

A sharp pain instantly shot through her entire body from her back!

“It hurts! Senior! Be gentle! It hurts so much!”

“That’s good, it hurts!”

“I can tell you didn’t sleep again last night! You look like someone about to die!”

“Ah! It hurts! Waaah~ It hurts!”

Zhou Yingying cried out in pain, tears streaming down her face, her body twisting and struggling.

But her strength was like an ant trying to shake a tree in front of Xia Feng's large hands; it was utterly useless.

Five minutes later.

Just when Zhou Yingying felt like her back was about to be crushed by his pressure,

Xia Feng's strength suddenly changed.

The intense pain disappeared, replaced by a warm and comfortable sensation.

Xia Feng's touch softened, gently kneading the aching acupoints on her body.

"Mmm~"

"Mmm...right...right there..."

This sudden, intense pleasure made Zhou Yingying let out a comfortable moan.

"It hurt a little just now, but the therapeutic effect was the best."

Xia Feng's voice came from above.

"Now, this kind of technique that makes you feel good isn't as effective."

"Hmph, Senior is bullying me!"

Zhou Yingying softly complained.

"You bad boy, I'm ignoring you!"

Xia Feng pretended not to hear, continuing to methodically regulate the disordered Qi and blood in her body caused by staying up late.

Combined with some ancient martial arts health techniques, his massage not only healed physical fatigue and damage but also nourished her vitality.

Half an hour later.

Having completed the entire process, Xia Feng finally withdrew his hand, satisfied.

He looked down.

Zhou Yingying was already lying on the bed, fast asleep.

Her breathing was even, and a faint, contented smile even graced her lips.



Chapter 37 Zhou Yingying's Thoughts


When Zhou Yingying woke up again, it was already noon.

Sunlight streamed in through the old window.

She felt as if she had slept for a very long time, a sleep sweeter and more restful than ever before.

Upon waking, she felt an inexhaustible energy coursing through her body; the feeling of immense ease made her stretch comfortably.

Over the years, juggling her studies and several part-time jobs, her body had been in a constant state of high-intensity fatigue, plagued by various minor ailments.

But now, all that accumulated fatigue and aches seemed to have been completely swept away after this sleep!

Immediately afterward, a rich and enticing aroma of food wafted in through the crack in the door, relentlessly assaulting her sense of smell.

Zhou Yingying's stomach rumbled loudly, much to her dismay.

Following the aroma, she curiously stepped out of her room.

And then she saw a scene she would never forget.

In the cramped kitchen, a tall, imposing figure stood before the stove, wearing an ill-fitting apron, busily working with practiced ease.

His movements—tossing the wok, chopping vegetables—were so skillful and natural.

The afternoon sun streamed through the small kitchen window, falling perfectly on him, bathing his earnest and handsome profile in a warm golden glow.

At that moment, Zhou Yingying felt her heart skip a beat.

All eyes were captivated by the man before her.

Xia Feng had already sensed the movement behind him; he knew Zhou Yingying had woken up.

"You're awake."

He chuckled and waved his hand in front of her.

"What's wrong? Still not awake?"

Zhou Yingying snapped out of her daze, her pretty face flushing crimson!

She quickly lowered her head, her long, flowing hair tracing a smooth arc in the air, obscuring her burning cheeks.

Obediently, she ran to the side and grabbed two clean bowls, then carried the entire inner pot of the rice cooker to the small dining table outside.

Having done all this, she pulled out a chair and sat down.

But instead of serving the rice, she rested her chin on her hands, tilting her head to the side and quietly watching the figure still busy in the kitchen.

The smile on her face never faded.

Her mind began to wander uncontrollably to all sorts of fantasies.

Xia Feng, cooking for her in the kitchen, became her husband.

And she was the little wife, happily waiting to be fed by her husband.

After dinner, they could hold hands and stroll in the park, just like any ordinary, happy young couple.

Thinking about it, Zhou Yingying shyly covered her face, fidgeting nervously in her chair.

As soon as he came out, he saw Zhou Yingying's adorable face-covering expression, seemingly blushing for some unknown reason, and a big question mark appeared on his mind.

Xia Feng's words finally snapped Zhou Yingying out of her reverie.

The next second, her eyes widened instantly!

"Waaah...it's so delicious!"

She felt she'd never eaten anything so good in her life!

Xia Feng, seeing her exaggeratedly moved expression, almost to tears, shook his head, half-laughing and half-crying.

"Alright, alright, stop praising me."

"I don't care! I just think it's delicious!"

Zhou Yingying shoveled rice into her mouth, mumbling her protest.

"Yes, yes, whatever makes you happy."

Xia Feng also picked up his chopsticks and started eating.

The two simplest home-style dishes were quickly devoured by the two of them.

After finishing their meal, Zhou Yingying volunteered to clean up all the dishes and utensils, preparing to take them to the kitchen to wash.

Seeing her virtuous demeanor, Xia Feng confidently entrusted this task to her.

After all, Zhou Yingying had to take care of her grandmother, unlike Liu Ruyan, a kitchen disaster who never lifted a finger.

Xia Feng, meanwhile, sat comfortably in his chair and took out his phone.

He first sent a message to Su Qingxue, reminding her to eat lunch on time.

Then he sent a text message to Liu Ruyan, who was on a business trip in a neighboring city, to check on her and ask if she was coming home that evening.

He quickly received a positive reply.

After doing all this, he opened the familiar short video app and started scrolling.

Zhou Yingying quickly finished washing the dishes.

She dried her hands and came out of the kitchen, only to see Xia Feng leaning back in his chair, engrossed in watching short videos.

Curious, she leaned closer to see what he was watching.

Just as she got closer, a video of a scantily clad, hot young woman dancing seductively to the camera appeared on the screen.

Zhou Yingying's face flushed crimson!

"Where's your comb? Let me comb your hair for you."

"Ah? Oh... okay!"

Hearing Xia Feng offer to comb her hair, Zhou Yingying was first stunned, then overjoyed!

She quickly turned and ran back to her room, retrieved her small wooden comb that she'd used for years, and handed it to Xia Feng with both hands.

Then she obediently pulled up a chair and sat down with her back to Xia Feng.

Her docile appearance was like a kitten waiting to be petted by its owner.

Xia Feng took the comb and began skillfully combing her long, smooth, black hair.

He often combed Liu Ruyan's and Su Qingxue's hair at home, so it was already second nature to him.

He could feel Zhou Yingying's initially tense body gradually relax under his touch, even closing her eyes in comfort.

Soon, her long, smooth hair was neatly combed.

Xia Feng then picked up a hair tie and skillfully tied it into a low ponytail.

Then he gently draped the black ponytail over her left shoulder.

Looking at the junior schoolmate in the mirror, who had instantly transformed back into a gentle, domestic, and utterly wifely woman, Xia Feng nodded in satisfaction.

Yes, that's the look.



Chapter 38 Helping Zhou Yingying Find Her Way

Zhou Yingying's ears picked up on that key phrase.

Chapter 41 Women are all born actresses


Finally, Xia Feng carried the barefoot girl, whose feet were covered in sand and making it difficult to wear shoes, on his back.

Zhou Yingying nestled against Xia Feng's broad, sturdy back, her arms wrapped around his neck.

Her cheek was pressed tightly against the back of his neck, and she could clearly feel the warmth of his skin and the steady, powerful beating of his heart.

Her weight was only slightly less than Liu Ruyan's!
