But I have to take Yingying home first, then I'll go home later and tell Ruyan, and we'll go together then."

"No need! No need for Sister Ruyan to come along!"

Su Qingxue quickly said.

"My dad told me to take you back, so Sister Ruyan doesn't need to go. Otherwise, my dad will definitely interrogate her for ages."

Xia Feng thought about it and agreed.

He'd choose a strategy with fewer comments.

"Okay, whatever you say."

Su Qingxue was even happier: "Okay! It's settled then!"

She excitedly swung her legs.

"Speaking of which, it's my first time meeting my future father-in-law. Should I bring a gift? Maybe... a couple of bottles of Moutai?"

"No, no need."

Su Qingxue immediately said.

“My dad is so rich, he doesn’t lack anything, and he won’t care about these little bits and pieces. Just go.”

She thought for a moment, then added, “If it really doesn’t work, just bring a pack of Zhonghua cigarettes; my dad likes them.”

“But… honey, you don’t smoke, so never mind, let’s just bring a bottle of Moutai.”

"Got it! I'll buy the most expensive Moutai on my way tonight!"

Xia Feng smiled and agreed, then joked,

"Speaking of which, will my father-in-law be unhappy to see this blond-haired guy who stole his precious daughter, and then kick me out with a broom?"

Su Qingxue playfully retorted,

"I don't care! You'll have to make a good impression then! But I believe in you, my husband is so outstanding, my dad will definitely love him!"

"Okay, we'll see how I do then."

As they spoke, the massage was coming to an end.

Xia Feng's large hand lightly patted Su Qingxue's pert spot.

"All done, you can get up now, my dear Boss Su."

"You're so annoying!"

Su Qingxue's pretty face flushed red as she turned her head and scolded playfully.

"You keep patting me there, I feel like you've made it bigger!"

Xia Feng raised an eyebrow, leaned close to her ear, and chuckled in his magnetic voice:

"Heh, I wonder who it was last night, that wouldn't let me pat them, insisting on pulling my hand up there?"

"You…!"

Su Qingxue's face instantly turned red to the roots of her neck, the embarrassing scenes from last night flooding her mind.

She sprang up from the sofa, fled the cubicle without looking back, sat back in her boss's chair, and pretended to be seriously reviewing documents.

Xia Feng watched her fleeing figure, shaking his head with a smile.

He also returned to his seat, turned on his computer, and began to continue optimizing the game he was developing.

His fingers danced across the keyboard, lines of code flowing down like a waterfall.

He plans to lower the game's performance requirements to the lowest level currently available on the market.

This way, even gamers with older computers will be able to run the game smoothly.

He wants this game to take the market by storm!



Chapter 45 Tell her loudly, let her be the victim.


At noon, most of the office staff had already gone out to find lunch.

Only from the innermost office could one faintly hear the rapid, almost torrential, tapping of keyboards.

Xia Feng's eyes were fixed on the computer screen, completely immersed in the world of data.

His brain was like a supercomputer running at full power, countless lines of code and data flashing before his eyes, then being organized, analyzed, and optimized at an astonishing speed.

Ever since acquiring those two top-tier programming and hacking skills, he had fallen in love with this feeling.

This feeling of having everything firmly in his grasp was simply amazing!

"Knock, knock, knock."

A gentle knock came at the office door.

"Come in."

It was Su Qingxue who responded.

The door opened, and a petite figure quietly entered.

It was Zhou Yingying.

She spotted the man diligently working behind his desk at a glance, her bright eyes instantly sparkling.

He looks so handsome when he's focused.

Without making a sound, she tiptoed in, intending to wait quietly.

Then she heard a soft "hmm~" from beside her.

The voice carried a hint of languidness and allure.

Zhou Yingying instinctively turned her gaze.

In another executive chair, a stunningly beautiful woman, seemingly approachable, was stretching, relaxing her body, which had become stiff from sitting all morning.

Today, she had playfully styled her long, glossy black hair into two cute buns, making her already delicate face appear even more charming.

But in stark contrast to this adorable hairstyle was the same business suit she wore—the same one Liu Ruyan wore—a suit exuding an air of restraint and sophistication.

Even more damning was the way she stretched, which stretched her white silk blouse to its limit!

It looked as if it were about to burst out of the fabric, creating a breathtaking visual impact!

Zhou Yingying subconsciously looked down at herself.

Beneath the loose white short-sleeved shirt lay her prized asset.

While not large, it wasn't small either.

She had secretly measured it herself; she was just a tiny bit short of officially entering the realm of a D-level expert!

But compared to the approachable Boss Su, who was only at the E-level…

Only one thought remained in Zhou Yingying's mind.

Utterly and completely defeated!

A wave of frustration instantly washed over her.

Su Qingxue, having finished stretching, also noticed Zhou Yingying's arrival.

She naturally saw the other woman's subtle gesture of first looking at herself, then down at Zhou Yingying herself.

Su Qingxue saw clearly the shock, envy, and fleeting inferiority in her eyes.

A slight chuckle rose in her heart.

This junior was quite cute.

"Pfft."

Su Qingxue couldn't help but chuckle softly.

This soft chuckle snapped Zhou Yingying out of her reverie, her pretty face instantly turning bright red!

"Hello... Boss Su!"

She quickly and respectfully greeted Su Qingxue.

"I... I'm Zhou Yingying, the new girl here today..."

Her voice was barely a whisper, filled with restraint and unease, even a hint of guilt.

After all…

she was the wicked woman who coveted someone else's husband!

Wasn't this the behavior of a mistress, universally condemned?!

Su Qingxue took in her mistress-like demeanor upon seeing the wife, her smile widening.

Yes, spending so much time with Xia Feng, she'd picked up that wicked sense of humor too.

She cleared her throat, trying to make her voice sound authoritative and aloof.

"Ahem."

She gestured to the small sofa in the office used for receiving guests.

"Come, let's sit over there and chat."

"Yes! Yes!"

Zhou Yingying nodded like a chick pecking at rice, taking tiny steps to one of the single sofas, placing her hands on her knees, sitting ramrod straight, her posture impeccably dignified.

Su Qingxue walked gracefully to the seat opposite her.

She casually crossed her long, slender legs, encased in smooth black stockings.

The delicate high heels on her feet swayed with her movements, like pounding on Zhou Yingying's already pounding heart.

Zhou Yingying lowered her head even further, almost burying it in the soft depths of her chest.

This Boss Su's aura… is too strong!

Su Qingxue looked at her cowering like a quail and nodded with satisfaction.

Hmm, very good, the first step of intimidation was successful.

Next…

She spoke slowly, her voice cold.

She dropped a bombshell right from the start!

"I heard you like my husband?"

BOOM—!!!

Zhou Yingying's mind went blank, a complete void!

"I...I..."

She opened her mouth, but couldn't utter a single word, only feeling her cheeks burning hot.

Su Qingxue gave her no chance to catch her breath, continuing to press her with that oppressive tone:

"Do you know he's already married?"

Zhou Yingying's brain finally started functioning again.

She took a deep breath, as if using all her strength, to make her voice sound less trembling.

"I...I know...I know my senior is married."

"But..."

"Hmph."

Su Qingxue snorted coldly, directly interrupting her.

"Knowing that, you still dared to announce so loudly in front of the whole company that you were pursuing him?"

"You've got some nerve."

Su Qingxue's words were like a bucket of cold water poured over Zhou Yingying's head.

Her face, which had just flushed, paled even more instantly.

But this time, she didn't back down.

She raised her head, her bright eyes flashing with determination and stubbornness.

She met Su Qingxue's scrutinizing gaze head-on without flinching.

"I...I know what I'm doing is wrong!"

"But my feelings for my senior are real! I...I really can't suppress them!"

"And..."

Her voice grew louder and more resolute.

"I don't need him to give me any title, nor do I need him to do anything for me!"

"Even if I can't be by his side..."

"But just being able to quietly watch him, protect him, is enough for me!"

Looking at the girl before her, whose body was trembling slightly with nervousness yet who still mustered all her courage,

Su Qingxue couldn't help but think of her past self.

Wasn't she once like that?

Carefully hiding her feelings of love in her heart, afraid to let anyone know.

Feeling that being by his side every day was the greatest happiness.

If only she had possessed that courage and drive back then.

Even just a little bit.

Would she and Xia Feng already be happily married, with children old enough to run errands?

Su Qingxue quietly watched her, her gaze becoming complex.

That sharp scrutiny gradually softened into tenderness and heartache.

In the end, Zhou Yingying was the first to give in.

In front of the legal wife, she loudly declared that she would be the mistress, making her the victim.

This was simply outrageous!

Her skin wasn't thick enough to back it up.

Feeling a little guilty, she slowly shifted her gaze.

But the instant she looked away,

she heard Su Qingxue's familiar soft laugh again.

"Pfft."

Zhou Yingying looked up in confusion, only to see Su Qingxue looking at her with an amused expression.

"Hey, little sister."

Su Qingxue's expression shifted to a teasing one, as if she wanted to continue testing her.

"If in the end, my husband is just playing around with you, and dumps you when he's bored, what will you do?"

"Impossible!"

Zhou Yingying blurted out without thinking!

She looked up again, staring at Su Qingxue with unwavering certainty.

"My senior could never be that kind of person!"

"He's had so many opportunities to take advantage of me before!

Even yesterday, I practically threw myself at him, even suggested we go to a hotel, but he still took me home!"

"I...I still have my first kiss!"

"And..."

She looked at Su Qingxue, her tone brimming with wisdom as she turned the tables.

"If my senior were really that kind of heartless scumbag, then I think someone as outstanding as you, Boss Su, would never even be interested in him, right?"

Su Qingxue was stunned.

She looked at this junior student before her, whose thinking was clear, whose logic was meticulous, and who could even praise her in return.

Finally, genuine approval and recognition appeared in her eyes.

How long had they known each other? Less than half a month, right?

This Zhou Yingying, she actually understood Xia Feng's personality so thoroughly!

Interesting.

She slowly stood up from the sofa and sat down next to Zhou Yingying.

Under Zhou Yingying's nervous yet curious gaze, Su Qingxue suddenly reached out and ruffled her hair, her voice becoming incredibly gentle.

"From now on, call me Sister Qingxue."

"No need to call me Boss Su anymore, it's too formal."

"Huh?"

Zhou Yingying was completely dumbfounded.

A big question mark slowly appeared above her head.

What...what's going on?

This plot development is completely different from what she imagined!

Shouldn't it be a scene of the main wife battling the mistress, being publicly humiliated, and then being kicked out?

Why is she suddenly being asked to call her "sister"?

But she still tentatively called out softly in an uncertain tone.

"Sister Qingxue?"

"Eh~ So good."

Su Qingxue smiled, her eyes crinkling, a satisfied smile exactly like Liu Ruyan's back then.

No wonder Sister Ruyan made me call her "sister" the moment we met; this feeling…

It really is quite nice!



Chapter 46 Because I'm a loser too


Su Qingxue was overjoyed by Zhou Yingying's address of "Sister Qingxue," but she was just about to say something when...

*Gurgle, gurgle—*

An untimely, embarrassing sound suddenly came from Zhou Yingying's stomach.

"!!!"

Zhou Yingying's pretty face flushed crimson from her neck to her ears!

She quickly covered her stomach with both hands, wishing she could disappear into the ground!

Ugh~ How embarrassing!

Why did her stomach have to growl at this moment!

And in front of Sister Qingxue, so incredibly embarrassing!

Su Qingxue, seeing her adorable expression of wanting to die on the spot, was about to tease her.

*Gurgle, gurgle—*

An even louder sound came from her own stomach.

Su Qingxue: "..."

Zhou Yingying: "..."

The two stared at each other, and the atmosphere in the office became extremely awkward.

Su Qingxue's face flushed slightly.

No wonder, she had engaged in over three hours of intense exercise last night, which had taken a toll on her.

She hadn't eaten much this morning, so it was normal for her stomach to be growling.

"Ahem."

Su Qingxue coughed lightly, breaking the awkward silence.

She stood up confidently from the sofa and took Zhou Yingying's hand.

"Come on, Yingying, let me take you downstairs to get some yummy food. We'll come up and eat together."

"Okay...okay."

Zhou Yingying was still immersed in the subtle atmosphere from earlier, her mind blank, and could only nod subconsciously.

Then, Su Qingxue led her out of the office.

The two arrived at the small restaurant downstairs from the company building that she and Xia Feng often frequented.

The owner of the restaurant was a very enthusiastic middle-aged man. As soon as he saw Su Qingxue enter, he immediately greeted her with a beaming smile.

"Oh, Mr. Su, you're here so early today?"

He glanced at the pretty, white-stockinged junior schoolmate beside Su Qingxue, his eyes lighting up.

"Bringing a new colleague to dinner today?"

"Yes."

Su Qingxue smiled and nodded, expertly ordering.

"Boss, the usual, one sweet and sour pork ribs, one stir-fried pork with green peppers, one shredded pork with garlic sauce, and one side of garlic greens."

"Pack them all up for me, I'll take them upstairs."

"Alright! Please wait a moment!"

The boss quickly went to the kitchen to place the order.

Su Qingxue pulled Zhou Yingying to a clean table nearby and waited patiently.

After this period of adjustment, Zhou Yingying's mind finally started working again.

Looking at Mr. Su, who was friendly, even affectionate, towards her, she finally couldn't help but ask the question that had been nagging at her.

"Um... Sister Qingxue... why?"

Her voice was soft, filled with confusion.

She couldn't understand.

She was a complete homewrecker! The third party who came to steal her boyfriend!

Why... why wasn't she hostile towards her at all?

She even called her "little sister" so affectionately and dragged her to dinner?

Su Qingxue looked at her beautiful eyes filled with confusion and simply smiled mysteriously.

"What why?"

"Why...why are you suddenly being so nice to me?"

Zhou Yingying mustered her courage and looked directly into Su Qingxue's eyes.

"I...I'm a mistress! I'm a bad woman who likes my senior!"

Hearing her frank yet somewhat naive words, Su Qingxue finally couldn't help but chuckle.

She reached out and affectionately pinched Zhou Yingying's small nose, then leaned close to her ear and whispered in a voice only the two of them could hear:

"Because..."

"I'm a third party too."

BOOM—!!!

This sentence stunned her completely!

I...I'm a third party too?!

What...what does this mean?

Is this even Chinese?!

She stared blankly at Su Qingxue, her mind filled with question marks, feeling as if her worldview was about to collapse.

"But...but...I clearly heard my senior say with his own ears that you're his wife! What...what's going on?"

Seeing Zhou Yingying's adorably bewildered expression, Su Qingxue stopped teasing her.

She slowly recounted the story of her relationship with Xia Feng and Liu Ruyan, in detail.

From her eight years of unrequited love for Xia Feng, to the heartbreak and resentment when Liu Ruyan beat her to it.

From her resolute decision to withdraw completely, only to have Liu Ruyan unexpectedly approach her and invite her to join her and Xia Feng's family.

And finally, to their current three-way relationship.

Zhou Yingying listened quietly, her expression constantly shifting with Su Qingxue's narration.

Shock, astonishment, sympathy, envy...

Finally, after hearing the whole story,

she finally understood why Su Qingxue's gaze had held such complex emotions.

That was the look of someone looking at their own kind!

Zhou Yingying spoke tentatively, her voice tinged with uncertainty.

"So... Sister Qingxue means... you... you agree to me pursuing my senior?"

"Yes."

Su Qingxue nodded without hesitation.

"But... but why?"

Zhou Yingying was still puzzled.

"Why would Sister Qingxue, and that Sister Ruyan, agree to... something like this?"

"The reason is simple."

Su Qingxue held up two slender, white fingers.

"First of all, like I just said, I'm actually a failure in relationships."

Her voice held a hint of self-deprecation.

"I liked him for so many years, but in the end, I still lost to someone else."

"I'm already very content to have this opportunity to be by his side."

"So, having you here or not, it really makes no difference to me."

"Secondly, and most importantly..."

Su Qingxue's face suddenly showed lingering fear and...resentment?

Zhou Yingying tilted her head, asking with some confusion.

"You mean...that senior's work ability is very strong?"

In this naive girl's mind, which still only had theoretical knowledge, she subconsciously interpreted it as referring to professional skills.

Seeing Zhou Yingying's innocent and adorable expression, Su Qingxue was amused once again.

She leaned close to Zhou Yingying's ear.

As Zhou Yingying listened, her already fair face visibly flushed, from her cheeks to her ears, and then to her neck.

Finally, it seemed as if white steam was rising from the top of her head.

"?!"

Her voice stammered.

Su Qingxue, seeing her almost bursting with embarrassment, nodded emphatically, a look of lingering fear on her face.

She patted Zhou Yingying's shoulder, giving her a "you're still too young, little sister" look.

"Boss Su! Your food is ready!"

Just then, the boss's booming voice came from the kitchen.

"As usual, I've increased the portions for you! Plenty to go!"

Su Qingxue smiled, got up, and went over to pick up the several packed lunch boxes.

"Thank you so much, boss! I wish you booming business!"

Then, she pulled Zhou Yingying, who was still in shock, along with her back to the company.

On the way back, they passed a convenience store.

Zhou Yingying, almost without thinking, grabbed Su Qingxue's arm.

"Sister, wait for me!"

She ran into the store and bought an ice-cold Coke.

She wanted to take it back for her senior.

Hmm, he should like it, right?



Chapter 47 Su Qingxue, who provides the assist


When the two women returned, the atmosphere in the office was completely different.

Just a dozen minutes ago, Zhou Yingying had been trembling like a frightened rabbit in front of Su Qingxue.

Now, the two chatted and laughed like longtime best friends, radiating an aura of mutual appreciation.

When they pushed open the office door again, they saw the same figure still working.

Xia Feng was still sitting behind his desk, completely immersed in the data world composed of 0s and 1s.

He was the sole god in this world, controlling everything, changing everything.

Zhou Yingying's eyes sparkled uncontrollably once more.

His serious expression was so handsome!

Just then, a bold and playful idea suddenly popped into her head.

She turned her head, tugged at Su Qingxue's sleeve, and asked softly, with a tone of anticipation and excitement:

"Sister Qingxue, is it okay if I play a little prank on my senior?"

"A prank?"

Su Qingxue paused for a moment, then understood her little scheme.

A doting smile, tinged with amusement, appeared on her face.

"Of course, no problem! Go ahead and do it."

"But... you'll have to bear the consequences."

"Hehe, I know!"

With her sister's permission, Zhou Yingying's courage instantly grew.

Carrying the bottle of cola still glistening with cold droplets, she tiptoed to Xia Feng's side like a kitten about to launch a sneak attack.

Looking at his handsome profile, completely absorbed in his gaze, her eyes almost overflowed with infatuation.

The next second, she reached out her small hand and gently pressed the chilled Coke bottle against Xia Feng's cheek.

"Hiss—!"

Xia Feng's body jolted violently, as if he'd been electrocuted!

The data world in his eyes instantly collapsed, his consciousness forcibly pulled back to reality.

He turned his head somewhat blankly and saw the culprit.

Zhou Yingying stood prettily beside him, holding a Coke in one hand and the other behind her back, a sweet yet slightly smug smile on her face.

"Senior, it's time to eat~"

Her voice was soft and sweet, like a marshmallow coated in honey.

Looking at Xia Feng's stunned and frightened expression, Zhou Yingying felt as if she had done something incredibly exciting; her heart was pounding!

Xia Feng glanced around the office and then noticed that Su Qingxue had already opened the packed meals on the table next to the small sofa.

Even the chopsticks were laid out, just waiting for him to come and eat.

He glanced at the time in the bottom right corner of the computer screen.

[12:36]

It was already this late.

He took the cola from Zhou Yingying, stood up from his chair, and stretched languidly, a series of cracking sounds coming from his bones.

"Thanks, Yingying."

He pulled the tab on the can and tilted his head back to take a large gulp.

The cool, bubbly liquid slid down his throat, instantly washing away the fatigue from his intense concentration.

"Burp—"

Xia Feng let out a satisfied burp, looked at Zhou Yingying, and asked curiously,

"How did you know I like cola?"

Zhou Yingying put her hands behind her back, tilted her head slightly, and winked playfully.

"Hehe, I just suddenly thought that you work so hard, you must be very tired. Drinking some ice-cold cola would be very comforting, so I bought it."

"Looks like... I did the right thing."

As soon as she finished speaking, she reached out and grabbed Xia Feng's large hand, pulling him towards the small sofa.

"Senior, it's time to eat. Not eating on time will harm your health."

Xia Feng felt the softness and warmth of her hand and let her lead him over.

The three of them sat down at the small table, forming a triangle.

Xia Feng looked at the two stunningly beautiful women opposite him who had suddenly become so close, and felt incredibly pleased.

But he still asked with some curiosity:

"Is it just my imagination?"

"How come you two seem so close in such a short time?"

"Yes."

Su Qingxue smiled brightly as she put food into Xia Feng's bowl.

"I had a good chat with our Yingying just now."

"I already told her we don't mind her joining our family."

"Yes, yes!"

Zhou Yingying nodded quickly, like a kitten trying to please its owner.

"Sister Qingxue said she doesn't mind me! Then, senior, you..."

She looked at Xia Feng expectantly, her eyes seeming to say, "Say yes! Say yes!"

"..."

Xia Feng watched the two women's back-and-forth, feeling utterly overwhelmed.

What could he say?

He could only bury his head in his food and remain silent.

Seeing Xia Feng's neither-refusal-nor-acceptance stance, Zhou Yingying's cheeks immediately puffed out in anger.

Su Qingxue, looking at her adorable expression and then at the man beside her who was feigning ignorance, could only offer words of comfort:

"It's alright, Yingying."

"He's just a little embarrassed, he's shy."

Her words were a way of giving Xia Feng a way out.

There was no other way.

Although Xia Feng had already made up his mind to accept this brave and pitiful girl,

it was too difficult for him to admit to being a philandering man in front of Su Qingxue right now.

That was just too much!

You see, he, Liu Ruyan, and Su Qingxue all had deep emotional foundations built over several years, even decades.

And their eventual union was due to a series of coincidences and their initiative.

But Zhou Yingying…

They had known each other for far too short a time, so short that Xia Feng felt it was almost unreal.

Could he really accept this girl he had only known for less than half a month so easily?

He was afraid that he was acting impulsively and might end up hurting her.

So, he could only play dumb for now, intending to let time slowly reveal all.

The atmosphere at lunchtime that followed became harmonious and warm.

Su Qingxue kept putting Xia Feng's favorite dishes on his plate.

After a fierce internal struggle, Zhou Yingying finally mustered her courage, her chopsticks trembling as she picked up a piece of pork rib and placed it in Xia Feng's bowl.

Xia Feng, seeing her nervous yet expectant expression, smiled and ate the rib.

Zhou Yingying watched Xia Feng eat the food she had given her, and a bright, happy smile instantly spread across her face.

Looking at her innocent and content expression, Xia Feng's heart softened instantly.

He also filled both of the beauties' bowls with food.

"You two should eat more too."

"Hehe, thank you, honey."

"Thank you, senior!"

Lunch passed in this harmonious atmosphere.

After lunch, Xia Feng planned to continue his game optimization work in the afternoon.

But as soon as he stood up, Su Qingxue called him back.

She also waved to Zhou Yingying, who was preparing to pack up her takeout containers.

"Honey, don't rush into work."

"I have a client meeting this afternoon, but I can't get away. Could you go in my place?"

"Perfect, take our little Yingying with you too. Let her learn and broaden her horizons."

"Ah? Okay."

Xia Feng agreed without hesitation.

Taking a newcomer to meet a client is quite normal.

He saved the optimization progress he was working on on his computer and then got up to leave.

So, he didn't see...

The instant he turned around, Su Qingxue was frantically winking at Zhou Yingying, her face beaming with an encouraging smile that said, "Good luck, little sister!"

Zhou Yingying nodded emphatically, indicating that she completely understood her sister's meaning.

My sister is creating an opportunity for me!

I absolutely can't let her down!

I must win over that senior!

She clenched her little fists and made a silent vow in her heart.



Chapter 48 Zhou Yingying's Courageous Advance


Su Qingxue pulled a document from the pile on the table and handed it to Xia Feng.

"Honey, take this document."

Xia Feng took it with some hesitation and opened it.

At the top of the document, in bold black font, was the client's basic information:

[Name: Wang Defa]

"Wang Defa?"

Xia Feng's lips twitched involuntarily. That name was certainly unique.

He continued reading. The document was simple; it concerned the subsequent publicity and promotion of their upcoming beta test game.

Su Qingxue pointed to the address and time on the document and said in a very calm tone:

"This client is very important. It greatly affects whether our game can be a hit."

Xia Feng gave her an OK sign.

Then he closed the document and waved to Zhou Yingying.

"Yingying, let's go, we're going to meet a client."

"Ah? Oh! Okay!"

Zhou Yingying quickly stood up from the sofa and ran to Xia Feng's side.

Before leaving, she waved to Su Qingxue.

"Then, Sister Qingxue, we'll be going now."

"Go ahead."

...

Xia Feng and Zhou Yingying walked out of the office side by side.

At this time, the employees who had gone out for lunch gradually returned to the office.

When they saw their boss, Feng, carrying a document, followed by that pure and pretty junior schoolgirl in white stockings, looking like they were about to go out,

everyone's gossip spirit instantly ignited!

A male colleague who always liked to joke with Xia Feng immediately chimed in, grinning slyly:

"Hey, Feng-ge, are you taking our junior Yingying out on a date?"

"Great! Things are progressing fast!"

Another female colleague joined in the teasing, winking at Xia Feng.

"Feng-ge, aren't you afraid Boss Su will be angry? Taking another girl out on a date in front of her, you'll be kneeling on a washboard when you get home tonight!"

"Exactly! Feng-ge, if Boss Su kicks you out, we can't save you, haha!"

Xia Feng, listening to their increasingly outrageous teasing, felt a headache coming on.

He waved them off impatiently, as if shooing away a swarm of annoying flies.

"Get out of here! What nonsense are you all spouting! Can't you see I'm holding the documents?"

"I'm taking Yingying to meet a client, to let her learn something, understand?!"

"Yes, yes, yes! We understand!"

Everyone immediately flashed a knowing, knowing smile, a smile brimming with meaning.

"Meet the client first, then go on the date! We know the process!"

"Hahaha!"

The entire office instantly filled with a cheerful atmosphere.

Xia Feng, watching this group of people who seemed to enjoy the drama, could only shake his head helplessly.

He grabbed Zhou Yingying, whose face was already flushed, and practically fled into the elevator.

A burst of good-natured laughter followed behind.

Zhou Yingying, pulled by Xia Feng, felt the warmth and comfort of his hand, her heart filled with sweetness, even her steps became lighter.

Ding—

The elevator doors slowly closed, shutting out all the noise outside.

In this enclosed space with only two people.

Xia Feng released Zhou Yingying's hand, somewhat embarrassed, and began to explain.

"Um... Yingying, don't mind it, they just like to joke like that, they don't mean any harm."

Zhou Yingying looked up, her face, already flushed with shyness, appearing even more radiant under the soft elevator lights.

She gently shook her head, her single ponytail swaying slightly.

"It's okay, senior."

Her voice was soft and sweet, filled with anticipation.

"I don't mind."

"I meant a date."

"!!!"

Xia Feng felt as if an invisible hand had gripped his heart tightly, his heart skipped a beat!

This junior!

Looking into her beautiful eyes, filled with cunning and probing, he felt his head spinning.

What could he do?

He could only reach out and gently ruffle Zhou Yingying's soft hair.

"Little brat, what nonsense are you thinking about now?"

Feeling the doting touch on her head, Zhou Yingying squinted her eyes happily.

“Don’t worry.”

His voice was filled with determination.

“I will definitely make them acknowledge our relationship openly and honestly in the future.”

“Trust me.”

“Yes.”

Liu Ruyan looked into his earnest eyes and nodded heavily, her eyes slightly moist.

After dinner, Xia Feng and Su Qingxue quickly tidied up.

Xia Feng had originally planned to take a shower and change clothes before going out.

Su Qingxue immediately stopped him.

"No need for all that trouble, just come to my place to shower."

Xia Feng thought about it and agreed.

Anyway, they're all family, no need for so much formality.

"Okay, let's go now!"



Chapter 53 Rich Woman


Before setting off, Xia Feng first visited Jiangcheng's most upscale wine cellar.

He spent a full 200,000 yuan on two bottles of top-grade Feitian Moutai.

After carefully placing the beautifully packaged gift box into the trunk, he drove off onto the highway to Haicheng with Su Qingxue in the car.

That's right, Su Qingxue's home wasn't in Jiangcheng.

It was in Haicheng, a neighboring city a full three hours' drive away.

The eldest daughter of the prestigious Su family of Haicheng, who had come to Jiangcheng alone to attend university in pursuit of so-called freedom.

And then, she was simply lured away by Xia Feng, this guy who appeared out of nowhere.

And that luring lasted for eight whole years.

…

The car drove smoothly along the highway, the night scenery outside the window rushing past.

Soothing music played inside the car, creating a warm and tranquil atmosphere.

Su Qingxue reclined the passenger seat slightly, relaxing completely like a languid cat.

She turned her head to look at Xia Feng, who was focused on driving.

She began to tell Xia Feng about her childhood.

"Back then, my family was very strict; it was like being in prison."

Her voice held a hint of nostalgia.

“Every day it was either learning this or that.”

“Piano, ballet, horseback riding, foreign languages… I feel like not a single day of my childhood was truly my own.”

“Even going out to play with friends required prior application and waiting for my dad's approval.”

“Once I asked my dad why he was so strict with me.”

“He said that once I went to university, he would give me enough freedom.”

“He said everything he was doing now was to protect me.”

“So, I thought that when I took the university entrance exam, I had to get into a university far, far away!”

“Otherwise, I would definitely still be restricted in every way, just like at home.”

“In the end, I secretly applied to a university in Jiangcheng and ran away.”

Su Qingxue leaned back in her chair, her eyes filled with nostalgia for the past.

"I had it all planned out."

"I'd live freely in Jiangcheng for four years, and after graduation, I'd immediately go home to learn how to manage the family company, so I could inherit my father's Su Group."

As she said this, she turned her gaze back to Xia Feng, a sweet smile unconsciously playing on her lips.

"But then..."

"I never imagined that meeting Xia Feng would change my life forever."

"For four years of university, I was so focused on pursuing you, my mind was completely filled with you, I completely forgot about my family."

"In the end, I even inexplicably started a game company with you."

Hearing her words filled with emotion, Xia Feng reached out his free right hand and affectionately pinched her soft cheek.

"What, regretting it?"

"Hmph, no way."

Su Qingxue pouted, muttering unhappily.

"I went through so much trouble to be able to stay by your side like this."

"How could I possibly regret it?"

"Speaking of which, I really should thank Sister Ruyan."

Her voice carried a hint of relief.

"If it weren't for her, I'd probably be a rich, single woman, living a lonely life, unable to find love."

The atmosphere inside the car was warm and cozy.

...

After more than three hours of travel.

The clock on the wall had quietly struck ten o'clock at night.

The Maybach finally entered Haicheng's territory.

Then, following the address given by Su Qingxue, Xia Feng drove to the foot of a mountain.

Before him stood a massive gate, ten meters high, made of heavy metal.

The gate was tightly closed, like a city wall.

Looking at this extravagant sight, Xia Feng couldn't help but exclaim.

"It's huge."

"Qingxue, is this whole mountain yours?"

Su Qingxue got out of the car and walked to a facial recognition device beside the gate.

She brought her face close to it.

“Beep—”

A soft sound rang out.

[Identity confirmed, Miss Qingxue, welcome home.]

A cold, synthesized electronic voice sounded.

The next second, the massive metal door slowly slid open to both sides, revealing a winding mountain road leading uphill.

Xia Feng drove the car slowly up the mountain road.

A few minutes later, a huge parking lot, large enough to hold hundreds of cars, appeared before him.

Inside the parking lot were all sorts of top-of-the-line luxury cars that he had only ever seen in magazines.

Each one was incredibly valuable.

“Qingxue, it seems your father-in-law really likes cars.”

Xia Feng clicked his tongue in amazement.

Unexpectedly, Su Qingxue shook her head.

“It’s not that he likes them.”

“These cars, he bought them all for me.”

“Huh?”

“My dad, I don’t know where he heard this twisted logic, says girls should play with cars, and driving sports cars is cool.”

Su Qingxue’s tone was full of helplessness.

“And then, he bought me all these.”

“But I don’t like any of these at all.”

Xia Feng understood after hearing this.

It seems this future father-in-law is also a staunchly straight man.

Just then, a black Rolls-Royce Phantom silently pulled up in front of them.

A driver in a sharp suit got out of the car, bowed respectfully to the two of them, and then opened the back door.

“Miss Qingxue, Mr./Ms., I’ve come to pick you up. Please get in.”

The two got in.

The Rolls-Royce started smoothly and drove for nearly ten minutes.

Outside the car window, there was a meticulously maintained, enormous fountain, neatly manicured gardens, and a cluster of villas.

Finally, the car drove towards a brightly lit, magnificent villa—the most imposing of all.

Xia Feng looked at the scene outside the window, comparable to a royal garden, then turned to Su Qingxue beside him and joked,

"Seriously, if you wanted to go out before, just walking to the front gate would take you more than half an hour, right?"

"Yes."

Su Qingxue nodded in deep agreement.

"That's why I haven't liked going out much lately; it's just too much trouble."

As she spoke, she tightened her grip on Xia Feng's arm once more.

"So, it's really my luck that you took a liking to me on our first outing."

"Yes!"

Su Qingxue rubbed against his arm.

"So, you have to treat me well from now on, okay?"

"Otherwise... I'll cry!"

As she finished speaking, she playfully poked Xia Feng's cheek with her slender, white index finger.

Looking at her charmingly adorable expression, Xia Feng immediately put her mischievous finger in his mouth.

"Ah!"

Su Qingxue exclaimed, quickly pulling her finger away.

Looking at the glistening saliva on it, she gave Xia Feng a flirtatious glare, and then...

She directly put that finger in her mouth and gently sucked on it.

!!

Xia Feng, seeing her bold and seductive action, felt a surge of heat rush to his head!

This little vixen!

Feeling the car slowly come to a stop, Xia Feng forcibly suppressed the burning impulse in his heart.

He followed Su Qingxue out of the car.

Upon looking up, he saw a sprightly old man, dressed in an elegant butler's uniform, his hair neatly combed, looking energetic and vigorous, standing respectfully at the door.



Chapter 54 Su Tianxiong's Approval


"Uncle Wang! I'm back!"

Su Qingxue, clinging to Xia Feng's arm, greeted the old butler happily.

Then she turned to Xia Feng and introduced him:

"Honey, this is Uncle Wang. He's my father's most trusted right-hand man."

"Hello, Uncle Wang."

Xia Feng also greeted him politely.

"Miss, Young Master, welcome back."

Uncle Wang, with a gentle smile, bowed slightly to the two.

"Master has been waiting for you in the living room for a long time. Please follow me."

He then turned and led the way.

The two followed.

Xia Feng followed behind, his eyes scanning the surroundings.

The long corridor was lined with extremely valuable oil paintings.

On every small table were antiques he had only ever seen on television.

Xia Feng felt this deeply once again.

Su Qingxue's father…

He's really rich!

Following Uncle Wang through several doors, they finally arrived at a spacious living room.

Behind a coffee table crafted from a single piece of golden nanmu wood sat a man who looked to be around fifty years old, dressed in an exquisite Tang suit.

The man was intently preparing tea.

His movements were fluid and meticulous, imbued with a certain mysterious charm.

Although he simply sat there quietly, the imposing aura of a superior emanating from him commanded respect, making it impossible to underestimate him.

Xia Feng's heart skipped a beat.

Damn!

This father-in-law's aura is too strong!

After leading them there, Uncle Wang quietly withdrew from the living room, leaving them alone.

Su Qingxue, holding Xia Feng's arm, quickly walked to the man's side.

"Dad! I'm home!"

Her voice was filled with the sweet innocence of a young girl.

Xia Feng quickly stepped forward and gently placed the two bottles of expensive Moutai on the corner of the coffee table.

"Father-in-law, this is a small token of my appreciation."

The man addressed as "Dad," Su Tianxiong, chairman of the Su Group, slowly raised his head upon hearing this.

His gaze swept over Xia Feng, then fell on the two bottles of liquor, and he simply nodded slightly.

He pushed two cups of tea, one prepared, in front of Xia Feng and the other of Su Qingxue.

"Sit down and have some tea first."

His voice was steady and firm.

"You must be tired from your trip back. Take a shower and rest for a bit."

Su Qingxue pulled Xia Feng to sit down on the sofa beside her.

Her face was filled with happiness.

She knew that her father's words meant he had accepted Xia Feng.

Xia Feng picked up the still-steaming cup of tea in front of him and took a small sip.

The tea was fragrant and mellow, with a sweet aftertaste.

“Lin family lad,”

Su Tianxiong suddenly spoke.

“I know you. What you did back then was indeed somewhat impulsive.”

Xia Feng paused slightly.

He placed the teacup back on the coffee table and sat up even more upright.

He raised his head, looking directly into Su Tianxiong's deep eyes without fear, and said firmly:

“I know.”

“But if I had to choose again, I would still do the same.”

"My family cannot be bullied by anyone."

Su Tianxiong's eyes flashed with approval upon hearing Xia Feng's resolute reply.

This was also why he hadn't objected to his daughter's relationship with Xia Feng after investigating his background.

He was responsible, principled, and, most importantly, knew how to protect his family.

He could entrust his daughter to him with peace of mind.

Su Tianxiong picked up the teapot and personally refilled Xia Feng's teacup.

Su Qingxue, standing to the side, listened to their conversation with some curiosity.

She didn't know Xia Feng's past, nor what he had done.

But she believed that Xia Feng would tell her himself someday.

"Qingxue."

Su Tianxiong's tone softened considerably.

"Has Xiao Feng bullied you?"

"If he has, tell Dad, and I'll teach him a lesson!"

"No!"

Su Qingxue refused without hesitation.

She hugged Xia Feng's arm even tighter, like a kitten guarding its food.

"What if you hurt him?!"

"Besides, he's so good to me, so incredibly kind!"

"Sigh..."

Su Tianxiong shook his head helplessly.

"Girls are naturally drawn to their surroundings."

Then, he turned to look at Xia Feng.

"Xia Feng, Qingxue can be quite mischievous sometimes, remember to be lenient with her."

"Understood, Father-in-law."

Xia Feng nodded quickly, his face solemn.

"I'll always be good to Qingxue."

"Still calling me Father-in-law?"

Su Tianxiong raised an eyebrow.

Xia Feng paused for a moment, then reacted, a sincere smile spreading across his face.

"Dad."

"Hmm."

Su Tianxiong nodded in satisfaction.

He waved to the two of them.

"Alright, you must be tired from the journey, go and rest."

"Today, I mainly wanted to meet you, to see what kind of person my daughter chose."

"Then I'll take my husband to rest. Goodnight, Dad."

"Goodnight, Dad."

The two stood up and walked out of the living room.

As soon as they stepped out of the living room, a petite maid with shoulder-length short hair appeared silently in front of them.

She had a very pretty face, but it was completely expressionless, like a delicate doll.

"Three-nothing."

The word instantly popped into Xia Feng's mind.

She stopped in front of them and bowed respectfully.

"Miss, Master, Steward Wang sent me to serve you both."

"Please follow me, I'll take you to the bathroom."

The two followed this three-nothing maid to a luxurious bathroom even larger than their living room.

But the maid showed no sign of leaving.

She walked up to the two men and began to help them undress.

Xia Feng instinctively shrank back.

But when he turned his head, he saw that Su Qingxue didn't seem to mind at all.

Xia Feng could only sigh silently.

Well, when in Rome, do as the Romans do.

He let the unassuming maid remove his clothes piece by piece.

After she finished, the maid went to the huge bathtub and began to add various essential oils and vibrant flower petals.

Then, she took two brand-new towels and began to carefully scrub the backs of the two men already soaking in the water.

Xia Feng enjoyed this meticulous service and couldn't help but sigh inwardly.

Back when he was still the young master of the Lin family, he hadn't enjoyed this much.

It seems…

the Lin family wasn't rich enough back then!



Chapter 55 Happiness


Under the meticulous care of a professional maid, the two cleaned themselves and donned expensive bathrobes that had been prepared beforehand.

The seemingly ordinary maid led them to the door of the room where Su Qingxue had lived since childhood.

She bowed again to them.

"Miss, young master, I'm right behind the door."

"If you need anything, just call me."

With that, she left Su Qingxue's room and gently closed the door.

"Wow."

Xia Feng looked at the closed door and couldn't help but exclaim to Su Qingxue beside him.

"Your maids are so professional, so amazing!"

"Indeed, the world of the rich is wonderful."

As Xia Feng spoke, he began to curiously examine the room where Su Qingxue had grown up.

The entire room was decorated in a dreamy, pink princess style.

A huge pink princess bed stood in the center of the room, adorned with several large teddy bears.

Xia Feng's gaze swept over the toys, and he spotted a familiar figure.

Among the pile of teddy bears, a slightly worn, brown teddy bear was prominently displayed, like a star surrounded by the moon.

Xia Feng paused slightly.

He walked over and picked up the small teddy bear.

"I didn't expect you to still have this."

His voice held a hint of nostalgia.

Seeing that Xia Feng recognized the teddy bear, Su Qingxue's face instantly lit up with a radiant smile.

"Of course!"

She quickly walked to Xia Feng's side, took the teddy bear from him, and carefully hugged it to her chest.

"This was the only gift you ever gave me."

"I cherish it!"

Xia Feng looked at her, treasuring her like a precious gem, and smiled a little embarrassedly.

Back then, he simply considered Su Qingxue his best friend, a true buddy.

He couldn't just give gifts to any friend casually, could he?

But…

After they got together, he realized he hadn't really paid attention to that aspect.

Looks like he'll have to be more mindful of these little gestures in the future.

Seeing Xia Feng suddenly lost in thought, Su Qingxue waved her hand in front of him.

"What's wrong? Suddenly spacing out?"

"Nothing."

Xia Feng smiled.

"Let's sleep."

He scooped Su Qingxue up from the floor and tossed her onto the soft bed!

"Ah~ Hahaha!"

Su Qingxue bounced on the bed, letting out a delighted scream, then giggled.

Xia Feng jumped onto the bed too.

...

Outside the door.

Zhao Rou stood silently outside the door, like a statue.

Hearing the faint sounds of play and commotion coming from inside, her usually calm heart began to race slightly.

She recalled the same uncontrollable heartbeat she had felt when she was close to Xia Feng in the bathroom earlier.

"Am I... sick?"

Zhao Rou wondered silently to herself.

...

The night passed without incident.

When ten o'clock in the morning...

Around four in the morning, Zhao Rou, who had gone to her own room to rest, returned to Su Qingxue's door once more.

She raised her hand and gently knocked.

"Miss, Young Master, breakfast is ready."

But after waiting a while, there was no response from inside.

"Excuse me,"

she said softly, then pushed open the door and went in.

She saw the two still fast asleep on the bed.

Su Qingxue was clinging to Xia Feng like an octopus, her arms and legs tightly wrapped around him, holding him close.

After seeing their state, a barely perceptible blush appeared on Zhao Rou's usually expressionless face.

She tiptoed out of the room again.

She stood outside the door again, her hands clasped in front of her lower abdomen, looking dutiful.

But her thoughts had already drifted away.

The image of that opened bottle of top-quality red wine she'd seen a few days ago while cleaning the winery uncontrollably resurfaced in her mind.

The cork must have made a sound when it was pulled from the bottle, right?

...

Time quickly passed to 10:30.

Xia Feng finally slowly opened his eyes.

The moment he opened them, he saw Su Qingxue lying on top of him, her beautiful eyes gazing at him with deep affection.

"What time is it?"

Xia Feng's voice was still a little hoarse.

"It's 10:30~"

Su Qingxue's voice was soft and sweet.

"Have you been awake for a long time? And have you been just looking at me like this?"

"No."

Su Qingxue shook her head.

"I've only been awake for a few minutes."

"It's just that I feel so happy to see my loved one as soon as I wake up."

Xia Feng looked at her happy expression, his heart warming. He reached out and gently stroked her small nose.

"Then you can be even happier."

Saying this, he looked up and planted a gentle good morning kiss on her red lips.

"Alright, it's time to get up and wash up."

"Okay."

Su Qingxue obediently climbed off him.

'Pots'

She stretched, and Xia Feng did the same.

Then the two of them went into the en-suite bathroom in Su Qingxue's room to wash up.

After they finished getting ready, they saw Zhao Rou still standing outside the door.

But she seemed to be in a daze; even though the two of them were right next to her, she hadn't noticed.

Xia Feng looked at this seemingly ordinary maid, who was about the same height as Zhou Yingying, and waved curiously in front of her.

She snapped out of her reverie and quickly bowed to the two of them, apologizing.

"I'm sorry! Miss! Young Master! I was lost in thought!"

"It's alright."

Su Qingxue waved her hand.

"Please come with me, breakfast is ready."

"Okay."

Zhao Rou led the way.

The three of them arrived at a spacious dining room.

A long dining table came into view, on which were laid several exquisitely prepared breakfast dishes that looked very appetizing.

Su Tianxiong was sitting in the main seat, reading a newspaper and drinking tea.

Seeing Xia Feng and Qingxue arrive, he put down his newspaper and greeted them.

"Xiao Feng, Qingxue, come and have breakfast."

"Eat your breakfast before you go back."

The two nodded and sat down beside him.

Zhao Rou prepared utensils for them and then began her professional feeding service.

Xia Feng was now used to Zhao Rou's service and ate without hesitation.

When they were almost finished with breakfast, Su Tianxiong suddenly spoke up.

"Xiao Feng."

"Dad, what is it?"

"When you go back later, take Zhao Rou with you."

Su Tianxiong pointed to the maid standing dutifully beside him.

"Let Zhao Rou go; she can take good care of your daily needs."

"Yes, sir."

Zhao Rou nodded in agreement.

Xia Feng thought about it.

It didn't seem like a problem.

Having another maid in the house seemed quite nice.

It was just another mouth to feed; no big deal.

"Okay, Dad."

He readily agreed.



Chapter 56 Ten Babies in One Pregnancy


In the dining room, the three chatted for a while longer.

Su Tianxiong looked at Xia Feng, a gentle smile on his face.

“Xiao Feng, I’ve heard about you and that girl from the Liu family.”

His voice was steady and strong.

“You don’t need to worry.”

“At our level, a man with some ability can have a few women around him; this little thing is nothing.”

Hearing this, Xia Feng felt a warmth in his heart.

He knew that his father-in-law was reassuring him in his own way.

He nodded solemnly.

“Dad, I understand.”

…

The clock on the wall had quietly pointed to eleven o’clock.

Seeing that it was getting late, Xia Feng stood up from his seat, preparing to take his leave.

Su Tianxiong also stood up, seemingly intending to personally see them to the door.

Uncle Wang had silently appeared in the dining room sometime earlier, bowing slightly to everyone.

"Master, the car is ready."

Su Tianxiong led the way outside.

Upon arriving at the villa's entrance, the black Rolls-Royce Phantom from yesterday was parked quietly.

Su Tianxiong watched the figure preparing to leave with his beloved daughter and the plain-looking maid.

He finally spoke to Xia Feng, his tone filled with domineering authority, and gave him a final instruction.

"Xia Feng, remember this."

"When help is needed, make full use of all your strength."

"In the entire southern region, there is nothing I, Su Tianxiong, cannot do."

Xia Feng felt a surge of emotion upon hearing these powerful words.

He nodded emphatically.

"Understood, Dad."

"I won't act recklessly."

"Okay, go ahead."

Su Tianxiong nodded in satisfaction.

"Goodbye, Dad!"

Su Qingxue clung to Xia Feng's arm and waved to Su Tianxiong.

"I'll come back to see you again!"

"When I have the chance, I'll bring back a big, fat grandson for you to play with!"

Hearing his wife's playful, unserious words, Xia Feng couldn't help but smile wryly.

He pulled Su Qingxue into the back seat of the Rolls-Royce.

Zhao Rou also quietly got in.

The car started smoothly.

Xia Feng sat in the middle, Su Qingxue on his left, and the prim and proper little maid, Zhao Rou, on his right.

He reached out and pinched Su Qingxue's soft cheek, saying irritably,

"What did you just say?!"

Su Qingxue's cheek was pinched, and she could only make indistinct sounds.

“Oh well, it’s bound to happen sooner or later anyway. It’s not like we don’t have the money to raise children.”

Xia Feng remembered that Liu Ruyan had mentioned wanting children several times recently.

But he wasn’t ready to take on that responsibility.

“We’ll talk about it later.”

His voice carried a hint of apology.

“Let me calm down first.”

“Then remember, you must have one before you’re thirty.”

Su Qingxue also dropped her joking expression and looked at him seriously.

“I’ve heard that having children after thirty isn’t good for the baby.”

“What do you take me for!”

Xia Feng joined in the joke.

“I’ll have you two come along!”

Soon, the car arrived at the parking lot.

The three of them got into Xia Feng’s Maybach.

He drove the two beauties home.

Rewind to last night.

Moonlit Villa, in a guest room.

Zhou Yingying was half-asleep when she was woken up by the urge to urinate.

Rubbing her sleepy eyes, she sat up from the soft bed, preparing to get out of bed to go to the bathroom.

But as soon as she moved, she felt as if she had touched something warm and soft.

She instinctively turned her head.

By the dim moonlight filtering through the window, she saw a graceful figure lying on her side beside her.

Zhou Yingying's body stiffened abruptly!

Liu Ruyan, beside her, was also awakened by her sudden movement.

Liu Ruyan slowly sat up, her gossamer-thin silk nightgown slipping down with her movement, revealing a large expanse of smooth, white skin.

She rubbed her eyes and asked softly in a slightly languid and hoarse voice:

"What's wrong, Yingying?"

Zhou Yingying was startled by the voice, her body trembling.

Her brain began to race.

This is her senior's house…

He has two wives…

One is Qingxue, whom I know…

Then this one in front of her…

It must be Ruyan, the one she's only heard of but never seen!

That means she's now officially his wife!

Having figured it all out, Zhou Yingying quickly got out of bed and bowed respectfully to Liu Ruyan.

"Hello, Sister Ruyan!"

"Um... I'm Zhou Yingying. Today... I'm sorry to have trouble staying here today, but thank you so much!"

Looking at the adorable junior student in front of her, who was so nervous she was practically jumping around,

"Just as Qingxue said, she's a very cute little sister."

She waved to Zhou Yingying.

"Alright, alright, don't be so formal."

"Qingxue must have told you everything, right?"

"From now on, just treat this place as your home."

"Yes!"

But just as she relaxed,

her bladder, which had been holding back for so long, began to protest loudly.

Her legs began to rub together uncontrollably, and a look of pain appeared on her pretty face.

"Um... Sister Ruyan..."

Her voice was trembling with tears.

"Where...where's the toilet?"

Liu Ruyan, seeing her adorable expression as she was about to burst, understood her predicament.

"Come with me."

She smiled, stood up, and pulled Zhou Yingying towards the bathroom attached to the room.

By the time they both finished their business and returned to bed, more than five minutes had passed.

To bridge the gap between them, they started talking about the man they both shared.

As they chatted, their relationship grew closer.

After all…

You like him, and I like him too.

Then we're on the same side!

We're best friends!



Chapter 57 Su Qingxue Sheds Tears (Bonus chapter for the godfathers today!)


The two chatted for almost an hour.

Finally, they felt sleepy, pulled the covers over themselves, and went back to sleep.

After all, Liu Ruyan had a mountain of company business to handle the next day and couldn't afford to indulge herself.

Zhou Yingying felt the same way.

She had only recently joined "Dream Chaser" and was still learning and adapting; she couldn't let personal matters affect her work.

Moreover, she wanted to quickly integrate into that harmonious and energetic team and build good relationships with her colleagues.

...

The next morning.

As the first rays of dawn illuminated the room.

She looked at the still sleepy, adorable, and slightly dazed Zhou Yingying beside her and smiled gently.

"Come on, Yingying, let me take you to wash up."

She said, getting out of bed and heading towards the en-suite bathroom.

"Use the spare toothbrush for now. You can move in later, and then buy some of your personal items."

"From now on, this room will be yours."

Zhou Yingying, following behind her, paused upon hearing this!

She looked at Liu Ruyan's graceful back with some surprise, her voice filled with uncertainty.

"Sister Ruyan, I...can I really move in?"

Liu Ruyan turned around, looking at her adorable, cautious expression, and affectionately tapped her nose with her slender finger.

"What? Don't you want to move in?"

A mischievous "I understand" smile appeared on her face.

"Here, you can see Xia Feng every day, you know?"

This was a surefire way to win her over!

Zhou Yingying's head bobbed up and down like a chicken pecking at rice, without a trace of hesitation.

"Yes! I want to!"

But then, she lowered her head shyly, her little hands nervously clutching the hem of her clothes.

“But…but wouldn’t that be too much trouble for you?”

“Sigh.”

Liu Ruyan walked straight over, took her soft, boneless hand, and pulled her into the bathroom.

“If you want to stay, then move in. Don’t worry about the trouble.”

“Besides…”

Liu Ruyan placed the toothbrush in Zhou Yingying’s hand, then added softly.

“Your moving in would be a huge benefit for me too.”

Zhou Yingying’s mind instantly flashed back to what Su Qingxue had told her yesterday.

Her pretty face flushed crimson!

She looked up, her large, watery eyes filled with shyness and understanding.

“Is…is it because senior is too strong, right?”

Her voice was barely a whisper, filled with a deep, shy charm.

"Hehe, good to know."

Liu Ruyan nodded in satisfaction.

A promising student indeed.

"So, we really need to work together from now on."

"Otherwise, we won't be able to withstand his antics."

"Yes!"

Zhou Yingying nodded emphatically.

For her senior's happiness, and for her own life, the Women's Alliance must be unbreakable!

Zhou Yingying took the toothbrush and stood next to Liu Ruyan, squeezing toothpaste onto it.

She looked in the mirror at the two figures, one tall and one short, one mature and alluring, the other pure and lovely.

She felt as if she were in a dream; everything seemed so unreal.

After washing up, the two changed their clothes.

Xia Feng looked at her, somewhat puzzled, and asked,

"Xiao Rou? Is something the matter?"

Zhao Rou walked to his side, her usually calm eyes simply gazing at him.

Then, in a flat tone, she asked a question that made Xia Feng's jaw drop.

"Young Master."

"Should I go and deal with that Ji Bo?"



Chapter 71 Interesting Information


"Young Master, should I go and deal with that Ji Bo?"

She asked in a calm tone, utterly shocking a question.

Xia Feng was completely stunned, almost thinking he'd stayed up late and was hallucinating.

He slowly turned his head, looking at the expressionless, emotionless maid beside him, feeling his worldview crumble.

After regaining his composure, he tried to ask in a joking tone:

"Um, Xiao Rou..."

"Aren't you a maid? How could you say something like that?"

"Have maids' services become this extensive now? Even handling this kind of thing?"

Zhao Rou, seeing Xia Feng's question, maintained her delicate, pretty face, remaining expressionless, and began to explain in a factual tone.

"Young Master, I was brought from a place by the Su family that specialized in training private servants for top-tier noble families."

"In that place, a qualified servant had to be omnipotent."

"That naturally included acting as the master's 'black glove,' clearing away all obstacles in their path."

She spoke of this extraordinary past with a nonchalant tone.

Xia Feng listened, but his heart felt as if it had been stabbed.

Black glove? Clearing obstacles?

These cold words, spoken by a girl who looked about the same age as Zhou Yingying, sounded so incongruous, so heartbreaking.

What had she experienced in her past?

He couldn't help but reach out and gently place his hand on her head.

Feeling the sudden warmth and weight on his head.

Zhao Rou's body trembled slightly.

She looked up at Xia Feng with some confusion.

Although her face remained expressionless, she secretly enjoyed Xia Feng's gentle head pat.

Was this… a reward from her son-in-law for proactively helping him solve his problems?

This thought popped into her head.

Xia Feng spoke, his voice tinged with pity.

"Xiao Rou, you don't need to do this anymore."

"You just need to take care of our three meals a day and cleaning the villa."

"Of course, if you feel tired, you can rest. We can do the cleaning then, or we can just eat out."

"Cleaning doesn't have to be done every day; we're not that fussy."

Hearing Xia Feng's words, Zhao Rou was even more confused.

A hint of bewilderment flashed in her beautiful eyes.

"But… son-in-law, do you really not need me to get rid of him?"

"I've received the most professional training; I can definitely do it without leaving a trace…"

"No need."

Xia Feng gently but firmly interrupted her.

"Just be a good housekeeper."

"I'll handle Ji Bo's matter."

He gave her a reassuring smile.

"You know, my father-in-law is Su Tianxiong."

"With him backing me up, I'm perfectly safe."

"There's no need for you to take that kind of risk."

"Go do your own thing first."

"If you really have nothing to do, you can sit on the bed and watch my performance."

Zhao Rou listened to Xia Feng's unquestionable words, remained silent for a moment, and then nodded gently.

She obediently walked to the soft bed next to her and sat down obediently.

Seeing this, Xia Feng also turned his attention back to the computer screen.

As he looked, he discovered a very interesting piece of information.

To verify the authenticity of this information, he even hacked into Ji Bo's and his father Ji Er'er's phones.

After reviewing a large number of chat logs and files, he finally confirmed the information's authenticity.

A cold smile curled at the corner of his mouth.

He organized and packaged all the useful information.

Then, he privately sent a copy to Liu Ruyan.

【Ruyan, I found something very interesting, take a look, there's a surprise.】

The message arrived instantly.

【Okay!】

About ten minutes later.

Liu Ruyan's message popped up again.

【So that's how it is! With this, as long as no one stops me, I can just swallow the entire Ji family whole! Thank you so much, honey! I'll reward you properly when we get back!】

Xia Feng looked at this message, filled with surprise and excitement.

He could imagine that Liu Ruyan was now eager to make her move.

【Then I'll have to look forward to it. Let me know when you're ready to act, and I'll send a copy to the law enforcement bureau as well.】

【Okay! I'll prepare for a while, and then I'll deliver a fatal blow!】

After that, Liu Ruyan didn't send any more messages.

It seemed she had already gone to prepare her scheme.

Xia Feng stretched, preparing to loosen his stiff muscles.

A pair of soft, cool hands reached out from behind him and gently pressed against his waist.

It was Zhao Rou.

After massaging for a while, she pulled Xia Feng's arm.

"Young Master, lie down on the bed, I'll give you a massage."

Xia Feng raised an eyebrow with some curiosity.

He never expected to be massaged himself.

Usually, he was the one providing massages to Liu Ruyan and the other two women.

Following Zhao Rou's instructions, he obediently lay down on the bed.

Zhao Rou knelt beside the bed and began to give Xia Feng a professional massage on his back.

Xia Feng felt her technique, which, while not as good as his, was still at least forty percent of his own, and let out a satisfied sigh.

Don't underestimate that forty percent of skill.

If this were outside, she would definitely be considered a top-tier massage master!

Indeed, this maid, Xiao Rou, is truly all-around capable.

Xia Feng, lying on his stomach, suddenly became curious about how Zhao Rou had lived her life before.

While enjoying the massage, he casually asked,

"Xiao Rou, can you tell me about your past?"

"I'm a little curious."

"If not, that's fine."

Zhao Rou didn't stop her massage, continuing to focus intently on it.

Meanwhile, she answered Xia Feng's question in a calm tone, seemingly multitasking.

"There's nothing I can't say, son-in-law."

"My past is actually quite boring."

"If you don't mind."



Chapter 72 Zhao Rou's Past


Zhao Rou began to slowly recount her past.

Her voice remained calm, as if she were talking about something completely unrelated to herself.

“As far back as I can remember, I was already in an orphanage.”

“I don’t know who my parents are; maybe I didn’t have any parents at all.”

“My life in the orphanage was relatively easy until I was four years old.”

“But after I turned four, we had to start learning all sorts of skills.”

Zhao Rou paused, as if recalling a distant past.

“We had to learn cooking, cleaning, etiquette, foreign languages, martial arts, first aid, even computer skills…”

“Because the director said that only by mastering enough skills could we be noticed by truly important people and have a reason to live.”

“And those children who couldn’t learn, or who learned slowly, would be…”

She didn’t finish, but Xia Feng already understood what that word meant.

Abandoned.

“However, those who are prettier, even if they don't study well, will be kept and carefully nurtured.”

“Because, these can be used as decorative objects later.”

Hearing this, Xia Feng instantly understood.

These so-called decorative objects, to put it bluntly, are just tacitly understood playthings in wealthy circles.

“I was always the most hardworking and the most talented one.”

Zhao Rou continued in her calm tone.

“So, when I was sixteen, I was spotted by Steward Wang, who came to our place to select servants.”

“Then, he took me back to the Su family.”

“And then, I began my work as a servant in the Su family.”

For her, the eight years in the Su family seemed like just a change of scenery, continuing that routine life.

Although the Su family's treatment was quite good.

But at that time, Zhao Rou didn't encounter anything that could stir her heart.

In her world, there were no friends, no entertainment, only endless orders and work.

“It wasn't until eight years later, when you, young master, arrived, that the master assigned me to you.”

At that moment, she suddenly realized that being by Xia Feng's side, her heart was drawn to his every move.

After saying this, Zhao Rou's massage reached its final step.

She gently patted Xia Feng's back.

“My past was rather boring, wasn't it, young master?”

“Nothing particularly exciting.”

“All done, you can get up now.”

Xia Feng slowly sat up from the bed.

But instead of getting up, he gently pushed Zhao Rou back onto the bed.

Zhao Rou's body stiffened slightly!

She thought her young master was going to do something.

Instinctively, she braced herself, her soft, cool hands even reaching for the collar of her maid outfit.

Seeing her so submissive, Xia Feng quickly stopped her.

"Wait!"

"Xiaorou, I just wanted to give you a massage, that's not what I meant."

"You...you can just turn over and lie face down."

After hearing this, Zhao Rou's body slowly relaxed.

She lowered her hands, then obediently turned over and lay face down on the bed.

But...

Xia Feng seemed to see a fleeting hint of disappointment on her face.

Hmm, it must be an illusion.

"Alright, now, just enjoy yourself."

Xia Feng's voice was full of gentleness.

"Forget all those unpleasant things from the past."

"From now on, you'll live happily with us."

As he spoke, his hands began massaging Zhao Rou's back, which was covered by the delicate fabric of her maid outfit.

"Okay."

"Young Master..."

"From now on, Xiao Rou will always be with Young Master..."

Just then, an idea flashed through Xia Feng's mind.

He seemed to have a passive skill.

It could have a stronger effect on the opposite sex.

He had only tried this passive skill when he first acquired it.

What would happen if he activated it during the massage?

Thinking it, he did it!

But with his [Divine Healing Skill], he could clearly sense that the healing effect was amplified several times after activating the passive skill!

This gave him an unexpected surge of joy!

He massaged her even more diligently!

This was tough on Zhao Rou.

After Xia Feng finished his enhanced treatment,

looking at Zhao Rou, who had fallen completely asleep, Xia Feng smiled and shook his head.

He turned her over so she was face up.

Then, he considerately covered her with the blanket.

But suddenly, he couldn't remember where he had smelled it before.

He decided not to think about it anymore.

Now, Xia Feng planned to go out.

He needed to get some good ingredients and traditional Chinese medicine to use in conjunction with his divine medical skills to properly nourish the women in his family.

...

Liu Group, CEO's Office.

Liu Ruyan sat refreshed in her executive chair, processing documents.

Her mood today was incredibly sunny and bright.

First thing this morning, Xia Feng had sent her such a big surprise!

"That's amazing!

He's truly my man!

What should I wear to reward him tonight?

That catgirl outfit?

Or that nurse's uniform?

Or a collar and rope?

Just as Liu Ruyan's thoughts were starting to drift off course...

"Knock knock."

There was a knock on the office door.

"Come in."

The door opened.

Her good mood vanished instantly.

It was Li Mei, walking in with Ji Bo, the one who made her want to vomit.



Chapter 73 Ji Bo's Hypocritical Pretense


Li Mei and Ji Bo walked in through the door.

Seeing these two people she least wanted to see, Liu Ruyan's pretty face, which had just been carrying a hint of a smile, instantly turned cold.

The temperature in the office seemed to drop several degrees.

Her good mood from just moments before vanished.

Liu Ruyan didn't even bother to get up, simply leaning back in her executive chair, coldly watching them.

She was about to ask them what they wanted when

Li Mei's temper flared up!

She rushed to Liu Ruyan's desk in a few strides and slammed her hand on it!

"Bang!"

"You, Liu Ruyan!"

She pointed at Liu Ruyan's nose and launched into a torrent of abuse!

"What did I teach you yesterday?! I told you to take good care of Ji Bo, and what did you do?! You arranged for his office to be in such a remote corner?!"

"You're clearly disobeying me, aren't you?!"

Liu Ruyan's gaze bypassed the furious Li Mei and coldly landed on Ji Bo behind her.

Heh.

What a despicable person.

I didn't expect him to actually go and tattle on her to his mother.

Ji Bo seemed to sense Liu Ruyan's icy gaze, his heart skipped a beat, and he quickly stepped forward to pull the still-angry Li Mei away.

"Auntie, please don't be like this, please don't be angry."

He first gave Liu Ruyan an apologetic smile, then began to explain in an innocent and aggrieved tone:

"I'm sorry, Ms. Liu."

"It's all my fault that Auntie found out about this."

"Because you told me yesterday not to bother you unless necessary, I didn't dare to come over casually."

"Auntie said she wanted to come and see how I was settling in today, so I could only take her to my office."

"I...I didn't expect Auntie to be so angry, really, it's all my fault."

His words were perfectly watertight.

He both absolved himself completely and subtly sowed discord among Li Mei's eyes.

Sure enough, upon hearing this, Li Mei immediately stopped Ji Bo, who was still "apologizing" to Liu Ruyan.

“Ji Bo! You did nothing wrong! You don’t need to apologize to her!”

She looked at the “sensible” young man with pity, then turned to Liu Ruyan and unleashed an even more intense barrage of criticism!

“Look at him! Look how sensible he is! How considerate he is of you!”

“And look at you! What kind of behavior is this!”

“What kind of president’s assistant would be so far away from the president?! Is this appropriate?!”

“And another thing!”

As if remembering something, she pointed at Ji Bo and questioned Liu Ruyan:

“Why did you make her call you President Liu?!”

Ji Bo immediately feigned a wronged expression, as if he had really done something wrong, and explained to Li Mei:

“It’s like this, Auntie.”

“I think it’s better to address people by their job titles in the company; it sounds more professional.”

“So… so I took the liberty of calling her President Liu.”

After hearing his explanation, which was full of “politeness” and “professionalism”…

Li Mei's gaze softened as she looked at him.

"Oh my, look at him, look at him! Our little Ji Bo is such a polite and well-behaved child!"

"From now on, don't call her 'President Liu' anymore, it's too formal! Just call her by her name, Ru Yan!"

"After all, this huge Liu Group will need the two of you to develop together!"

"Calling her that so formally won't do!"

Her eyes darted around, as if she'd thought of something.

"How about this! I think you don't need to be an assistant anymore!"

"From now on, you'll be Ru Yan's secretary!"

"That way, you two can spend every day together and get closer!"

Ji Bo felt his heart was about to jump out of his chest with excitement!

He felt like he'd received a tremendous encouragement, and a delighted smile immediately appeared on his face as he gratefully said to Li Mei:

"Really?! Auntie!"

"I understand! I will definitely work hard from now on! I will definitely work with Ru Yan to develop the Liu Group even better!"

He was now filled with pride!

Ha, what an easily fooled, stupid woman!

With just a few words, he could completely manipulate her!

Liu Ruyan, oh Liu Ruyan!

Even if you resist me, what can you do?

As long as I have your family under my control!

But…

He was also a little puzzled.

Judging from Liu Ruyan's aggressive behavior during their first meeting yesterday,

she should be slamming her fist on the table and vehemently objecting by now.

Why is she so quiet today?

He turned his head, puzzled, to look at Liu Ruyan.

He saw Liu Ruyan resting her hands on the desk, watching them with unhurried composure.

Her beautiful face even held a hint of amusement.

Her gaze…

was as if she were watching two clowns performing energetically on stage.

Seeing that her daughter hadn't spoken, Li Mei assumed that her authority had worked.

She turned her gaze to Liu Ruyan and said in a commanding tone:

"Did you hear me!"

"From now on, Xiao Jibo will be your secretary!"

"Right now, arrange a good seat for him! Understand?"

"Okay."

To everyone's surprise.

Liu Ruyan agreed very readily.

"Then where do you think would be best?"

Li Mei didn't even think, pointing directly to the small cubicle partitioned off in the office specifically for resting.

"Isn't there another rest area in your office?"

"Clean that up, and Xiao Jibo can use it."

"No."

Liu Ruyan refused without hesitation.

"Anywhere but mine, you can take him to choose."

"But not here."

What a joke!

The only reason she agreed temporarily was to avoid alerting him and ruining the wonderful gift her husband had given her!

Could she really bear to see that face that she felt such physical disgust for every day?

She was afraid she wouldn't be able to control herself and would actually throw him out the window!

"Hey! What's wrong with you, child..."

Seeing that Li Mei was about to explode again,

Ji Bo quickly stepped forward and calmed her down.

"Auntie, Auntie, please don't be angry."

He knew that becoming Liu Ruyan's personal secretary was already a huge step forward.

He needed to know when to stop; he couldn't try to get ahead too quickly.

"This is good enough, this is already very good."

He wore a gentle smile.

"Ruyan... she's just not familiar with me yet."

"I believe we'll get along very well in the future."



Chapter 74 Custom Recording


With Ji Bo's reassurance, Li Mei finally calmed down.

After taking a few deep breaths, she said to Liu Ruyan,

"Okay!"

"But remember, stay close to Ji Bo, understand?"

"Ji Bo, let's go! I'll pick out an office for you."

With that, she led the way out of the office.

"Yes, Auntie."

Ji Bo responded to Li Mei, then turned back to Liu Ruyan with an apologetic smile before following Li Mei.

Li Mei had just opened the office door when she seemed to suddenly remember something.

She turned to Liu Ruyan, who was still sitting in her chair, and said in an unquestionable tone:
