"You haven't been home in a long time, and tonight is your grandfather's birthday banquet."

"Your grandfather would also like to see you."

Then, without waiting for Liu Ruyan's reply, she took Ji Bo and left.

Liu Ruyan stared at the closed door, a look of disgust on her face.

She rubbed her arms incessantly, as if trying to scrub away some grime.

Then, as if remembering something, she quickly pulled her phone from the drawer and opened a pre-saved audio recording.

【Ruyan, I love you.】

Xia Feng's magnetic and gentle voice flowed softly from the phone.

"Ah~"

"That feels so good~"

Liu Ruyan let out a long sigh.

"Hearing my husband's voice really makes me feel so good."

This was a custom-made recording, just like the one Su Qingxue had.

That night, after returning home, Su Qingxue excitedly shared the recording that had made her and Zhou Yingying almost faint with happiness.

As a result, she and Zhou Yingying pestered Xia Feng that very night, asking for a copy for themselves.

Xia Feng was so embarrassed he wanted to dig a three-bedroom apartment out of the ground with his toes.

But since his wives wanted it, he still swallowed his immense shame and recorded various versions of private messages for each of them.

Liu Ruyan contentedly opened another recording.

【Ruyan, every day I spend with you is a precious treasure.】

“Ah~”

She wriggled happily in her executive chair like a boneless maggot.

Just then.

“Knock knock.”

The office door was knocked on again.

Liu Ruyan jumped in fright and quickly put her phone away!

She forcibly controlled her facial expression, cleared her throat, and instantly transformed back into the aloof, icy female CEO.

“Come in.”

Opening the door was her other capable female assistant, Wang Ya.

When Wang Ya walked in, she noticed a lingering blush on her boss's face and slightly disheveled clothes, and felt a pang of doubt.

However, she dutifully began her report.

"President Liu, that Assistant Ji, cough...that Secretary Ji, has found an empty room on your floor as his future office. What do you think?"

"Ignore him."

Liu Ruyan's tone returned to its icy tone.

“Just pretend he doesn’t exist.”

Wang Ya nodded.

“Also, regarding the shares of the Ji family company that you asked me to keep an eye on, we’ve already started secretly acquiring them.”

A cold smile curled at the corner of Liu Ruyan’s lips.

“Very good.”

“Acquire all the available individual shares on the market!”

“The day after tomorrow, when the stock price has reached its peak, then sell them all at once!”

“Understood.”

Wang Ya nodded and handed another document to Liu Ruyan.

“President Liu, this is your schedule for the coming days…”

Liu Ruyan picked it up, glanced at it casually, and then put it down.

“Go and rest now.”

“Oh, and just let that guy, Ji Bo, do all the dirty work.”

Wang Ya nodded in agreement and then left the office.

Liu Ruyan watched the door close and let out a cold laugh.

【I dreamt of you, dreamt of being with you, for a long, long time.】

"Mmm~"

A happy hum echoed in the office.

On the streets of Jiangcheng.

After finishing his work at the company, Xia Feng didn't go home immediately.

He first went to a private hospital under the Liu Group.

This was a top-tier hospital specifically for the Liu family's children and high-ranking officials.

With Liu Ruyan's help, Zhou Yingying's grandmother had already been transferred to this hospital, receiving the best and most professional care.

He carried a basket of freshly bought fruit and easily found his way to Grandma Zhou's VIP ward.

He pushed open the door and saw Grandma Zhou lying in her hospital bed, engrossed in watching a comedy variety show on TV.

"Grandma, I'm here."

"Oh! It's Xiaofeng!"

Seeing Xia Feng arrive, Grandma Zhou's face immediately lit up with a joyful smile.

She struggled to sit up.

"Come, come sit down!"

She warmly invited Xia Feng to sit down.

Xia Feng quickly went over and gently pressed her back down.

"Grandma, you can just lie there, you don't need to get up."

Xia Feng began to inquire about the old woman's health.

He had acquired [Divine-Level Medical Skill] yesterday, and today he had come to completely cure Grandma Zhou's illness!

Hearing Xia Feng's concern, Grandma Zhou smiled even more happily.

"Oh, these past few days have been so comfortable!"

A satisfied smile spread across her face.

Looking at her handsome, capable, and filial grandson-in-law, Grandma Zhou grew more and more satisfied and fond of him!



Chapter 75 Treating Heart Disease


The two chatted again.

As they talked, Grandma Zhou steered the conversation to Xia Feng's somewhat awkward question.

"Xia Feng,"

Grandma Zhou took Xia Feng's hand, her face filled with anticipation and longing.

"So, when are you and Yingying going to have a child?"

"This old body of mine, I don't even know if I'll live to hold my great-grandchild."

Xia Feng's scalp tingled instantly!

He could only manage a forced laugh and reply,

"Haha, don't worry, Grandma, you're in good health, you'll definitely live to be a hundred!"

"Well… about children, if there's a chance… if there's a chance, we definitely will!"

Grandma Zhou, seeing Xia Feng's embarrassed expression, understood his predicament.

She smiled understandingly and didn't pursue the topic further.

Xia Feng, seeing this, breathed a sigh of relief.

He quickly spoke up, revealing his main purpose for coming here today.

“Grandma, actually, the main reason I came today is to help you treat your heart condition.”

Grandma Zhou was taken aback, thinking she had misheard.

Looking at Xia Feng's incredibly serious eyes, she knew he wasn't joking.

“Xiao Feng, heart disease is no joke.”

“The doctors say they can only slow it down, not completely cure it.”

Xia Feng smiled reassuringly:

“Grandma, don't worry, I know what I'm doing.”

She was touched by Xia Feng's confidence, and her anxiety subsided.

“Then, Xiao Feng, what preparations should I make?”

She asked nervously.

“It's alright, Grandma, just lie down like I used to massage you.”

Xia Feng helped her lie face down on the hospital bed.

“I'll give you a few acupuncture needles, and that should be enough.”

“Just a few acupuncture needles? Is it that magical?”

Grandma Zhou was still full of doubts, wondering what kind of needles could be so powerful.

But she still unconditionally trusted the young man who had brought hope to her family.

She obediently lay down on the hospital bed.

Xia Feng pulled his grandmother's shirt up to her shoulders, revealing the old woman's back, slightly sagging due to age.

With a thought, he took out a set of silver needles from his system space.

It was the purple reward he had won in yesterday's lottery—the [Taiyi Divine Needle].

Xia Feng's eyes instantly focused.

Using the knowledge and instincts granted by [Divine Medical Skill], he picked up a slender silver needle, his movements fluid and graceful.

Without the slightest hesitation, he precisely inserted it into the key acupoint for treating heart disease!

Then, a second, a third…

In the blink of an eye, more than a dozen silver needles of varying lengths were inserted into Grandma Zhou's back.

Having done all this, Xia Feng began to use the techniques of [Divine Massage] to gently yet firmly press on other acupoints.

In this way, he stimulated and strengthened the life force within Grandma Zhou's body, then guided that force to repair her damaged organs.

During this time, Xia Feng was completely focused, and even his forehead was covered in a fine layer of sweat.

This was, after all, a matter of life and death, and he dared not be the slightest bit careless.

Grandma Zhou, lying on the bed, felt an incredibly comfortable warm current slowly flowing through her body.

Wherever that warm current passed, all fatigue and discomfort vanished!

Then, following Xia Feng's movements, that warm current slowly concentrated on her back!

She could clearly feel it!

Her heart was beating stronger and stronger!

No longer beating so weakly as before!

This feeling full of vitality made her groan with pleasure.

…

Sweat began to drip from Xia Feng's forehead.

This was tension.

Because they had now reached the most crucial step!

Using this activated life force to repair the most fundamental defects in Grandma's heart!

This required incredibly precise operation; the slightest error would lead to disastrous consequences!

Without the enhancement of the two golden skills, [Divine Medical Skill] and [Divine Massage], he truly wouldn't dare to do such a thing!

Finally!

After ten full minutes of effort!

Xia Feng slowly exhaled a breath of stale air.

It's done!

He had completely repaired Grandma's heart!

He didn't stop there.

Instead, he continued to guide the remaining life force within his body to nourish Grandma's other organs.

Having done all this, he slowly removed the silver needles inserted into her back, one by one.

Then, he considerately pulled up Grandma's shirt.

The [Taiyi Divine Needles] automatically cleaned and disinfected the moment they were returned to the system space, very conveniently.

Xia Feng took a tissue from the table and wiped the sweat from his forehead.

"Phew—"

"Alright, Grandma, get up and feel how you feel now."

Grandma Zhou obediently sat up from the bed.

She first moved her limbs somewhat dazedly, then tentatively got out of bed.

She stood on the floor.

When she felt her heart pounding strongly in her chest,

and her body brimming with inexhaustible energy, an expression of utter astonishment appeared on her face!

“Xiao Feng! You…you’re amazing!”

“I feel like I’ve become thirty years younger!”

She began to sway left and right, even doing a few chest-expanding exercises.

Feeling her seemingly refreshed and vibrant body!

Finally, she walked up to Xia Feng, her eyes filled with excitement and gratitude.

Her legs went weak, and she was about to kneel before Xia Feng!

“Holy crap! Grandma! What are you doing?!”

Xia Feng was startled and quickly stepped forward to stop her, helping her back to sit up on the bed.

Two streams of hot tears were already streaming down Grandma Zhou’s wrinkled face.

Her withered hands gripped Xia Feng's tightly as she said excitedly,

"Xiao Feng! I...I wanted to thank you for saving my life!"

"This old woman has no way to repay you, so this is the simplest way I could think of!"

Xia Feng patted the back of her hand that was holding his, gently comforting her:

“Grandma, you’re my grandma now, we’re family.”

“Since we’re family, let’s not talk like we’re from two different families.”

“No need for thanks, this is what I should do.”

“I also wanted Grandma to help me take care of my and Yingying’s child.”

He pulled a tissue from the table and handed it to Grandma Zhou.

Grandma Zhou took it, wiping away tears and nodding repeatedly.

“Yes, yes, yes! We’re family! Look at me, so senile, why am I being so formal!”

“Don’t worry! From now on, Grandma will help you take care of your and Yingying’s child!”

Then, as if remembering something, she said to Xia Feng:

“By the way, Xiao Feng, if Yingying does anything wrong, you must tell me! I’ll help you discipline her!”

Xia Feng was both amused and exasperated by this.

"Grandma, Yingying is such a good girl."

"I always feel that sometimes I'm not attentive enough to her, and that I, as her boyfriend, haven't been good enough."

Finally, Xia Feng instructed Grandma Zhou to stay in the hospital for a few more days to observe her condition.

She could be discharged after all the test results were available.



Chapter 76 Preparing to Go to the Liu Family


"Alright, Grandma, I'll be going now."

Xia Feng stood up from his chair, preparing to leave.

"Just rest well, and wait for the hospital to come and do a full check-up."

"Oh, right!"

He walked to the door, then seemed to remember something, turning back to Grandma Zhou and adding,

"Grandma, please don't tell anyone that I treated you."

"I don't have a medical license yet. If people find out, they might arrest me."

"Ah?!"

Grandma Zhou was startled by his words!

"Do you need a license to treat patients these days?!"

In her mind, such things didn't exist.

"Don't worry, Xiao Feng!"

"If anyone asks, I absolutely won't say anything! I'll just say it just happened for no reason!"

Grandma Zhou quickly patted her chest to assure him.

Finally, still worried, she escorted Xia Feng to the door of the ward.

"Xiao Feng, be careful on the road."

"Okay, Grandma."

Xia Feng waved to Grandma Zhou, who was still watching him leave from the doorway, before turning and leaving the hospital.

...

Back in his car, Xia Feng didn't start the engine immediately.

He was thinking about his conversation with Grandma Zhou.

He really should get a medical license.

Otherwise, if he tried to save someone again, it would be considered illegal medical practice, which would cause a lot of unnecessary trouble.

Thinking this, he immediately took out his phone and dialed Liu Ruyan's number.

The call was answered almost instantly.

This speed warmed Xia Feng's heart.

"Hi~ Honey, did you miss me?"

Liu Ruyan's voice, full of surprise and sweetness, came from the other end of the line.

Instantly, the techniques he had learned from the book "Male Virtue" flashed through Xia Feng's mind.

He answered immediately:

"Yes, I missed you."

"Wow~~"

Those three simple words elicited a joyful exclamation from the other end of the phone!

"Mmm! I missed you so much too! Honey!"

"I want to go straight home from get off work right now and be held tightly in your arms!"

"Haha, don't worry, I'll definitely comfort you when I get home tonight."

Xia Feng said with a laugh.

"By the way, Ruyan, can you help me get a medical license?"

Liu Ruyan, who had been incredibly excited on the other end of the phone, changed her tone instantly upon hearing the last part of his question.

"Hmph!"

She huffed, speaking in a resentful tone:

"I knew it! You only call me when you need something!"

"Waaah... I'm so unlucky... I can only be a tool... Waaah..."

As she spoke, she even pretended to cry.

Although Xia Feng knew it was all an act by this little vixen,

hearing her pitiful "crying," he still felt utterly overwhelmed.

He could only helplessly begin to make all sorts of unequal terms.

"Okay, okay, it's my fault, it's my fault."

"Don't cry, my dear wife."

"I promise! Tonight I'll make you queen! I'll let you be on top!"

"And you can play whatever you want! Even wearing a blindfold is fine! It's your choice!"

Xia Feng agreed to all the terms.

The crying on the other end of the phone stopped abruptly.

Liu Ruyan then began to get down to business, satisfied.

"A medical license, right? A piece of cake."

"No problem, I'll get it ready for you within an hour."

"Let me show you the power of your wife's money!"

Her tone was full of confidence and smugness.

"By the way, honey."

"Can you come back to the Liu family home with me tonight?"

"My mom brought Ji Bo over again this morning, and she told me I absolutely have to come home for dinner tonight."

"I really can't refuse, so honey, will you come back with me?"

Xia Feng agreed without hesitation.

"Okay."

"I'll go back with you tonight."

"After all, an ugly son-in-law has to meet his in-laws sooner or later."

"What are you saying!"

Liu Ruyan on the other end of the phone immediately protested!

"How am I ugly?! My husband is the most handsome man in the world! The best man!"

"I won't allow you to say that about yourself! Do you understand?!"

"Okay, okay, I'll listen to my wife."

Xia Feng was amused by her adorable protectiveness.

"Alright, you go ahead and do your work, I'm hanging up."

"Remember! You must come home with me tonight!"

After saying that, Liu Ruyan reluctantly hung up the phone.

Xia Feng put away his phone, the smile on his face gradually fading.

His mind began to wander as he thought about meeting Liu Ruyan's family that evening.

Because of some past reasons, Liu Ruyan's mother had never really liked him.

"Sigh..."

Xia Feng sighed.

"When soldiers come, we'll block them; when water comes, we'll dam it."

"We'll play it by ear."

He drove to the largest traditional Chinese medicine shop in Jiangcheng and began selecting medicinal herbs.

...

While Xia Feng was selecting herbs...

In the villa's room, Zhao Rou, who had fainted from the incredibly pleasurable massage, slowly awoke.

Upon waking, she vaguely recalled what had happened.

When those blush-inducing images flooded her mind,

her pretty face instantly turned bright red!

She pulled the blanket, still carrying Xia Feng's scent, over her head and buried herself completely in it.

"Ugh~"

Sure enough, even a clueless maid like her couldn't withstand such an extreme experience!

After blushing in bed for a while, Zhao Rou finally crawled out of bed.

She carefully folded the blankets, then carried this "trophy," still bearing the scent of her young master, back to her room.

After doing all this, she took her change of clothes and went into the bathroom.

She wanted to take a shower.

Because…

While showering…

When she took off her maid outfit and examined her body…

She was astonished to discover!

The hidden injuries she had sustained from her past rigorous training had all vanished!

She immediately thought of the massage Xia Feng had given her earlier, the one that had made her so comfortable she almost fainted!

Her son-in-law was truly shrouded in mystery.

He seemed to know everything.

Perhaps it was recalling the feeling during the massage.

Her cheeks flushed uncontrollably again.

"Son-in-law..."

An hour later.

Zhao Rou, her steps slightly unsteady, slowly emerged from the bathroom.

...

When Xia Feng returned to the villa with a large pile of medicinal herbs and ingredients, it was almost five in the afternoon.

Checking the time, Xia Feng knew time was running out.

He had to hurry and start preparing the evening's medicinal meal.

Zhao Rou heard the commotion downstairs and crawled out of her newly acquired "trophy" of a bed.

She changed into her light maid outfit before heading to the kitchen on the first floor.

Upon arriving in the kitchen, Zhao Rou saw Xia Feng preparing various Chinese herbs and ingredients.

She asked curiously,

"Young Master, are you making medicinal cuisine?"

Xia Feng also noticed Zhao Rou entering the kitchen.

"Xiao Rou, you're awake."

He nodded with a smile.

"Yes, I'm planning to make some medicinal cuisine to nourish you all."

Zhao Rou stepped forward and naturally began to help.

"Young Master, let me help you."

"I've learned how to make medicinal cuisine before."

Xia Feng watched her skillful movements and couldn't help but admire her.

"You're really versatile."

"Xiao Rou, it's so good to have you in this family."

Hearing Xia Feng's praise, a gentle smile appeared on Zhao Rou's usually expressionless face.



Chapter 77 Targeted Lottery


In the kitchen, the delicate aroma of herbs mingled with the fresh scent of ingredients, filling the air.

Xia Feng and Zhao Rou worked in perfect harmony.

One meticulously prepared the herbs, while the other skillfully chopped the ingredients into the perfect sizes.

Soon, all the preparations were complete.

A pressure cooker and a clay pot sat quietly on the stove, simmering over the fire.

"Phew~"

Xia Feng let out a long breath and glanced at his watch.

It was already 5:30.

He looked at the young maid beside him, quite satisfied.

In their recent collaboration, Zhao Rou's methods for preparing the medicinal cuisine had been remarkably professional.

"Xiao Rou, the rest is up to you."

Xia Feng removed his apron and casually hung it aside.

"I'm going to take a shower first. I'm going back to the Liu family with Ru Yan tonight, so I won't be eating with you."

Zhao Rou stopped what she was doing, turned around, and bowed slightly to Xia Feng.

“Okay, son-in-law, leave the rest to me.”

She looked up, a mischievous glint flashing in her usually calm eyes.

“Would you like me to help you bathe?”

“Huh?”

Xia Feng was stunned for a moment upon hearing this.

He looked at Zhao Rou with some surprise, then saw the fleeting mischievous smile on her face.

Damn!

When did this little girl become so naughty?!

Xia Feng shook his head with amusement, reaching out to gently tug at her smooth, jade-like cheek.

“You, you’ve even learned to joke around.”

It feels really nice.

He silently commented to himself.

“But that’s good, it proves you’ve fully integrated into our family.”

“Keep it up.”

With that, Xia Feng patted her head with satisfaction before turning and walking towards the bathroom on the second floor.

Left behind, Zhao Rou watched Xia Feng's departing figure, slowly raising her hand to touch her cheek where he had just pinched it.

The warmth of his fingertips still lingered there.

"I wasn't joking..."

She murmured softly, a voice only she could hear.

Then, she turned back to her studies, focusing intently on the two pots of medicinal food simmering in the kitchen.

...

Less than ten minutes later.

The villa's front door clicked open from the outside.

It was Liu Ruyan returning.

She had come home unusually early today. As soon as she entered, she tossed her bag onto the entryway cabinet and began searching the living room for the figure she had been longing for.

"Honey! I'm home!"

She called out loudly as she changed her shoes.

From the kitchen, Zhao Rou heard her voice and peeked out.

Liu Ruyan's eyes lit up instantly upon seeing her.

"Xiaorou, is your husband home?"

Zhao Rou nodded and replied,

"Yes, my husband just went upstairs to take a shower. He said he's going back to the Liu family home with you tonight, Ruyan."

"Okay, I'll go take a shower too."

Upon hearing this, Liu Ruyan immediately gave a knowing, mischievous smile.

"You go ahead and do your work."

With that, she hummed a little tune and walked briskly towards the bathroom on the second floor.

In the kitchen, Zhao Rou watched Liu Ruyan's cheerful figure, then glanced at the steaming medicinal soup in the pot.

She actually wanted to join too.

...

In the second-floor bathroom, the sound of running water filled the air.

Xia Feng was enjoying the comfort of the hot water washing over his body with his eyes closed.

Suddenly, he heard the bathroom door being gently pushed open.

He didn't even need to turn around.

Just by the familiar, slightly excited footsteps, he knew who it was.

"Ruyan, you're back so early today?"

He opened his eyes, turned his head, and looked at the stunningly beautiful woman who was smiling as she walked towards him.

"Yes."

Liu Ruyan walked along, skillfully unbuttoning her business suit.

"I'm going home with you tonight, husband, and I also need to see Grandpa, so I had to come back early to prepare."

She casually tossed her clothes into the laundry basket, then sat down on a small stool and began washing her hair.

Xia Feng, gazing at her long, flowing hair, smiled and stood up from the bathtub.

He walked behind her and naturally took over the task from her hands, beginning to wash her hair.

Feeling the gentle yet strong hands now resting on her head.

Liu Ruyan happily squinted her eyes, withdrawing her own hands, like a lazy cat, enjoying Xia Feng's care.

She leaned against Xia Feng, feeling the warmth and scent emanating from him, a sense of peace washing over her.

After a moment's thought, her eyes lit up, and her mind began to work.

She turned to face Xia Feng.

Looking at him like this, Liu Ruyan raised her chin triumphantly, a mischievous smile spreading across her face.

…

Finally, both of them finished washing up and comfortably settled into the large bathtub for a soak.

The warm water enveloped their bodies, making them feel drowsy.

Xia Feng leaned against the bathtub, while Liu Ruyan, like a boneless, beautiful snake, rested her entire body against his chest.

Xia Feng played with her soft hair, then suddenly spoke, asking about the events of the evening.

"Hey, Ruyan, what do you think I should bring when I go back to meet your family?"

Liu Ruyan lazily raised her head, nuzzling against his firm chest.

"Hmm~"

She thought for a moment, then said with some distress,

"I don't know."

"Don't worry about my dad. Just bring him a bottle of good wine, or even nothing, he won't say anything."

"And my mom… hmph, she won't be satisfied with anything you bring, so just don't bring anything, save the money."

"As for my grandfather…"

Liu Ruyan's eyes turned serious.

"His greatest love is all sorts of valuable calligraphy and paintings."

"Calligraphy and paintings..."

Xia Feng's brows furrowed slightly.

These things aren't easy to come by.

Liu Ruyan seemed to sense his distress.

She stretched out her arms and tightly embraced Xia Feng's large hands, comforting him.

"It's alright, husband."

Her voice was full of firmness and tenderness.

"You don't need to bring anything, just yourself."

"Because, I've only ever loved you."

"I don't care what others think or how they see me."

Hearing Liu Ruyan's heartfelt words of love, Xia Feng felt a warm glow in his heart.

To be loved so wholeheartedly by such an outstanding woman was truly an unparalleled blessing.

He was deeply moved.

But moved as he was, he still had to maintain appearances!

He didn't want his beloved woman to lose face in front of his family because of him.

At that moment, he thought of the system.

He silently called out to it in his mind.

"System, are you there?"

"I want to draw a painting or calligraphy that can command respect. Can you do that?"

[Yes, host.]

The system's voice quickly rang in his mind.

[Your request is possible.]

[However, to accurately draw this level of reward, you need to use all your current points for a targeted draw.]

Xia Feng glanced at his points.

During this time, he and Liu Ruyan had worked hard for a long time, and now they had accumulated 230 points again.

Without thinking, he made a decision in his mind.

"Draw!"

"Points can be earned again!"

"Tonight, I'm going to support my wife! I absolutely can't let her down!"

[Received!]

[Special targeted lottery, begin!]

[Ding!]

[Congratulations, host, you have drawn—Dragon and Phoenix Auspiciousness Painting (Tang Yin's authentic work)!]

[Item has been stored in the system space and can be retrieved at any time.]

Holy crap!

An authentic work by Tang Yin?!

And a Dragon and Phoenix Auspiciousness Painting with such a wonderful meaning!

Seeing that the system had actually given him such a good thing, Xia Feng instantly felt confident!

He felt full of power!

He pulled one of Liu Ruyan's hands out of her arms and gave her a light squeeze.

"Ah~"

Liu Ruyan was startled by his sudden attack and let out a gasp.

She turned her head and glared at him reproachfully.

"Honey, what are you doing~"

Xia Feng grinned at her, his face radiating confidence.

"Ruyan, don't worry."

"Tonight, I'll back you up!"

Liu Ruyan's heart fluttered at his confident gaze.

She nodded vigorously.

"Yes, I believe you."

They lingered in the bathtub for a few more minutes.

The two then got up, dried themselves off, and returned to the bedroom.

Next, it was time to choose what to wear that evening.



Chapter 78 The Liu Family Banquet


Liu Ruyan changed into a fiery red strapless gown.

The dress was extremely form-fitting, perfectly outlining her figure, which had become even more voluptuous after being nourished by the summer breeze day and night.

Her curves were exquisite, her waist slender.

Especially the expanse of snow-white skin on her chest, which, against the red backdrop, was dazzling.

Xia Feng's Adam's apple bobbed involuntarily.

He stepped forward, gently encircling her waist from behind, resting his chin on her fragrant shoulder, his voice tinged with a hint of teasing.

"Ruyan, I feel like we're going to some grand banquet, not just having a casual dinner at home?"

Liu Ruyan felt the familiar presence behind her and comfortably narrowed her eyes.

She turned her head and kissed him on the cheek.

"Oh dear, honey, I forgot to tell you."

Her voice carried a hint of apology.

“Tonight’s family dinner is actually my grandfather’s birthday banquet.”

“My grandfather is the patriarch of the Liu family. All the Liu family members return to celebrate his birthday.”

“So you need to dress formally.”

Xia Feng nodded knowingly.

“I see.”

He released Liu Ruyan and walked towards the wardrobe.

“Then it seems I’ll have to wear a suit too.”

He opened the wardrobe door and took out a brand-new, bespoke suit.

This suit was something Liu Ruyan had prepared long ago.

From the moment she decided to set a trap for Xia Feng, she had already anticipated this day.

She imagined herself appearing openly and proudly with this man before all her family.

Therefore, she had long ago commissioned a top designer to tailor this suit for him.

Xia Feng looked at the obviously expensive suit and felt a warmth in his heart.

This woman was always like this, silently preparing everything for you where you couldn’t see it.

He quickly and efficiently put on his suit.

The man in the mirror was tall and imposing, with broad shoulders and long legs.

The black suit added to his composed and sharp appearance, perfectly complementing his already handsome face; he looked like a domineering CEO straight out of a comic book.

Liu Ruyan looked at Xia Feng in the mirror, her eyes practically sparkling.

No wonder he's my man!

He's handsome no matter how you look at him!

She walked up to Xia Feng, noticing his slightly crooked tie, and couldn't help but reach out her hand.

"Your tie is crooked, let me straighten it for you."

Her voice was gentle and soothing.

Xia Feng looked down at Liu Ruyan, who was intently straightening his tie.

She was very close to him.

Close enough that he could clearly smell the delicate fragrance emanating from her hair.

His gaze naturally followed her fair neck, sliding down to that deep abyss…

Xia Feng's brows furrowed involuntarily.

A powerful possessiveness, like vines, instantly entwined his heart!

This won't do!

After Liu Ruyan straightened his tie, she patted his chest with satisfaction.

"All done."

Xia Feng, without a word, turned and went back to the wardrobe.

He rummaged through it for a moment, then took out a red silk shawl with delicate lace trim.

He walked behind Liu Ruyan and draped the shawl over her shoulders.

The luxurious shawl perfectly concealed a large expanse of her bare chest and back.

Xia Feng looked at his handcrafted masterpiece and nodded in satisfaction.

Hmm, much better this way.

Although less skin was exposed, it gave her a dignified and elegant air, making her appear even more noble.

Liu Ruyan was taken aback for a moment, then quickly understood Xia Feng's intention.

Looking at Xia Feng's somewhat domineering yet childish expression, she wasn't angry at all; instead, she burst out laughing.

That smile was like a blooming rose, bright and captivating.

"That's wonderful."

She tiptoed and pecked Xia Feng's lips.

"My husband looks so cute when he's jealous."

Xia Feng blushed slightly at her comment, feeling a little embarrassed.

He coughed lightly, forcibly changing the subject, and took her hand, leading her downstairs.

"Ahem, it's getting late, we should go out."

The two walked hand in hand downstairs.

Xia Feng spoke to Zhao Rou, who was still intently watching the medicinal cuisine in the kitchen.

"Xiao Rou, Ru Yan and I are heading out first."

"The family dinner might end late tonight, so we probably won't be back."

Zhao Rou peeked out from the kitchen and nodded in response.

"Understood, son-in-law."

Her voice was as calm as ever.

"Please be careful on your journey, you and Sister Ru Yan."

Xia Feng nodded, then pulled Liu Ru Yan out.

He planned to drive Liu Ru Yan's flashy red Maserati to the Liu family home.

...

The Liu family, as one of the oldest and most prestigious families in Jiangcheng, could be considered the true local power.

Their mansion was situated atop Crescent Mountain, Jiangcheng's most exclusive upscale neighborhood.

The entire mountaintop belonged to the Liu family.

When Xia Feng arrived at the Liu family manor in his flamboyant red Maserati, even though he was somewhat prepared, he was still slightly surprised by the sight before him.

The enormous parking lot outside the manor was already filled with all sorts of top-of-the-line luxury cars.

Rolls-Royces, Bentleys, Ferraris…

It was practically a world-class luxury car exhibition.

They were placed in a simple yet exquisite wooden box.

Then, like a gentleman, he opened the car door for Liu Ruyan.

Liu Ruyan took his arm, and the two walked side by side toward the imposing, ornately carved iron gate.

A row of security guards in black suits and sunglasses stood at the entrance.

The moment they saw Liu Ruyan, they immediately stood ramrod straight and bowed in unison.

"Greetings, Miss!"

Their voices were loud and clear, exuding authority.

Then, their gazes fell upon the handsome man whose arm Liu Ruyan was intimately holding.

These security guards were shrewd and naturally knew how to play the game.

They bowed again.

"Greetings, Young Master!"

Xia Feng, hearing this "Young Master," felt nothing.

He subconsciously compared it to something else in his mind.

Hmm, it still doesn't sound as good as my Xiaorou's greeting.

Xiao Rou's cry was so sincere and full of dependence.

Xia Feng nodded to them, then walked into the manor with Liu Ruyan.

Passing through a garden manicured like a work of art, the two arrived at a brightly lit building.

This was the Liu family's banquet hall.

The hall was about the size of a large stadium.

A giant crystal chandelier hung from the high ceiling, radiating dazzling light.

The spacious hall was filled with long tables covered with pristine white tablecloths.

Various fine wines, champagne, and premium cigarettes were already laid out on the tables.

A considerable number of people had already gathered in the hall.

They were in small groups, holding wine glasses, chatting and laughing.

These people were all members of the Liu family.

"Sister Ruyan, you're back!"

"Hello, Sister Ruyan!"

"Sister Ruyan, this must be your brother-in-law, right? He's so handsome!"

Xia Feng was also experiencing such a scene for the first time, and could only smile and nod in acknowledgment.

"So grand."

He was telling the truth.

Although the Lin family he belonged to was a considerable clan, it was related to the early death of his grandfather when he was young.

After his father became the head of the family, he disliked these formalities, so the family remained much like an ordinary household.

“Heh, don’t be fooled by how glamorous things seem on the surface.”

“It’s better to go home early, hug you beauties, and comfortably lie on the sofa watching TV.”

Liu Ruyan was amused by his lighthearted remark and gave him a light pat on the shoulder.

“Alright, stop joking.”

“I’ll take you to meet my parents and grandfather.”

She led Xia Feng through the crowd towards the head table at the very front of the hall, a table significantly larger than the others.

That was a seat reserved only for core members of Liu Ruyan's lineage.

As Xia Feng drew closer, he could see who was sitting there.

It was Liu Jianguo, the patriarch of the Liu family and Liu Ruyan's grandfather, sitting upright, a string of gleaming Buddhist prayer beads in his hand, his eyes slightly closed, exuding an air of quiet authority.

The current head of the Liu family, Liu Ruyan's father, Liu Cangyun, sat somewhat reserved, glancing frequently at his wife's expression—a typical henpecked husband.

Liu Ruyan's mother, Li Mei, wore an icy expression. When she saw Xia Feng, her eyes revealed undisguised disgust and contempt.

Beside them sat someone who surprised Xia Feng.

It was Ji Bo.

He was also dressed in an expensive suit, a smile on his face, sitting a seat next to Li Mei, albeit a bit far away.

However, his father, Ji Er, hadn't come along.

His presence at this level of the Liu family banquet was entirely due to Li Mei's connections.

Liu Ruyan took a deep breath, her smile becoming standard and polite.

She led Xia Feng to the front of the group, greeting them with a graceful smile.

"Dad, Mom, Grandpa, good evening."

Then, she pulled Xia Feng forward a step and solemnly introduced him:

"This is my husband, Xia Feng."

"I brought him here today especially to introduce him to you."



Chapter 79 This, this is...


Xia Feng's gaze calmly swept over the three people at the table, neither servile nor arrogant, a gentle smile on his face.

"Dad, Mom, Grandpa, hello."

"I am Ruyan's husband, Xia Feng."

He bowed slightly, nodding to the three elders with perfect poise.

"Hmph."

A disdainful snort escaped Li Mei's nostrils.

She didn't even bother to look at Xia Feng directly, simply turning her head to the side.

Her disdainful expression made it seem as if even a glance would offend her eyes.

However, she only snorted and said nothing more.

After all, the backbone of the Liu family, Old Master Liu Jianguo, hadn't spoken yet.

Although she could completely control Liu Cangyun at home, in this situation, she didn't have the right to overstep her bounds in front of the old man.

Liu Jianguo slowly opened his half-closed eyes.

A glint of shrewdness flashed in those seemingly cloudy old eyes.

He sized Xia Feng up and down.

Hmm, not bad.

Tall and straight posture.

A sunny and cheerful demeanor, clear eyes, without the slightest timidity or evasion.

To remain so calm and composed in front of him—that composure alone surpassed that of many young people his age.

Liu Jianguo nodded silently in his heart.

He spoke slowly, his voice, though aged, was full of strength.

"Yes, I'm glad Xiao Ruyan likes it."

"Sit down first."

A simple sentence, yet it was like a royal decree, instantly determining Xia Feng's status.

Liu Ruyan knew that her grandfather had initially approved of Xia Feng!

A radiant smile instantly bloomed on her face, and she happily pulled Xia Feng to sit down in the empty seat next to her.

Li Mei's face immediately turned ugly, as if she had swallowed a fly.

Ji Bo, standing beside her, also wore a strange expression; his smug smile froze on his face.

Neither of them spoke.

One was merely a woman, not daring to be disrespectful in front of the old man.

The other was an outsider who only got to sit there because of Li Mei's connections; he had no right to speak.

The atmosphere became somewhat awkward.

Just then, Xia Feng spoke up.

He gently placed the seemingly antique wooden gift box on the table.

"Grandpa, today is your birthday banquet, and I didn't prepare anything particularly valuable."

"I just heard from Ruyan that you usually like calligraphy and paintings, so I took the liberty of bringing a small gift to wish you a happy birthday."

Xia Feng had barely finished speaking.

Li Mei, who had been holding back her anger, finally found her chance to lash out!

She looked at the seemingly ordinary gift box and scoffed.

"Ha, a small gift?"

Her voice wasn't loud, but it was full of sarcasm.

"What good stuff could a poor boy who's lost his status as the young master of the Lin family possibly have?"

"I bet it's just some junk he bought from a street stall. He dares to show it off like that."

After saying that, she immediately turned to Ji Bo beside her, her face instantly transforming into one of pride and smugness.

"Speaking of gifts, little Ji Bo has specially prepared a calligraphy and painting for you, sir!"

She gave Ji Bo a look.

Ji Bo understood immediately and stood up.

He also took out an exquisitely wrapped gift box, held it with both hands, and respectfully placed it on the table.

"Hello, Grandpa Liu."

His voice was full of humility and politeness.

"I heard from your wife that you like calligraphy and paintings. I'm not very talented, so I've prepared a small gift. Please accept it."

Li Mei immediately chimed in, deliberately raising her voice so everyone around could hear.

"Yes, Dad! I heard from Ji Bo that this painting cost tens of millions. He specially commissioned one of the top calligraphy and painting masters in the country to create it just for you!"

Liu Ruyan was so angry that her ample bosom trembled violently!

She was about to slam her hand on the table and argue with her materialistic mother!

But a warm, large hand gently pressed down on her hand under the table.

It was Xia Feng.

He shook his head at her, his eyes filled with reassurance and confidence.

“Ruyan, no need.”

“Just wait and see the show.”

Liu Jianguo looked at the two gift boxes on the table, a smile appearing on his face.

He hadn't originally wanted to open the gifts in public.

After all, he knew Xia Feng's current situation; what decent gifts could he possibly have now?

Opening them on the spot would only embarrass him.

But seeing Xia Feng's calm and composed demeanor, a hint of curiosity arose in his heart.

What was this kid up to?

“Alright.”

Liu Jianguo nodded.

“Since you two youngsters are so thoughtful, then this old man will certainly open his eyes and feast his eyes today.”

He first pointed to Ji Bo's gift box.

“Take a look at this first.”

Liu Cangyun immediately stood up.

He carefully opened the gift box and took out the scroll inside.

As the scroll slowly unfurled, a magnificent landscape painting instantly appeared before everyone's eyes!

The painting depicted towering mountains, swirling clouds and mist, and rushing rivers—a truly awe-inspiring sight!

Liu Jianguo examined it carefully and nodded in satisfaction.

“Not bad, not bad.”

He praised.

“The painting is steady and grand, the brushstrokes conveying the power of mountains and rivers. It's indeed a well-made piece.”

Although it was a compliment, his tone was very calm, as if he were commenting on a student's work.

Upon hearing this, Ji Bo quickly waved his hand modestly.

"Not at all, Grandpa Liu, you flatter me."

"I just thought it wouldn't be appropriate to be so casual at your birthday banquet."

"So I used my connections to find a renowned calligrapher and painter I know, and commissioned him to paint this to add auspiciousness to your celebration."

His words were humble, but the wide grin that almost reached his ears betrayed his inner pride and arrogance.

After Liu Jianguo offered a few comments, he gestured for Liu Cangyun to reroll the painting and put it back.

Then, his gaze fell on Xia Feng's gift box.

Liu Cangyun took Xia Feng's box and helped the old man open it.

As the scroll painting, also a scroll, was slowly unfurled,

a lifelike painting of dragons and phoenixes, depicting auspiciousness, was revealed to everyone.

The dragon in the painting was powerful and vigorous, the phoenix magnificent and noble, both soaring and dancing amidst auspicious clouds, their vibrant energy brimming with joy and peace.

However, the moment he saw the painting!

Liu Jianguo was completely stunned!

Li Mei, who knew nothing about art, glanced at it and found it less appealing than Ji Bo's landscape painting.

She immediately launched into a new round of mockery.

"Ha, what a tasteless poor boy."

"He specially picked out such a common painting as a gift, how low-class!"

Ji Bo didn't speak, but his face also revealed undisguised mockery.

Liu Ruyan was trembling with anger, about to explode.

Xia Feng gently patted her shoulder, then gestured with his eyes for her to look in the direction of Old Master Liu.

Liu Ruyan followed his gaze.

Grandpa Liu's hand was gently stroking the painting.

His hand, covered in age spots, was trembling slightly.

His lips quivered, and he mumbled something.

"This...this is..."

Li Mei also noticed something was wrong.

She leaned closer and asked suspiciously,

"Dad, what's wrong? It's just a common painting, what's so interesting about it?"

"Shut up!"

A furious shout erupted from Liu Jianguo's mouth!



Chapter 80 Clown Ji Bo


"Shut up!"

Liu Jianguo's thunderous roar, like a thunderclap, exploded in the brightly lit hall!

Everyone around was stunned by this sudden outburst!

The entire hall fell silent instantly, so quiet you could hear a pin drop.

All eyes turned to the head of the table, faces filled with shock and confusion.

What...what's going on?

Why is Old Master Liu so angry?

Li Mei, the one who was yelled at, trembled violently, her face turning deathly pale!

She stood there, frozen in fear.

Liu Jianguo, however, completely ignored everyone else.

His eyes were now fixed solely on the painting of a dragon and phoenix on the table.

He stretched out his wrinkled hand, caressing the scroll gently as if it were a priceless treasure.

His gaze traveled from the lifelike dragon to the magnificent phoenix, finally settling on a small, somewhat blurred red seal in the lower right corner.

When he clearly saw the words on the seal, his pupils constricted sharply!

His breathing quickened!

After a long while,

he carefully rolled up the scroll again and placed it with utmost care back into the antique wooden box.

Having done all this, he slowly raised his head.

A kind smile appeared on his usually stern face!

He looked at Xia Feng, his eyes filled with excitement and admiration!

"Little Feng..."

His voice trembled slightly with emotion.

"This painting of yours... is it an authentic work by Tang Yin?"

Boom—!!!

These words were even more shocking than the roar just now!

Everyone present felt their heads buzzing!

An authentic work by Tang Yin?!

All eyes instantly focused on the young man who was calmly holding Liu Ruyan's hand!

Their eyes were filled with disbelief and shock!

My God!

That's an authentic work by Tang Yin that has long been lost!

This thing... cannot be measured in money!

It's already a national treasure!

Xia Feng, seeing the shocked looks on everyone's faces, still wore his gentle smile.

He smiled at Liu Jianguo and said casually,

"Well, Grandpa, to be honest, I'm not too sure either."

"Because this painting was a gift from a friend."

"He found out about my marriage to Ruyan and gave me this auspicious painting as a wedding present."

"And since today is your birthday banquet, Grandpa, I thought I'd take this opportunity to present this auspicious gift to you."

Xia Feng spoke lightly.

But as Liu Jianguo listened, his hand, which was stroking the wooden box, trembled even more violently!

His gaze towards Xia Feng grew increasingly appreciative and satisfied!

What a fine lad!

With his discerning eye honed by a lifetime of immersion in calligraphy and painting, he was certain this painting was an authentic work by Tang Yin, without a doubt!

And Xia Feng's calm and composed demeanor throughout showed that he knew the painting's value!

This was a priceless treasure to him, a man who loved painting more than life itself!

And this grandson-in-law had simply given it to him without batting an eye!

Such magnanimity! Such boldness!

It was something only extraordinary people possessed!

At this moment, the most ashamed were Li Mei and Ji Bo.

Their faces stung as if they'd been slapped hard across the face!

Especially considering that just minutes before, they had been arrogantly mocking Xia Feng's work as utter garbage.

They felt even more humiliated.

Especially Ji Bo!

His so-called "masterpiece," which he'd spent tens of millions on and confidently presented, was nothing but trash compared to Xia Feng's national treasure!

He felt like everyone's gaze was a sharp needle piercing him!

His face flushed, then paled, finally turning a hideous liver color!

In stark contrast to them was Liu Ruyan.

At this moment, she looked at the man holding her hand with eyes full of adoration.

Her heart was completely filled with immense pride and happiness!

Countless sparkling stars shone in her eyes!

This is my man!

This is my most beloved and proud husband!

He always manages to be my savior like an invincible hero in the most crucial moments!

From childhood, when he single-handedly fought dozens to protect her and Lin Yu, it was always like this!

And now, when he casually produced a national treasure to save face, it was still the same!

He has never changed!

An indescribable warmth welled up in Liu Ruyan's heart.

She subconsciously stroked her long legs slightly.

She immediately pulled Xia Feng's entire arm tightly into her embrace!

Feeling her arm suddenly enveloped by that amazing softness.

Xia Feng turned to Liu Ruyan, giving her a doting smile.

Looking at his profile, which now appeared even more handsome and dashing, Liu Ruyan felt her heart melt, and her eyes welled up with tears.

"Good, good, good!"

Liu Jianguo, seeing the loving couple, exclaimed "Good!" three times with delight!

"Our Ruyan is so lucky to have married you!"

"Come, come, everyone, don't stand, sit down! Let's eat, let's eat!"

Old Master Liu happily gestured for everyone to sit down again.

Then, he carefully handed the wooden box to Liu Cangyun beside him.

"Cangyun, you personally put this in the safe in my study."

"Remember, be very careful, don't bump it!"

Liu Cangyun carefully took the wooden box, then glanced at Ji Bo's gift box on the table, and asked Liu Jianguo:

"Dad, what about this?"

Liu Jianguo casually waved his hand, not even glancing at it.

"That? Just find someone to put it in my storage room, which is for miscellaneous items."

"Pfft—"

Upon hearing this, Ji Bo felt as if he had been stabbed in the heart, almost spitting out a mouthful of blood!

Storage room?!

The painting he spent tens of millions preparing was only fit to be treated as junk?!

Liu Cangyun, being a shrewd man, immediately understood the old man's meaning.

He nodded.

"Understood, Dad."

Then, he personally took Xia Feng's box and casually called a servant to take Ji Bo's box, leaving his seat to put them away.

The atmosphere at the dinner table changed drastically.

Liu Jianguo pulled Xia Feng aside and began asking him all sorts of questions, showing concern for their lives.

"Xia Feng, is there anything you need help with lately? If so, just tell Grandpa, and Grandpa will take care of it!"

Xia Feng smiled and raised his glass to the old man.

"No, no, Grandpa, I don't need anything. Ruyan is taking good care of me."

"That's good, that's good."

Liu Jianguo nodded in satisfaction.

Suddenly, as if he had thought of something, he dropped a bombshell!

"By the way, Xiaofeng, how about this, I'll give you 20% of the Liu Group's shares."

"That way, you and Ruyan can work together, and you'll have someone to look after you in the company. What do you think?"

Xia Feng quickly waved his hand.

"Grandpa, really, that's unnecessary."

He glanced at Liu Ruyan beside him and said with a smile:

"Shares are useless to me. But I can give them directly to Ruyan."

"That way, she'll have more say in the company, and I, as her husband, will feel more at ease."

Liu Jianguo's eyes lit up instantly upon hearing this!

Good lad! Not greedy or covetous! He's always thinking of his granddaughter!

He couldn't be more satisfied!

He nodded, then turned to look at Li Mei, whose face had become quite pale.

“Xiaomei.”

“Don’t you also hold 20% of the group’s shares?”

“I think you should transfer them directly to Ruyan sometime.”

“You’re getting old. Don’t worry about the company anymore. Just follow Cangyun and enjoy life.”

Li Mei’s heart sank!

Although she was extremely unwilling, she couldn’t refuse Liu Jianguo’s arrangement!

She could only grit her teeth and squeeze out a few words.

“I understand, Dad.”

“I…I’ll go and handle the share transfer tomorrow.”

Liu Jianguo nodded in satisfaction, then continued chatting happily with Xia Feng, as if they were grandfather and grandson.

Throughout the meal, Ji Bo was left out like a ghost.

He could only sit awkwardly to the side, drinking silently, sip by sip.

Xia Feng thought he should wear a red nose.

Hurry back to Gotham, Batman said he won't hit you anymore.



Chapter 81 Kidney Deficiency, I Can Cure It


After several rounds of drinks, the banquet reached its climax.

The Liu family members present all recognized Xia Feng, Liu Ruyan's husband.

Liu Ruyan leaned against Xia Feng, her pretty face flushed, her eyes sparkling, every gesture exuding captivating charm.

She picked up the glass of wine in front of her, about to take a sip.

A large hand gently pressed down on her wrist.

"Husband, what's wrong?"

Liu Ruyan looked up at Xia Feng, puzzled, at him stopping her.

Xia Feng's eyes were full of concern.

"Your period is due in a few days, isn't it?"

He said, taking the wine glass from her hand and replacing it with a glass of warm water he had prepared beforehand.

"Don't drink alcohol."

"Here, drink more hot water, it's good for your health."

"I'll help you relax and improve your circulation later, I promise you won't feel any pain."

"Okay!"

Liu Ruyan nodded obediently and took the steaming cup of water.

She held the cup with both hands and sipped it slowly.

A warm current slid from her throat into her stomach, then spread throughout her body.

But even warmer than the hot water was her heart.

She hadn't expected Xia Feng to be so considerate.

He remembered her menstrual cycle perfectly.

This feeling of being cherished and loved made her heart feel like it was filled with honey, so sweet it was almost melting.

Her eyes almost overflowed with tears as she looked at Xia Feng.

And this scene was clearly seen by the Liu family members at the head table.

Looking at the affectionate couple, Liu Jianguo smiled with satisfaction and nodded.

Liu Cangyun also looked approving, thinking to himself that entrusting his daughter to him was definitely the right decision.

Even Li Mei, who had always had a stern face, softened her gaze.

Seeing Xia Feng's unconsciously considerate actions, her sharp tongue disappeared.

This young man, though his current status wasn't high, truly cared for his daughter.

Liu Jianguo smiled as he looked at the two younger generation, growing more and more fond of them.

Just then, Xia Feng suddenly turned to Liu Jianguo and asked,

"Grandpa, have you been sleeping poorly lately?"

This question immediately stunned Liu Jianguo!

"Xiao Feng, how did you know?!"

He looked at Xia Feng in astonishment, his face filled with disbelief.

“Yes, I don’t know what’s wrong with me lately. I toss and turn at night, just can’t sleep, and I have no energy during the day.”

“I thought it was just old age, that I’m no longer useful.”

Liu Jianguo chuckled self-deprecatingly.

Xia Feng, however, shook his head, a confident smile on his face.

“No, Grandpa.”

“I know a little bit of medicine. You just caught a cold recently because the weather turned cool, causing some imbalance in your qi and blood.”

“It’s nothing serious. I’ll give you a couple of acupuncture points later to clear your meridians.”

“Oh?”

Liu Jianguo was genuinely surprised this time!

“Xiao Feng, you even know medicine?”

He hadn’t expected his grandson-in-law to know traditional Chinese medicine!

Moreover, with just a glance, he could accurately describe his recent physical condition!

Based on this alone, Liu Jianguo knew that Xia Feng's medical skills were absolutely extraordinary!

Xia Feng turned his gaze to Liu Ruyan's father, Liu Cangyun.

Xia Feng thought that since he was going to make a show of himself, he might as well do it thoroughly.

He wanted to cultivate a good relationship with this father-in-law!

He beckoned to Liu Cangyun, signaling him to come over.

"Dad, I have something I want to tell you."

Although Liu Cangyun was somewhat suspicious, Xia Feng was now a favorite of the old man, so he naturally dared not be negligent.

He leaned closer, intending to hear what Xia Feng had to say.

"Just say what you have to say, there are no outsiders here."

Li Mei couldn't help but speak up.

She was also very curious about what this increasingly unfathomable son-in-law was up to this time.

Her tone was no longer as harsh as before; clearly, Xia Feng's previous behavior was starting to make her accept him as her son-in-law.

Xia Feng smiled somewhat embarrassedly.

"Mom, this...this is a rather private matter, so it's better to talk to Dad alone."

"You can ask Dad directly later."

After saying that, he whispered a few words in Liu Cangyun's ear, in a voice only the two of them could hear.

Liu Cangyun's expression changed drastically at a visible speed!

From initial doubt, to shock, to disbelief, and finally to boundless ecstasy!

He grabbed Xia Feng's hand!

The force was so great, it felt as if he wanted to crush Xia Feng's hand bones!

"Really?!"

Liu Cangyun's voice trembled violently with excitement!

"Xiao Feng! You...what you just said, is it all true?!"

Xia Feng knew why he was so excited.

Just moments ago, he had instantly discerned his father-in-law's greatest hidden ailment.

He was a typical "three-second man" (a man who only lasts three seconds).

And Xia Feng had just told him that he could cure him!

Under his burning gaze, Xia Feng nodded earnestly.

"Hmm."

"After the banquet, I'll give you a couple of acupuncture treatments, Dad, along with some massage. You can try it out right there."

"However, for a complete cure, it's best to combine it with medication."

"I'll write you a prescription later. If you're worried, you can have a trusted doctor review it."

"Dad! What are you doing!"

Liu Ruyan immediately protested when she saw Xia Feng's furrowed brow!

She slapped Liu Cangyun's hand away, then tenderly grasped Xia Feng's hand, gently rubbing it.

"You're hurting my husband!"

Liu Cangyun then realized his lapse in composure and quickly smiled apologetically.

"Haha, Dad got too excited, it's Dad's fault, I'm sorry, Xiaofeng."

Xia Feng, his hand held by Liu Ruyan, could only shake his head at him.

"It's alright, Dad."

"After the banquet, I'll show it to you and Grandpa first."

"Okay, okay!"

Liu Cangyun responded repeatedly, then sat back down in his seat with a happy expression.

As soon as he sat down, Li Mei grabbed him from beside him.

"Old Liu! Tell me! What did that kid say to you? Why are you so excited?"

Liu Cangyun glanced at Xia Feng, who was still clinging to his daughter, then secretly leaned close to Li Mei's ear and repeated what he had just said.

Li Mei froze upon hearing it!

The next second, two blazing flames instantly ignited in her usually cold and sharp eyes!

My God!

Is this true?!

You see, since marrying into the Liu family, she had never truly been satisfied!

She wasn't the kind of woman who would have an affair, so she could only pour all her energy into her career, using frantic work to numb herself.

It was precisely this long-term repression and dissatisfaction that made her increasingly irritable and controlling.

And Liu Cangyun, precisely because he felt so guilty towards his wife, was so obedient and compliant to her every whim.

After all, it was all his own fault!

But now…

This son-in-law she had always looked down on was actually saying he could cure her?!

Then…then wasn't he her savior?! Her benefactor?!

Thinking back to how she had previously mocked and looked down on him,

Li Mei's face burned with embarrassment; she wished she could disappear into the ground!

No!

She had to change her attitude!

She, Li Mei, wasn't some indecisive woman!

Having figured this out, her gaze towards Xia Feng instantly became incredibly warm and affectionate!

…

Soon, the birthday banquet, with its several dramatic shifts in atmosphere, finally came to an end.

The Liu family's territory was large enough that several detached villas were built on the estate, specifically for the Liu family members who had traveled from afar to attend the banquet.

Xia Feng, however, followed Liu Jianguo and his entourage to the core residential area belonging to their main branch.



Chapter 82 Li Mei's Apology


Ji Bo, still wearing what he thought was a gentle smile, naturally intended to follow Li Mei to the main villa.

In his mind, this was just another place to further their relationship.

However, he had only taken one step.

Li Mei's icy voice came from ahead, like a bucket of ice water poured over his head!

"Ji Bo, you should go back first."

She didn't pause, not even turning to look at him.

"What happens next is our family matter."

One sentence, and he was completely excluded!

Ji Bo was dumbfounded!

His body froze on the spot, his smile instantly freezing.

Huh?

Wait…

What's going on?!

Just now at the dinner table, she was calling me "Little Ji Bo"!

How come her attitude has become so distant and cold in just one meal?!

"Weren't you my biggest supporter?!"

His mind was a complete mess; he couldn't understand what had happened in the past half hour!

He tried to salvage the situation, unwilling to give up.

"Um... Auntie, I think..."

"No, you don't."

Li Mei's voice was firm and resolute, brooking no argument!

"Go back."

She interrupted Ji Bo directly, then turned and walked into the brightly lit main villa without looking back, leaving the bewildered man completely behind.

Ji Bo stood alone in the courtyard outside the villa.

The night wind blew, swirling a few fallen leaves, making his figure appear particularly desolate and forlorn.

Two tall security guards appeared beside him.

"Mr. Ji, please come with us."

One of the guards said expressionlessly.

"The mistress said you should leave."

With that, the two women, one on each side, grabbed his arms before he could react, half-dragging, half-pulling him down Crescent Moon Mountain.

...

Meanwhile.

Li Mei quickly entered a spacious bedroom.

Upon entering, she saw Xia Feng already administering acupuncture to Liu Jianguo.

Xia Feng told Liu Jianguo to take off his shirt and lie comfortably on the bed.

"Grandpa, please lie down comfortably. I'll give you a few acupuncture needles and a simple massage."

"Okay, okay, thank you for your help, Xiao Feng."

Liu Jianguo was now completely obedient to his grandson-in-law, overjoyed.

Without a word, he immediately took off his Tang suit, revealing his still-strong upper body despite his age, and then lay down on the soft bed.

Xia Feng pretended to take something out of his pocket, but actually, with a thought, he retrieved the [Taiyi Divine Needle] set from his system space.

He picked up a silver needle, his eyes instantly focusing!

He swiftly located several key acupoints on Liu Jianguo's back, his movements fluid and decisive, inserting the needles with pinpoint accuracy.

Then, he extended his hands and began a gentle yet firm massage on the acupoints on Liu's back where the needles were not.

"Mmm..."

Liu Jianguo felt waves of warmth, accompanied by indescribable comfort, instantly spreading throughout his body from where Xia Feng's hands touched!

The feeling was so pleasant that he couldn't help but groan!

Ten minutes later.

Xia Feng had collected all the silver needles.

“Alright, Grandpa, get up and feel how you are now.”

Liu Jianguo, who was almost asleep in comfort, heard Xia Feng's words and slowly sat up in bed.

He first stretched his stiff limbs, then got off and jumped up and down on the spot!

“Amazing! Amazing!”

Liu Jianguo's face showed an expression of immense joy!

“I feel full of energy! I feel at least twenty years younger! I feel like I could kill a bull!”

He hadn't expected Xia Feng's medical skills to be so superb!

Our Ruyan has truly struck gold!

Just with this extraordinary skill, Xia Feng could become a top guest wherever he goes!

Liu Cangyun, watching from the side, was already itching with anticipation!

He rubbed his hands, his face full of anticipation as he asked Xia Feng.

"Um...Xiao Feng, isn't it my turn?"

Xia Feng looked at him and shook his head with a smile.

He turned his head and looked at Li Mei, who had been standing quietly to his side since they came in, her eyes filled with complicated emotions.

"Dad, don't rush, let me massage Mom first, what do you think?"

Li Mei hadn't expected Xia Feng to bring her up!

She thought that because she had treated him so badly before, he would definitely hold a grudge and dislike her.

"Me...me?!"

She pointed to herself, speaking in disbelief.

Xia Feng gave her a gentle smile and nodded.

"Yes, Mom."

A simple address, a word of affirmation.

Yet, Li Mei's eyes uncontrollably welled up with tears.

This young man, far from holding a grudge, was even willing to take the initiative to treat her health…

She quickly raised her hand to touch the corner of her eye, forcibly suppressing the tears that were about to well up, then hurried to Xia Feng.

“Then…then what should I do?”

Her voice carried a hint of nervousness and unease.

“Do…do I need to take off my clothes?”

At the end, a rare blush appeared on her well-maintained face.

Xia Feng quickly waved his hand.

“No, no.”

“Mom, you can just lie down, I'll massage you and regulate your blood and energy.”

Li Mei nodded.

But before proceeding, she did something that surprised everyone.

She bowed deeply to Xia Feng.

“I'm sorry, Xiao Feng!”

Her voice was filled with sincere apology.

"I apologize for everything I did and said to you before!"

"If you can forgive me, I'll do anything you ask!"

Xia Feng quickly stepped forward and helped Li Mei up.

"Mom, what are you doing?"

"I understand, please don't do this."

He looked at Li Mei's sincere expression and sighed.

"After all, in your eyes before, I was indeed just a poor boy who had lost his family status and had nothing, wasn't I?"

"Everything you did was for Ru Yan and the future of the entire Liu Group."

“So, I don’t blame you.”

Xia Feng’s words made Li Mei feel even more ashamed.

“I only have one small request.”

Xia Feng continued.

“I hope that in the future, you won’t be so strict with Ruyan anymore. Let her have more freedom, okay?”

Looking into Xia Feng’s sincere eyes and listening to his words, which were all for his daughter’s sake.

Li Mei nodded heavily!

Then, she turned to look at Liu Ruyan, who was equally shocked.

“Ruyan, it’s because I was too controlling of you before.”

“It turns out that I’m really getting old, and my judgment isn’t as good as yours.”

“From now on, do whatever you want.”

“I’ll support you!”

Liu Ruyan was completely stunned!

She never expected that her mother, who had strictly controlled her every word and action since childhood, would say such a thing to her!

This feeling was too unreal!

"N-nothing...it's nothing."

She could only reply dryly.

She hadn't yet recovered from this immense surprise and change.

She looked up at the man smiling at her.

All of this was brought about by him.

Liu Ruyan felt her heart melting with this overwhelming happiness.

She looked at Xia Feng, her already moist eyes now seeming to overflow with tears.



Chapter 83 Empress Ruyan's Reward


“Alright, Mom, you can lie down now.”

Xia Feng gestured to the still somewhat awkward Li Mei.

Li Mei took a deep breath, obediently walked to the bedside, and lay down.

To avoid embarrassment, and also to allow himself to concentrate more on his medical skills.

He turned to Liu Jianguo and Liu Cangyun, who were still standing beside him, and said:

“Grandpa, Dad, could you please go out for a moment? I need a quiet environment.”

“Okay, okay, we won’t disturb you.”

Liu Jianguo immediately nodded, pulling the still somewhat reluctant Liu Cangyun out of the room.

Once only the three of them were left in the room, Xia Feng officially began.

His hands gently landed on Li Mei’s back.

The instant his hands roamed over her back!

“Ugh…”

Li Mei’s body trembled violently!

An indescribable feeling of comfort, like an electric current, instantly coursed through her entire body!

She felt as if the pent-up frustration and anger that had accumulated within her for over a decade had finally found an outlet!

She couldn't control her voice, letting out suppressed moans.

"Ah~"

Liu Ruyan, watching her mother's state, blushed crimson!

She couldn't bear to watch any longer!

She quickly walked over, grabbed a clean towel, and shoved it into Li Mei's mouth.

"Mom! Bite down!"

Then, she gave Xia Feng a disapproving glare before continuing to watch anxiously.

Xia Feng smiled helplessly, his hands moving without pause.

His [Divine-Level Medical Skill] allowed him to clearly sense that Li Mei's physical condition was worse than he had imagined.

Years of emotional repression and accumulated desires had caused severe stagnation of her Qi and blood, affecting her internal organs to varying degrees.

No wonder she had become so irritable and controlling.

These were all illnesses!

Xia Feng increased his pressure.

He guided the flow of blood and energy within her body, beginning to unblock her congested meridians.

Li Mei, lying on the bed, trembled violently, like a leaf.

But she could clearly feel the invisible shackles that had plagued her for half her life being gradually broken!

This feeling…it was truly wonderful!

Because Li Mei's condition was somewhat unique, Xia Feng needed to spend more time completely harmonizing the chaotic blood and energy within her body.

By the time he finally finished, half an hour had passed.

Xia Feng slowly withdrew his hands, letting out a long breath.

A fine layer of sweat appeared on his forehead.

Just then, a glass of perfectly warm water was brought to his lips.

It was Liu Ruyan.

She had already poured the water sometime earlier and had been waiting beside him.

"Honey, you've worked hard. Have some water and rest."

Her eyes were filled with concern.

"Thank you, wife."

Xia Feng felt a warmth in his heart, thanked her, and took the water glass, drinking it all in one gulp.

Liu Ruyan walked to the bedside and looked at Li Mei, who was still lying on the bed, her body trembling slightly.

"Mom, how are you feeling now?"

Hearing Liu Ruyan's voice, Li Mei slowly came back to her senses from that intense feeling of comfort.

She removed the towel from her mouth and got out of bed.

She stretched lazily, her bones cracking with each breath!

"It feels... better than ever!"

Feeling the invisible shackles completely broken, her whole body was filled with lightness and vitality!

Li Mei exclaimed sincerely.

She turned to look at her son-in-law, who was resting beside her.

She walked over and looked at him with utmost sincerity.

"Thank you, Xiao Feng."

"From now on, if you need anything, if you need my help, just tell me, and I'll do anything for you!"

Xia Feng smiled and waved his hand.

"Mom, we're all family, no need for formalities."

"You're being too polite."

"Yes! We're family!"

Li Mei nodded happily.

"Mm!"

Liu Ruyan, watching this harmonious scene, smiled and opened the door.

Outside the door, Liu Cangyun had been waiting impatiently.

Liu Jianguo had already gone back to rest.

“Xiaofeng, is it my turn?”

As soon as the door opened, Liu Cangyun rushed in impatiently, looking at Xia Feng expectantly.

“Old Liu!”

Li Mei frowned, immediately scolding him!

“What’s the rush?! Xiaofeng just finished treating me, he’s very tired. Can’t you let him rest first?!”

“Xiaofeng, if you’re tired, you can rest today. We can deal with your father’s matter tomorrow, there’s no rush.”

She was finding this son-in-law more and more pleasing to the eye; how could she bear to let him be tired?

Xia Feng stood up, giving Li Mei a reassuring smile.

"No need, Mom, I'm fine."

"I'm in great shape, you can ask Ruyan if you don't believe me."

Liu Ruyan's pretty face flushed red instantly!

She glared at Xia Feng, embarrassed and annoyed.

Xia Feng laughed, stopping teasing her, and turned to Liu Cangyun.

"Dad, take off your shirt and lie down."

"I'll help you right now."

"Okay! Sure enough!"

Liu Cangyun had been waiting for this!

Today, she would use this information to completely wipe these two families, who dared to provoke her man, from the face of the earth!

Once Liu Ruyan entered work mode, her entire aura instantly changed!

She was no longer the coquettish, clingy woman in front of Xia Feng.

She was now the decisive, ruthless, and strategically astute female CEO!

Precise commands were issued calmly and clearly from her red lips!

"Xiaoya, pass the word: Plan A, begin execution!"

"Have the trading team immediately start shorting all of the Ji family's stocks!"

"Simultaneously, have the public relations department leak all the information I sent you, in batches!"

Xia Feng, on the other hand, was even more direct and brutal!

His fingers tapped on the keyboard.

He directly hacked into the internal networks of the Ji and Li families!

Faced with his [top-tier hacking skills], the so-called firewalls of those two companies were as fragile as paper, utterly vulnerable!

He obtained all the internal fund flows, personnel movements, and trade secrets of those two companies…

Everything was crystal clear!

Then he relayed this most crucial and fatal intelligence to Liu Ruyan and her team in real time.

A silent, yet incredibly cruel "nibbling operation" had officially begun!

Meanwhile.

The Ji family.

In the study.

Ji Er, the head of the Ji family, was anxiously answering the phone.

His expression was like a dye vat, shifting between green and white in an instant!

“Chairman Ji! It’s over! Our stock market… our stock market has been maliciously shorted!”

“What happened?!”

"Yesterday our stock price was soaring, even hitting the daily limit! How come it's suddenly been shorted today?!"

"I don't know, Mr. Ji! But...but the attack is too fierce! Our cash flow simply can't hold!"

The voice on the other end of the phone was filled with despair!

Upon hearing this, Ji Er felt a wave of dizziness wash over him!

He couldn't even hold his phone properly!

"Snap!"

Just then!

"Dad! Something terrible has happened!"

"They...they've completely surrounded our house!"



Chapter 97 Ji Li is finished


This scene was playing out in the Li family compound in Hancheng, a thousand miles away.

The head of the Li family, Li Hao, sat ashen-faced in the main seat of the living room.

Because Li Lei had already been taken away and executed.

His eyes were vacant, and he muttered to himself.

Just then!

"So, tell me, should we go now, or go home and change our clothes first?"

Liu Ruyan jumped off him with joy, bouncing around on the spot!

Xia Feng felt as if he were under the law of universal gravitation, his gaze completely drawn to her two constantly bouncing heads.

"Of course we're going now!"

"If we go back, we'll definitely run into Qingxue and the others!"

Chapter 98 XX Kill, Activated!


With Xia Feng and Liu Ruyan working together, the Ji and Li families, two behemoths, collapsed in less than half a day.

But it didn't matter.

Wherever she wanted to go, he would go with her—it was that simple.

The Maserati sped along, finally stopping near a food street next to Jiangcheng University.

His voice held a hint of nostalgia.

Her eyes were also filled with reminiscence.

With that, he pulled Liu Ruyan along, heading straight for the milk tea shop.

Upon reaching the entrance.

"A taro boba, please."

Then, he turned to look at Liu Ruyan beside him and continued.

"And a jasmine milk green tea."

"The jasmine milk green tea, warm, less sugar."

This jasmine milk green tea was naturally for Liu Ruyan.

He remembered clearly that she liked to drink this before her period.

And it couldn't be iced, and the sugar had to be used sparingly.

The two found a small table by the window and sat down.

Feeling Xia Feng's meticulous thoughtfulness, Liu Ruyan's heart felt as if it were filled with honey, so sweet it was almost melting.

She looked at Xia Feng, a happy smile on her face.

'Hmph, at least you, you blockhead, have a conscience!'

She continued reminiscing about the past.

"Back then, you were always staying in the dorm playing games, like a shut-in, no matter how much I called you, you wouldn't come out."

Her tone carried a hint of complaint.

“If I hadn’t always had Lin Yu come to your dorm and drag you out of your computer, you probably would have stayed home until graduation, right?”

Speaking of this, Xia Feng felt a little embarrassed.

He scratched his head and explained with a dry laugh:

“Well… hahaha, I was addicted to games back then.”

He had indeed been particularly addicted to a competitive game for a while.

Because in the game, he met an incredibly skilled online friend.

Their skills were evenly matched, a true clash of equals.

Before long, they developed a mutual respect, forming a peculiar father-son relationship.

Whoever carried the game had to call the other “Daddy” in the public chat.

To get the other to genuinely accept calling him “Daddy,” Xia Feng practically neglected sleep and meals during that period.

But then…

Then the guy on the other end suddenly revealed he was a girl and insisted that he call her "Mommy."

He even unilaterally announced that he wanted to have an online romance with him.

Xia Feng immediately refused; it was purely for gaming, nothing real, and he absolutely refused to share any photos.

But she wouldn't give up, persisting until she finally declared Xia Feng her boyfriend.

Xia Feng just assumed she was joking.

The two maintained this strange relationship while playing games together.

However, since getting married, he hadn't logged into that account in a long time and didn't know how she was doing.

"Ahem, back then I found a gaming partner, her skill level was about the same as mine, and I was determined to make her call me 'Daddy'!"

He had barely finished speaking.

"Daddy~"

Liu Ruyan suddenly leaned in and whispered in his ear in a sweet, cloying voice.

Xia Feng froze instantly!

He turned his head, looking at the little vixen with a mischievous grin, her eyes gleaming with cunning!

He immediately reached out and pinched her smooth cheek.

“You! You!”

His voice was full of threat.

“You've gotten bold, haven't you? Aren't you afraid I'll just go straight for it?!”

Liu Ruyan wasn't afraid at all; instead, she confidently puffed out her chest.

That breathtaking curve made Xia Feng take a second look.

“So what?”

She met his gaze without flinching.

“I'll be waiting!”

“Then, I'll make sure you flee in utter defeat, begging for mercy on your knees!”

She directly challenged Xia Feng to a duel!

“Alright, alright, my Empress.”

"Let's talk about this after our date."

He decided he'd make sure she knew what he was getting into later—you can eat whatever you want, but you can't say whatever you want.

It's best not to get too carried away!

"Hello, your milk tea."

Xia Feng took the milk tea, inserted the straw, and handed it to Liu Ruyan.

Then, he pulled Liu Ruyan along and continued shopping.

The two chatted and laughed all the way, as if they were back in their carefree college days.
