Xia Feng gently pushed her from behind, and Liu Ruyan sat on the swing, laughing like a child.

Her clear, melodious laughter filled the entire park.

Next, they went to the nearest movie theater and randomly picked a romantic film that was playing.

The plot was a bit melodramatic, making them drowsy.

But neither of them cared.

What they cared about was the warmth of their tightly clasped hands and their close embrace in the darkness.

When the movie ended,

it was completely dark.

Xia Feng drove, not towards home.

But directly to their usual spot, the Rose Hotel.

He parked the car, turned to look at Liu Ruyan beside him, her pretty face slightly flushed, but her eyes filled with fighting spirit.

A predatory smile appeared on his face.

It's time to respond to my Empress's challenge, issued in the bubble tea shop.

God-level massage, god-level medical skills, to lend you a hand!

XX Kill, activate!



Chapter 99 Death Has Come to Collect People


The night was as dark as ink.

In a heavily guarded detention center on the outskirts of Jiangcheng.

In one of the musty-smelling cells, Ji Bo lay sound asleep on the cold cement floor with several fellow inmates.

Unbeknownst to him, death was already creeping in.

A figure appeared without warning in the shadows of the cell.

It was Xia Feng.

His presence here was entirely due to something he had just obtained from the system using all his points.

A set with a straightforward and brutal name.

【Murder and Robbery Set】!

【Includes: Teleportation Talisman x2, Sleep Talisman x1, Insulation Talisman x1, "I Love a Piece of Firewood" x1, Trace Erasure Card x1】

Xia Feng immediately used one of the Teleportation Talismans.

The next second, he appeared in the cell.

He took out a white Sleep Talisman from his system space and used it.

A faint light flickered.

Whether asleep or awake, everyone instantly fell into a deep sleep.

Then, Xia Feng took out a yellow soundproof talisman.

He affixed the talisman to the wall, and an invisible barrier instantly enveloped the entire cell.

From now on, even if there was thunder inside, not a sound could be heard outside.

The talisman would automatically disappear after a set time.

Alright.

The preparations are complete.

Next, it's time for the cleanup.

Xia Feng strode forward, step by step, to the unconscious Ji Bo.

He looked at the face that disgusted him utterly, his eyes cold and devoid of any emotion.

He slowly lifted his foot.

Then, he stomped hard on Ji Bo's exposed right hand!

"Crack!"

A crisp, ear-piercing sound of bone breaking echoed clearly in the silent cell!

"Aaaaaaahh ...

Ji Bo, who had been unconscious, was instantly jolted awake by the excruciating pain!

He let out a bloodcurdling scream, like a pig being slaughtered!

He opened his eyes in a panic, trying to grab Xia Feng's foot that was pressing down on his hand with his other hand.

But the foot didn't budge!

Snot and tears instantly smeared his face!

He looked up, and in the dim moonlight, he could barely make out the man's face before him!

His pupils contracted sharply, his face filled with disbelief and astonishment!

"It's...it's you!"

"Xia Feng!!"

"You...why are you here?!"

"Quick! Let go of my foot!!"

Xia Feng stared at him, his eyes like those of someone looking at a dead man.

He didn't answer any of his questions.

Instead, he ground his foot forcefully into Ji Bo's completely deformed hand.

"Aaaaaaahh ...

Ji Bo let out a scream several times more piercing than before!

The sound was heart-wrenching, filled with boundless pain and despair!

It was just too painful!

This excruciating pain directly exceeded the limits of his nerves' endurance!

His eyes rolled back, and he fainted once more.

Xia Feng looked at this pathetic piece of trash and sneered.

"You fainted over something so simple?"

"I can't let you have it so easy."

With a thought, he retrieved the [Taiyi Divine Needles] set from his system space.

He flicked his finger!

Several silver needles, as thin as cow's hair, whistled through the air and accurately shot into several key acupoints on Ji Bo's body!

This wasn't for healing.

It was a special technique from [Divine-Level Medical Arts]!

It could keep a person absolutely conscious!

Furthermore, it could amplify all the pain they felt several times over!

After doing all this, Xia Feng withdrew his hand with satisfaction.

Ji Bo on the bed quickly woke up.

The instant he awoke!

He felt an excruciating pain several times greater than before, sweeping through his entire body like a tidal wave!

Every cell, every nerve, was frantically sending pain signals to his brain!

Xia Feng released his foot.

Ji Bo immediately clutched his hand, now a mangled mess of flesh, and rolled wildly on the ground, howling in agony!

Xia Feng watched him expressionlessly.

Then, another kick!

A powerful kick to his stomach!

Ji Bo was sent flying into the air by the force of the kick!

Then he crashed heavily to the cold, hard ground!

He was curled up like a boiled shrimp, bile gushing from his mouth!

Xia Feng stepped forward.

Another kick!

This kick was swift and ruthless, striking precisely at his most vulnerable spot!

A soft "thud!"

This was the second eunuch of the new era, one he had personally created.

Xia Feng didn't stop.

Ignoring Ji Bo's hoarse screams,

Step by step, he shattered every bone in his body, one by one!

Finally, he retrieved the prop filled with twisted humor from his system space:

【I Love a Piece of Firewood】.

He used it on Ji Bo, his roommate who was still fast asleep.

Having done all this,

he looked at Ji Bo lying on the ground, his limbs severed, his face unrecognizable, yet still conscious, suffering a fate worse than death.

He spoke slowly.

“This is the consequence of coveting my woman.”

“Remember, be a better person in your next life.”

Then, he retrieved the Taiyi Divine Needles stuck in Ji Bo's body and returned them to his system space for purification.

First, he took out the 【Traces Erasure Card】 and completely erased all traces he had left there, including scents, fingerprints, footprints…

Next, he used his last teleportation talisman.

His figure flashed, and he disappeared from this cell filled with sin.

He returned to Liu Ruyan's hotel room.

Shortly after he left,

the roommate to whom he had used the "I love a piece of firewood" technique also awoke, overwhelmed by an uncontrollable heat coursing through his body.

His eyes were bloodshot, filled with primal desire, like a beast in heat!

His gaze instantly locked onto Ji Bo, who lay on the ground, half-dead but still twitching slightly!

He roared and pounced on him!

Ji Bo's eyes, already hollow from pain, once again revealed boundless terror!

He let out another blood-curdling scream!

But unfortunately, the soundproofing was still working.

This effect would last at least until the next morning.

...

The next day, when the guard on patrol passed by the cell,

he glanced inside casually.

Then, he saw a scene he would never forget, a scene utterly shocking.

A burly man was frantically attacking a mangled, unrecognizable figure!

He was terrified and immediately turned to find help.

When they finally managed to pull the completely crazed man away,

they discovered that Ji Bo on the ground was already dead.

This incident caused quite a stir throughout Jiangcheng.

But all of this was no longer relevant to Xia Feng.

After returning to his hotel, he took a comfortable hot shower.

He washed away all the resentment that had clung to him.

Then, he silently returned to bed and embraced the still-sleeping Liu Ruyan once more.

Liu Ruyan seemed to sense the familiar and comforting warmth of his embrace.

She nuzzled her head against his chest, a sweet smile spreading across her face, and slept even more soundly.

Xia Feng gazed at her peaceful sleeping face, his eyes tender.

'Don't worry.'

'I will make all those who have displeased you pay the price they deserve.'

Xia Feng did not regret what he had done tonight.

If he had regretted it, he wouldn't have infiltrated the Xu family alone to personally create the first eunuch of the new era.

Feeling the softness of Liu Ruyan's delicate body in his arms,

Xia Feng's heart calmed completely.

Soon, he too drifted off to sleep.



Chapter 100 Let's Face the Judgment

Rose Hotel, Presidential Suite.

Moments like this, where she could comfortably snuggle in his arms, would become rare.

A while later.

Xia Feng also woke up.

The moment he opened his eyes, he saw the stunningly beautiful woman smiling radiantly at him.

Today would be another day full of energy!

Liu Ruyan drove Xia Feng to Dream Chasing Company.

As soon as she stepped into the company, she saw everyone already in a state of bustling activity!

Today was the first day of the game's closed beta test!

Everyone was at their workstations, ready and waiting!

Upon seeing Xia Feng, everyone took the time to greet him.

Zhang Qiang, who was responsible for monitoring the server data in real time, saw Xia Feng as if he had seen a savior and immediately sought his help.

“Brother Feng! You’re finally here!”

“Come quickly and help me check if there’s a bug in this data stream!”

Xia Feng quickly went over to check.

He only glanced at the waterfall-like data stream on the screen and instantly found the root cause of the problem.

It turned out that the number of players flooding in at the moment the server opened was simply too large!

This caused some data to conflict and become congested during transmission.

This was indeed something Xia Feng hadn’t considered when initially designing the server framework.

He sat down, his fingers flying across the keyboard!

He worked quickly, in just a few minutes!

He completely solved the problem!

Then, he casually wrote a piece of backup code, like a “fuse.”

This code effectively neutralizes conflicts between players caused by data congestion.

Whenever a similar situation occurs again, it will automatically activate to distribute and optimize the flow.

After Xia Feng finished everything, he stood up and patted Zhang Qiang on the shoulder.

"All done."

"There shouldn't be anything else to do now."

"Everyone, work hard today. After the week-long closed beta ends smoothly, I'll see how things go and treat everyone to a meal!"

Zhang Qiang nodded vigorously immediately, then focused intently on the data on the screen again.

went into the CEO's office.

[Wow! This game is so much fun! The graphics are amazing! The combat is explosive! And there's even a flight system! Cultivators can really fly!]

【Waaaaah, this immortal cultivation is unavoidable! Am I right, downstairs?!】

【The fellow Daoist upstairs is right! There are three realms of immortal cultivation: Ant Realm, Fellow Daoist Realm, and Senior Realm, and I'm in the Non-Beef-Eating Realm!】

【Hehehehe… This setting of killing and looting, free PK, is such a wonderful thing~ I can't wait to become a great demon!】

【Parents ❤Aren't ❤Home ❤Alone ❤Lonely ❤Hot☆Energetic☆Enjoy☆Game☆】

“Looks like the feedback on our game is pretty good.”

After reading these comments full of silly humor, Xia Feng nodded in satisfaction.

“Ah!”

“Ah!”

His sudden remark startled the two girls who were completely engrossed!

Their bodies trembled simultaneously!

Then they abruptly turned around!

When they finally saw the culprit behind them, grinning maliciously, their beautiful eyes instantly ignited with fury!

Then, the two of them grabbed Xia Feng's arms, one on each side!

Without a word, they dragged him into a small cubicle next to them!

Wait…

What are you two doing?!

Let's talk this out!

A gentleman uses words, not fists!
